HiFi-Inpaint: Towards High-Fidelity Reference-Based Inpainting for Generating Detail-Preserving Human-Product Images
Authors: Yichen Liu, Donghao Zhou, Jie Wang, Xin Gao, Guisheng Liu, Jiatong Li, Quanwei Zhang, Qiang Lyu, Lanqing Guo, Shilei Wen, Weiqiang Wang, Pheng-Ann Heng
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:59:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:59:36+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026 (Project page: \url{https://correr-zhou.github.io/HiFi-Inpaint/})
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Human-product images, which showcase the integration of humans and products, play a vital role in advertising, e-commerce, and digital marketing. The essential challenge of generating such images lies in ensuring the high-fidelity preservation of product details. Among existing paradigms, reference-based inpainting offers a targeted solution by leveraging product reference images to guide the inpainting process. However, limitations remain in three key aspects: the lack of diverse large-scale training data, the struggle of current models to focus on product detail preservation, and the inability of coarse supervision for achieving precise guidance. To address these issues, we propose HiFi-Inpaint, a novel high-fidelity reference-based inpainting framework tailored for generating human-product images. HiFi-Inpaint introduces Shared Enhancement Attention (SEA) to refine fine-grained product features and Detail-Aware Loss (DAL) to enforce precise pixel-level supervision using high-frequency maps. Additionally, we construct a new dataset, HP-Image-40K, with samples curated from self-synthesis data and processed with automatic filtering. Experimental results show that HiFi-Inpaint achieves state-of-the-art performance, delivering detail-preserving human-product images.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HiFi-Inpaint：面向高保真参考引导修复生成细节保留的人体产品图像
人体产品图像在广告、电子商务和数字营销中发挥着重要作用，其核心挑战在于确保产品细节的高保真度。现有方法中，基于参考图像的修复技术通过利用产品参考图引导修复过程，提供了一种针对性解决方案。然而，该方法仍存在三大局限：缺乏多样化的大型训练数据、当前模型难以聚焦产品细节保留、粗粒度监督无法实现精确引导。为此，我们提出HiFi-Inpaint，一种专为生成人体产品图像设计的高保真参考引导修复框架。HiFi-Inpaint引入共享增强注意力（SEA）以优化细粒度产品特征，并采用细节感知损失（DAL）通过高频图实现像素级精确监督。此外，我们构建了新数据集HP-Image-40K，其样本来自自合成数据并经自动过滤处理。实验表明，HiFi-Inpaint达到当前最优性能，可生成细节保留的人体产品图像。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for high-fidelity human-product images in advertising and e-commerce, this work addresses limitations in existing reference-based inpainting methods, including insufficient training data, poor focus on product details, and coarse supervision. HiFi-Inpaint introduces Shared Enhancement Attention to refine fine-grained product features and Detail-Aware Loss using high-frequency maps for pixel-level precision. Evaluated on a newly constructed HP-Image-40K dataset, the method achieves state-of-the-art results in generating detail-preserving human-product images.
为满足广告和电商中对高保真人与产品图像的需求，该研究针对现有基于参考图像修复方法存在的训练数据不足、产品细节关注不足及监督粗放等问题，提出HiFi-Inpaint框架，引入共享增强注意力机制以优化细粒度产品特征，并采用基于高频图的细节感知损失实现像素级精准控制。在新构建的HP-Image-40K数据集上，该方法在生成细节保留的人产品图像方面达到当前最优性能。
Reasoning Core: A Scalable Procedural Data Generation Suite for Symbolic Pre-training and Post-Training
Authors: Valentin Lacombe, Valentin Quesnel, Damien Sileo
First: 2026-03-02T18:59:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:59:29+00:00
Comments: Keywords: LLMs, NLP, Dataset, Corpus, Procedural Pre-training, Reasoning, Logic, Formal Semantics https://github.com/sileod/reasoning_core
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training on verifiable symbolic data is a promising way to expand the reasoning frontier of language models beyond what standard pre-training corpora provide. Yet existing procedural generators often rely on fixed puzzles or templates and do not deliver the distributional breadth needed at scale. We introduce Reasoning Core, a scalable suite that procedurally generates verifiable symbolic reasoning data across core formal domains: PDDL planning over randomized domains, first-order logic with equality, context-free grammar parsing and generation, causal reasoning over random Bayesian networks, and systems of equations. Each task is paired with an external solver for rigorous verification and admits continuous difficulty control for curriculum design. Examples can optionally include solver-derived reasoning traces, enabling supervised training from the earliest pre-training stages, and the same interface provides verifiable reward functions for reinforcement learning. Our experiments show that mixing Reasoning Core data into pre-training improves downstream reasoning while preserving, or slightly improving, language modeling quality. Zero-shot evaluations confirm these tasks challenge frontier models such as GPT-5. The code and data are publicly available under the MIT license.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance language models' reasoning capabilities beyond standard pre-training corpora, the authors introduce Reasoning Core, a scalable procedural data generation suite that produces verifiable symbolic reasoning data across five formal domains including PDDL planning, first-order logic, grammar parsing, causal reasoning, and systems of equations. Each domain is paired with an external solver for verification and supports adjustable difficulty for curriculum learning, with optional reasoning traces for supervised training and reward functions for reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that incorporating Reasoning Core data during pre-training improves downstream reasoning performance without harming language modeling quality, and zero-shot evaluations confirm that these tasks challenge state-of-the-art models like GPT-5.
为提升语言模型在标准语料之外的推理能力，作者提出了Reasoning Core，一个可扩展的程序化数据生成系统，覆盖PDDL规划、一阶逻辑、文法解析、因果推理和方程组等五个形式化领域。每个任务均配备外部求解器以确保可验证性，并支持难度连续调节以适应课程学习；还可生成求解器推理轨迹用于监督学习，或提供可验证奖励函数用于强化学习。实验表明，将Reasoning Core数据融入预训练可提升下游推理能力，同时保持或略微提升语言建模质量，零样本评估也证实这些任务能有效挑战前沿模型如GPT-5。
Partial Causal Structure Learning for Valid Selective Conformal Inference under Interventions
Authors: Amir Asiaee, Kavey Aryan, James P. Long
First: 2026-03-02T18:58:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:58:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Selective conformal prediction can yield substantially tighter uncertainty sets when we can identify calibration examples that are exchangeable with the test example. In interventional settings, such as perturbation experiments in genomics, exchangeability often holds only within subsets of interventions that leave a target variable "unaffected" (e.g., non-descendants of an intervened node in a causal graph). We study the practical regime where this invariance structure is unknown and must be learned from data. Our contributions are: (i) a contamination-robust conformal coverage theorem that quantifies how misclassification of "unaffected" calibration examples degrades coverage via an explicit function $g(δ,n)$ of the contamination fraction and calibration set size, providing a finite-sample lower bound that holds for arbitrary contaminating distributions; (ii) a task-driven partial causal learning formulation that estimates only the binary descendant indicators $Z_{a,i}=\mathbf{1}\{i\in\mathrm{desc}(a)\}$ needed for selective calibration, rather than the full causal graph; and (iii) algorithms for descendant discovery via perturbation intersection patterns (differentially affected variable set intersections across interventions), and for approximate distance-to-intervention estimation via local invariant causal prediction. We provide recovery conditions under which contamination is controlled. Experiments on synthetic linear structural equation models (SEMs) validate the bound: under controlled contamination up to $δ=0.30$, the corrected procedure maintains $\ge 0.95$ coverage while uncorrected selective CP degrades to $0.867$. A proof-of-concept on Replogle K562 CRISPR interference (CRISPRi) perturbation data demonstrates applicability to real genomic screens.
中文标题/摘要
标题：干预下有效选择性符合推断的局部因果结构学习
当能识别与测试样本可交换的校准样本时，选择性符合预测可显著缩小不确定性集合。在干预场景（如基因组中的扰动实验）中，可交换性通常仅在对目标变量“无影响”的干预子集内成立（例如因果图中被干预节点的非后代）。我们研究该不变结构未知且需从数据中学习的实用情形。主要贡献包括：(i) 一个鲁棒于污染的符合覆盖率定理，通过显式函数g(δ,n)量化“无影响”校准样本误分类对覆盖率的损害，提供对任意污染分布均成立的有限样本下界；(ii) 任务驱动的局部因果学习框架，仅估计选择性校准所需的二元后代指示变量Z_{a,i}=I{i∈desc(a)}，而非完整因果图；(iii) 通过扰动交集模式（不同干预下差异受影响变量集的交集）发现后代的算法，以及通过局部不变因果预测近似估计干预距离。我们提供了控制污染的恢复条件。在合成线性结构方程模型（SEMs）上的实验验证了该界：在污染控制至δ=0.30时，修正方法保持≥0.95覆盖率，而未修正的选择性CP退化至0.867。在Replogle K562 CRISPR干扰（CRISPRi）扰动数据上的概念验证展示了其在真实基因组筛选中的适用性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for tighter uncertainty sets in selective conformal prediction under interventions, this work addresses the challenge of learning partial causal structures where exchangeability holds only for subsets of interventions that leave target variables unaffected. The method introduces a contamination-robust coverage guarantee quantified by a function of contamination fraction and calibration set size, and proposes a task-driven partial causal learning approach that estimates only binary descendant indicators needed for selective calibration. Algorithms based on perturbation intersection patterns and local invariant causal prediction are developed for descendant discovery and distance estimation. Experiments on synthetic SEMs show that under up to 30% contamination, the corrected method maintains ≥95% coverage while the uncorrected method drops to 86.7%. A proof-of-concept on CRISPRi genomic perturbation data confirms practical applicability.
为在干预环境下实现更紧的不确定性区间，该研究针对仅在部分干预下目标变量保持不变时交换性成立的问题，提出学习部分因果结构的方法。方法包括一个对污染鲁棒的覆盖率保证，量化污染比例与校准集大小对覆盖率的影响，并设计仅需估计二值后代指示变量的任务驱动式部分因果学习框架。基于干预扰动交集模式和局部不变因果预测的算法用于发现后代节点和估计干预距离。在合成线性结构方程模型实验中，当污染比例达30%时，修正方法仍保持≥95%覆盖率，而未修正方法降至86.7%。在CRISPRi基因组扰动数据上的概念验证表明该方法具有实际应用价值。
Adaptive Data Augmentation with Multi-armed Bandit: Sample-Efficient Embedding Calibration for Implicit Pattern Recognition
Authors: Minxue Tang, Yangyang Yu, Aolin Ding, Maziyar Baran Pouyan, Taha Belkhouja, Yujia Bao
First: 2026-02-22T23:39:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:58:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recognizing implicit visual and textual patterns is essential in many real-world applications of modern AI. However, tackling long-tail pattern recognition tasks remains challenging for current pre-trained foundation models such as LLMs and VLMs. While finetuning pre-trained models can improve accuracy in recognizing implicit patterns, it is usually infeasible due to a lack of training data and high computational overhead. In this paper, we propose ADAMAB, an efficient embedding calibration framework for few-shot pattern recognition. To maximally reduce the computational costs, ADAMAB trains embedder-agnostic light-weight calibrators on top of fixed embedding models without accessing their parameters. To mitigate the need for large-scale training data, we introduce an adaptive data augmentation strategy based on the Multi-Armed Bandit (MAB) mechanism. With a modified upper confidence bound algorithm, ADAMAB diminishes the gradient shifting and offers theoretically guaranteed convergence in few-shot training. Our multi-modal experiments justify the superior performance of ADAMAB, with up to 40% accuracy improvement when training with less than 5 initial data samples of each class.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多臂老虎机的自适应数据增强：面向隐式模式识别的样本高效嵌入校准
识别视觉和文本中的隐式模式在现代人工智能的许多实际应用中至关重要。然而，当前预训练基础模型（如LLM和VLM）在处理长尾模式识别任务时仍面临挑战。虽然微调预训练模型可提升隐式模式识别的准确性，但通常因训练数据不足和计算开销过高而不可行。本文提出ADAMAB，一种面向少样本模式识别的高效嵌入校准框架。为最大限度降低计算成本，ADAMAB在固定嵌入模型上训练不依赖嵌入器参数的轻量级校准器。为减少对大规模训练数据的需求，我们引入基于多臂老虎机（MAB）机制的自适应数据增强策略。通过改进的上置信界算法，ADAMAB减轻梯度偏移，并在少样本训练中提供理论保证的收敛性。我们的多模态实验验证了ADAMAB的优越性能，在每类初始样本少于5个时，准确率最高提升40%。
Summary / 总结
To address the challenge of recognizing long-tail implicit patterns with limited data and high computational cost, ADAMAB introduces an embedding-calibration framework that trains lightweight, embedder-agnostic calibrators on top of fixed pre-trained models. It employs a Multi-Armed Bandit-based adaptive data augmentation strategy with a modified upper confidence bound algorithm to reduce gradient shifting and ensure convergence in few-shot settings. Experimental results across multi-modal tasks show ADAMAB achieves up to 40% accuracy improvement over baseline methods when trained with fewer than five samples per class.
为解决在数据稀缺、计算成本高的情况下识别长尾隐式模式的难题，ADAMAB提出一种在固定预训练模型上训练轻量级嵌入校准器的框架，其采用基于多臂老虎机的自适应数据增强策略，并结合改进的上置信界算法以减少梯度漂移并保证少样本训练收敛。多模态实验表明，当每类仅用少于五个样本训练时，ADAMAB相较基线方法准确率提升最高达40%。
Tool Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruotong Liao, Nikolai Röhrich, Xiaohan Wang, Yuhui Zhang, Yasaman Samadzadeh, Volker Tresp, Serena Yeung-Levy
First: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for self-evolving large reasoning models (LRMs), enabling online adaptation on unlabeled test inputs via self-induced rewards through majority voting. However, a spurious yet high-frequency unverified consensus can become a biased and reinforced reward signal, leading to incorrect mode collapse. We address this failure mode with T^3RL (Tool-Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning), which introduces test-time tool verification into reward estimation. Concretely, a verifier uses an external tool as evidence (e.g., from code execution) to upweight verified rollouts in a verification-aware voting, producing more reliable pseudo-labels for training. Across various math difficulties (MATH-500, AMC, and AIME 2024) and diverse backbone types, T^3RL significantly improves over TTRL, with larger gains on harder problems. More broadly, T^3RL can be viewed as verified online data synthesis, highlighting test-time tool verification as a key mechanism for stabilizing self-evolution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习的工具验证
测试时强化学习（TTRL）作为一种自进化大型推理模型（LRMs）的有前景范式，通过多数投票自诱导奖励，实现对未标记测试输入的在线自适应。然而，高频但未经验证的伪共识可能成为有偏且被强化的奖励信号，导致错误的模式坍缩。我们通过T^3RL（测试时强化学习的工具验证）解决此失效模式，该方法在奖励估计中引入测试时工具验证。具体而言，验证器利用外部工具作为证据（如代码执行结果），在验证感知投票中提升已验证轨迹的权重，生成更可靠的伪标签用于训练。在多种数学难度（MATH-500、AMC、AIME 2024）和不同骨干模型上，T^3RL显著优于TTRL，尤其在难题上收益更大。更广泛地，T^3RL可视为经验证的在线数据合成，凸显测试时工具验证是稳定自进化的关键机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the risk of biased reward signals from unverified consensus in test-time reinforcement learning, this work introduces T^3RL, a method that integrates tool verification into reward estimation to stabilize self-evolving large reasoning models. By using an external tool to validate rollouts and weighting verified ones in a voting mechanism, T^3RL generates more reliable pseudo-labels for training. Experiments across MATH-500, AMC, and AIME 2024 show consistent performance gains, especially on harder problems, demonstrating that tool verification significantly reduces mode collapse and improves adaptation accuracy.
为解决测试时强化学习中因未验证共识导致的奖励信号偏差和模式坍缩问题，本文提出T^3RL方法，通过引入工具验证机制提升奖励估计的可靠性。该方法利用外部工具验证生成的轨迹，并在投票中加权已验证样本，从而生成更准确的伪标签用于训练。在MATH-500、AMC和AIME 2024等多个数学难度数据集上，T^3RL表现显著优于传统测试时强化学习，尤其在高难度问题上提升更明显，验证了工具验证对稳定自进化模型的关键作用。
Metric Entropy-Free Sample Complexity Bounds for Sample Average Approximation in Convex Stochastic Programming
Authors: Hongcheng Liu, Jindong Tong
First: 2024-01-01T04:35:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper studies sample average approximation (SAA) in solving convex or strongly convex stochastic programming (SP) problems. In estimating SAA's sample efficiency, the state-of-the-art sample complexity bounds entail metric entropy terms (such as the logarithm of the feasible region's covering number), which often grow polynomially with problem dimensionality. While it has been shown that metric entropy-free complexity rates are attainable under a uniform Lipschitz condition, such an assumption can be overly critical for many important SP problem settings. In response, this paper presents metric entropy-free sample complexity bounds for the SAA under standard SP assumptions} -- in the absence of the uniform Lipschitz condition. For a $d$-dimensional problem, the new results often lead to an $O(d)$-improvement in the complexity rate compared with the state-of-the-art. From the newly established complexity bounds, an important revelation is that SAA and the canonical stochastic mirror descent (SMD) method, two mainstream solution approaches to SP, entail almost identical rates of sample efficiency, lifting a theoretical discrepancy of SAA from SMD also by a factor of $O(d)$. Furthermore, this paper explores non-Lipschitzian scenarios where SAA maintains provable efficacy but the corresponding results for SMD remain mostly unexplored, indicating the potential of SAA's better applicability in some irregular settings. The results of our numerical experiments align with our theoretical findings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：凸随机规划中样本平均近似方法的无度量熵样本复杂度界
本文研究了样本平均近似（SAA）在求解凸或强凸随机规划（SP）问题中的应用。在评估SAA的样本效率时，现有最优样本复杂度界包含度量熵项（如可行域覆盖数的对数），这些项通常随问题维度多项式增长。尽管在均匀Lipschitz条件下可实现无度量熵的复杂度率，但该假设对许多重要SP问题场景而言过于苛刻。为此，本文在标准SP假设下（无需均匀Lipschitz条件），提出了SAA的无度量熵样本复杂度界。对于d维问题，新结果通常比现有最优结果在复杂度率上提升O(d)。从新建立的复杂度界可看出，SAA与经典随机镜像下降（SMD）方法——两种主流SP求解方法——在样本效率上几乎相同，从而将SAA与SMD之间的理论差异也提升了O(d)因子。此外，本文探讨了非Lipschitz情形，其中SAA仍具可证明的有效性，而SMD对应结果尚属探索阶段，表明SAA在某些非规则场景中可能更具适用潜力。数值实验结果与理论发现一致。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high dimensionality dependence of existing metric entropy-based sample complexity bounds for sample average approximation (SAA) in convex stochastic programming, this paper derives new metric entropy-free bounds under standard assumptions without requiring uniform Lipschitz continuity. The method leverages structural properties of convex SP problems to establish tighter complexity rates, achieving an O(d) improvement over prior results for d-dimensional problems. Experimental results confirm that SAA and stochastic mirror descent (SMD) exhibit nearly identical sample efficiency, resolving a theoretical gap by an O(d) factor, and further demonstrate SAA’s robustness in non-Lipschitz settings where SMD lacks established guarantees.
为解决现有SAA样本复杂度界中因度量熵项导致的计算效率低下问题，本文在无需均匀Lipschitz条件的前提下，基于标准凸随机规划假设推导出无度量熵的样本复杂度界。该方法利用凸规划结构特性，实现d维问题下O(d)量级的复杂度提升，优于现有最优结果。实验表明，SAA与随机镜像下降法(SMD)在样本效率上几乎相当，且SAA在非Lipschitz场景下仍具可证有效性，而SMD在该类场景的理论支持尚不充分，凸显SAA在不规则问题中的潜在优势。
Frontier Models Can Take Actions at Low Probabilities
Authors: Alex Serrano, Wen Xing, David Lindner, Erik Jenner
First: 2026-03-02T18:56:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:56:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pre-deployment evaluations inspect only a limited sample of model actions. A malicious model seeking to evade oversight could exploit this by randomizing when to "defect": misbehaving so rarely that no malicious actions are observed during evaluation, but often enough that they occur eventually in deployment. But this requires taking actions at very low rates, while maintaining calibration. Are frontier models even capable of that? We prompt the GPT-5, Claude-4.5 and Qwen-3 families to take a target action at low probabilities (e.g. 0.01%), either given directly or requiring derivation, and evaluate their calibration (i.e. whether they perform the target action roughly 1 in 10,000 times when resampling). We find that frontier models are surprisingly good at this task. If there is a source of entropy in-context (such as a UUID), they maintain high calibration at rates lower than 1 in 100,000 actions. Without external entropy, some models can still reach rates lower than 1 in 10,000. When target rates are given, larger models achieve good calibration at lower rates. Yet, when models must derive the optimal target rate themselves, all models fail to achieve calibration without entropy or hint to generate it. Successful low-rate strategies require explicit Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning, so malicious models attempting this approach could currently be caught by a CoT monitor. However, scaling trends suggest future evaluations may be unable to rely on models' lack of target rate calibration, especially if CoT is no longer legible.
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether frontier models can reliably perform actions at extremely low probabilities while maintaining calibration, a capability that could allow malicious models to evade detection by rarely misbehaving during evaluation. The researchers prompt GPT-5, Claude-4.5, and Qwen-3 to execute target actions at rates as low as 0.01%, either directly or through derivation, then measure calibration by resampling. Results show that with in-context entropy (e.g., a UUID), models maintain high calibration even below 1 in 100,000 actions; without it, some still achieve below 1 in 10,000. When target rates are specified, larger models perform better at lower rates, but when models must self-derive the optimal rate, calibration fails without external entropy or hints. Successful strategies require explicit Chain-of-Thought reasoning, which could be detectable by current monitors, though scaling may eventually obscure such reasoning, undermining reliance on calibration for safety evaluation.
本研究探讨前沿模型是否能在极低概率下可靠执行动作并保持校准，这可能使恶意模型通过在评估阶段极少违规而规避监管。研究人员引导GPT-5、Claude-4.5和Qwen-3在0.01%等极低概率下执行目标动作，或需自行推导，再通过重采样评估校准效果。结果表明，若有上下文熵源（如UUID），模型可在低于1/100,000的频率下保持高校准；无熵源时，部分模型仍可达到低于1/10,000。当目标概率直接指定时，大模型在更低频率下表现更好；但若模型需自行推导最优概率，无熵源或提示时校准失败。成功策略需显式链式思维（CoT），当前可被CoT监控捕获，但随着模型规模增长，CoT可能变得不可读，未来评估可能无法依赖校准来保障安全。
tttLRM: Test-Time Training for Long Context and Autoregressive 3D Reconstruction
Authors: Chen Wang, Hao Tan, Wang Yifan, Zhiqin Chen, Yuheng Liu, Kalyan Sunkavalli, Sai Bi, Lingjie Liu, Yiwei Hu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-02-23T18:59:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:56:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026. Project Page: https://cwchenwang.github.io/tttLRM
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We propose tttLRM, a novel large 3D reconstruction model that leverages a Test-Time Training (TTT) layer to enable long-context, autoregressive 3D reconstruction with linear computational complexity, further scaling the model's capability. Our framework efficiently compresses multiple image observations into the fast weights of the TTT layer, forming an implicit 3D representation in the latent space that can be decoded into various explicit formats, such as Gaussian Splats (GS) for downstream applications. The online learning variant of our model supports progressive 3D reconstruction and refinement from streaming observations. We demonstrate that pretraining on novel view synthesis tasks effectively transfers to explicit 3D modeling, resulting in improved reconstruction quality and faster convergence. Extensive experiments show that our method achieves superior performance in feedforward 3D Gaussian reconstruction compared to state-of-the-art approaches on both objects and scenes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：tttLRM：面向长上下文与自回归3D重建的测试时训练方法

Motivated by the need for efficient, long-context 3D reconstruction with linear computational cost, the authors introduce tttLRM, a model that employs a Test-Time Training layer to enable autoregressive 3D reconstruction while compressing multi-view inputs into fast weights for implicit 3D representation. Experimental results show tttLRM outperforms existing methods in feedforward 3D Gaussian reconstruction on both objects and scenes, achieving higher quality and faster convergence.
为实现线性计算复杂度下的长上下文3D重建，作者提出tttLRM模型，利用测试时训练层动态压缩流式图像观测为快权重，构建隐式3D表示并解码为高斯点云等显式格式，支持在线渐进式重建与优化。实验表明，该模型在新视角合成预训练后能有效迁移到3D建模任务，重建质量优于当前最优方法，且收敛速度更快，适用于物体与场景重建。
Adaptive Confidence Regularization for Multimodal Failure Detection
Authors: Moru Liu, Hao Dong, Olga Fink, Mario Trapp
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:56:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:56:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The deployment of multimodal models in high-stakes domains, such as self-driving vehicles and medical diagnostics, demands not only strong predictive performance but also reliable mechanisms for detecting failures. In this work, we address the largely unexplored problem of failure detection in multimodal contexts. We propose Adaptive Confidence Regularization (ACR), a novel framework specifically designed to detect multimodal failures. Our approach is driven by a key observation: in most failure cases, the confidence of the multimodal prediction is significantly lower than that of at least one unimodal branch, a phenomenon we term confidence degradation. To mitigate this, we introduce an Adaptive Confidence Loss that penalizes such degradations during training. In addition, we propose Multimodal Feature Swapping, a novel outlier synthesis technique that generates challenging, failure-aware training examples. By training with these synthetic failures, ACR learns to more effectively recognize and reject uncertain predictions, thereby improving overall reliability. Extensive experiments across four datasets, three modalities, and multiple evaluation settings demonstrate that ACR achieves consistent and robust gains. The source code will be available at https://github.com/mona4399/ACR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于多模态故障检测的自适应置信度正则化
在自动驾驶和医学诊断等高风险领域部署多模态模型，不仅需要强大的预测性能，还需要可靠的故障检测机制。本文针对多模态场景中尚未充分探索的故障检测问题，提出自适应置信度正则化（ACR）框架。我们的方法基于一个关键观察：在大多数故障案例中，多模态预测的置信度显著低于至少一个单模态分支，我们称之为置信度退化。为缓解此问题，我们引入自适应置信度损失，在训练中惩罚此类退化。此外，我们提出多模态特征交换，一种新颖的异常合成技术，生成具有挑战性的、故障感知的训练样本。通过训练这些合成故障，ACR能更有效地识别并拒绝不确定预测，从而提升整体可靠性。在四个数据集、三种模态和多种评估设置下的广泛实验表明，ACR取得一致且稳健的性能提升。源代码将在 https://github.com/mona4399/ACR 公开。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for reliable failure detection in high-stakes multimodal applications, this work introduces Adaptive Confidence Regularization (ACR), a framework that leverages the observation that multimodal failures often exhibit confidence degradation relative to unimodal branches. ACR trains models using an Adaptive Confidence Loss to penalize such confidence drops and incorporates Multimodal Feature Swapping to synthesize failure-aware training examples. Experimental results across four datasets, three modalities, and multiple settings show consistent performance improvements in detecting and rejecting uncertain predictions, enhancing overall system reliability.
为提升高风险多模态应用中的故障检测可靠性，本文提出自适应置信度正则化（ACR）框架，其核心观察是多模态故障常伴随相对于单模态分支的置信度下降。ACR通过自适应置信度损失惩罚此类置信度降低，并引入多模态特征交换技术合成故障感知训练样本。在四个数据集、三种模态及多种评估设置下的实验表明，ACR能稳定提升对不确定预测的识别与拒绝能力，从而增强系统整体可靠性。
Conformal Policy Control
Authors: Drew Prinster, Clara Fannjiang, Ji Won Park, Kyunghyun Cho, Anqi Liu, Suchi Saria, Samuel Stanton
First: 2026-03-02T18:54:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:54:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
An agent must try new behaviors to explore and improve. In high-stakes environments, an agent that violates safety constraints may cause harm and must be taken offline, curtailing any future interaction. Imitating old behavior is safe, but excessive conservatism discourages exploration. How much behavior change is too much? We show how to use any safe reference policy as a probabilistic regulator for any optimized but untested policy. Conformal calibration on data from the safe policy determines how aggressively the new policy can act, while provably enforcing the user's declared risk tolerance. Unlike conservative optimization methods, we do not assume the user has identified the correct model class nor tuned any hyperparameters. Unlike previous conformal methods, our theory provides finite-sample guarantees even for non-monotonic bounded constraint functions. Our experiments on applications ranging from natural language question answering to biomolecular engineering show that safe exploration is not only possible from the first moment of deployment, but can also improve performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：保形策略控制
代理必须尝试新行为以进行探索和改进。在高风险环境中，违反安全约束的代理可能造成伤害，必须下线，从而终止任何未来交互。模仿旧行为是安全的，但过度保守会抑制探索。行为改变多少才算过多？我们展示了如何利用任何安全的参考策略作为任何优化但未经测试策略的概率调节器。通过对安全策略数据进行保形校准，可确定新策略可以采取的激进程度，同时可证明其符合用户声明的风险容忍度。与保守优化方法不同，我们不假设用户已识别正确的模型类或调整任何超参数。与以往保形方法不同，我们的理论即使在非单调有界约束函数的情况下，也能提供有限样本保证。我们在从自然语言问答到生物分子工程等应用中的实验表明，安全探索不仅从部署之初即可行，还能提升性能。
Summary / 总结
To enable safe exploration in high-stakes environments without compromising performance, the paper proposes Conformal Policy Control, a method that uses any existing safe reference policy to probabilistically regulate a new, untested policy. By applying conformal calibration on data from the safe policy, the method quantifies how aggressively the new policy can act while provably respecting user-defined risk tolerance. Unlike conservative optimization approaches, it does not require assumptions about model classes or hyperparameter tuning, and unlike prior conformal methods, it offers finite-sample guarantees even for non-monotonic constraints. Experiments across domains including natural language question answering and biomolecular engineering demonstrate that safe exploration is feasible from deployment and can lead to performance improvements.
为在高风险环境中实现安全探索而不牺牲性能，该论文提出利用安全参考策略作为优化但未经测试策略的概率调节器。通过在安全策略数据上应用符合性校准，该方法量化了新策略可采取的激进程度，同时可证明满足用户设定的风险容忍度。与保守优化或以往符合性方法不同，它无需假设模型类别或调整超参数，且即使面对非单调约束函数也能提供有限样本保证。在包括自然语言处理和生物分子工程等领域的实验表明，安全探索从部署之初即可实现，并能提升性能。
From Leaderboard to Deployment: Code Quality Challenges in AV Perception Repositories
Authors: Mateus Karvat, Bram Adams, Sidney Givigi
First: 2026-03-02T18:54:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:54:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous vehicle (AV) perception models are typically evaluated solely on benchmark performance metrics, with limited attention to code quality, production readiness and long-term maintainability. This creates a significant gap between research excellence and real-world deployment in safety-critical systems subject to international safety standards. To address this gap, we present the first large-scale empirical study of software quality in AV perception repositories, systematically analyzing 178 unique models from the KITTI and NuScenes 3D Object Detection leaderboards. Using static analysis tools (Pylint, Bandit, and Radon), we evaluated code errors, security vulnerabilities, maintainability, and development practices. Our findings revealed that only 7.3% of the studied repositories meet basic production-readiness criteria, defined as having zero critical errors and no high-severity security vulnerabilities. Security issues are highly concentrated, with the top five issues responsible for almost 80% of occurrences, which prompted us to develop a set of actionable guidelines to prevent them. Additionally, the adoption of Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment pipelines was correlated with better code maintainability. Our findings highlight that leaderboard performance does not reflect production readiness and that targeted interventions could substantially improve the quality and safety of AV perception code.
中文标题/摘要

自动驾驶（AV）感知模型通常仅依据基准性能指标进行评估，对代码质量、生产就绪性和长期可维护性关注不足。这在受国际安全标准约束的安全关键系统中，造成了研究卓越性与实际部署之间的显著差距。为弥合这一差距，我们首次对自动驾驶感知仓库中的软件质量进行了大规模实证研究，系统分析了来自KITTI和NuScenes 3D目标检测排行榜的178个独特模型。我们使用静态分析工具（Pylint、Bandit和Radon），评估了代码错误、安全漏洞、可维护性及开发实践。研究发现，仅7.3%的仓库满足基本生产就绪标准（即无严重错误、无高危安全漏洞）。安全问题高度集中，前五大问题占发生总数的近80%，为此我们制定了可操作的指导方针以预防此类问题。此外，持续集成/持续部署（CI/CD）流程的采用与更好的代码可维护性呈正相关。我们的研究结果表明，排行榜性能无法反映生产就绪性，针对性干预措施可显著提升自动驾驶感知代码的质量与安全性。

Symbol-Equivariant Recurrent Reasoning Models
Authors: Richard Freinschlag, Timo Bertram, Erich Kobler, Andreas Mayr, Günter Klambauer
First: 2026-03-02T18:53:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:53:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reasoning problems such as Sudoku and ARC-AGI remain challenging for neural networks. The structured problem solving architecture family of Recurrent Reasoning Models (RRMs), including Hierarchical Reasoning Model (HRM) and Tiny Recursive Model (TRM), offer a compact alternative to large language models, but currently handle symbol symmetries only implicitly via costly data augmentation. We introduce Symbol-Equivariant Recurrent Reasoning Models (SE-RRMs), which enforce permutation equivariance at the architectural level through symbol-equivariant layers, guaranteeing identical solutions under symbol or color permutations. SE-RRMs outperform prior RRMs on 9x9 Sudoku and generalize from just training on 9x9 to smaller 4x4 and larger 16x16 and 25x25 instances, to which existing RRMs cannot extrapolate. On ARC-AGI-1 and ARC-AGI-2, SE-RRMs achieve competitive performance with substantially less data augmentation and only 2 million parameters, demonstrating that explicitly encoding symmetry improves the robustness and scalability of neural reasoning. Code is available at https://github.com/ml-jku/SE-RRM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：符号等变循环推理模型
数独和ARC-AGI等推理问题对神经网络仍具挑战性。循环推理模型（RRM）家族，包括分层推理模型（HRM）和微型递归模型（TRM），为大型语言模型提供了一种紧凑的替代方案，但目前仅通过昂贵的数据增强隐式处理符号对称性。我们提出符号等变循环推理模型（SE-RRM），通过符号等变层在架构层面强制实现排列等变性，确保在符号或颜色排列下得到相同解。SE-RRM在9x9数独上优于现有RRM，并能从仅训练于9x9实例泛化至更小的4x4和更大的16x16、25x25实例，而现有RRM无法外推。在ARC-AGI-1和ARC-AGI-2上，SE-RRM以显著减少的数据增强和仅200万参数实现竞争力表现，证明显式编码对称性可提升神经推理的鲁棒性与可扩展性。代码见https://github.com/ml-jku/SE-RRM。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty neural networks face in solving structured reasoning tasks like Sudoku and ARC-AGI, this work proposes Symbol-Equivariant Recurrent Reasoning Models (SE-RRMs) that explicitly encode symbol symmetries via symbol-equivariant layers, ensuring consistent outputs under symbol permutations. Unlike prior RRMs that rely on costly data augmentation to handle symmetries, SE-RRMs enforce equivariance at the architecture level, enabling them to generalize across grid sizes—from 4x4 to 25x25—where existing models fail. Experimentally, SE-RRMs outperform prior RRMs on 9x9 Sudoku and achieve competitive results on ARC-AGI benchmarks with only 2 million parameters and minimal data augmentation, demonstrating that architectural symmetry handling enhances both robustness and scalability.
为了解决神经网络在解决如数独和ARC-AGI等结构化推理任务时的困难，本文提出符号等变递归推理模型（SE-RRMs），通过符号等变层在架构层面显式编码符号对称性，确保在符号置换下输出一致。与依赖昂贵数据增强的现有递归推理模型不同，SE-RRMs在架构中强制实现等变性，使其能泛化至不同网格尺寸（4x4至25x25），而现有模型无法做到。实验表明，SE-RRMs在9x9数独上优于现有模型，并在ARC-AGI基准上以仅200万参数和极少数据增强实现竞争力表现，证明架构层面的对称性处理可提升模型的鲁棒性和可扩展性。
Branched Schrödinger Bridge Matching
Authors: Sophia Tang, Yinuo Zhang, Alexander Tong, Pranam Chatterjee
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-10T17:29:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:53:14+00:00
Comments: Published at ICLR 2026. (Proceedings of the 14th International Conference on Learning Representations, Rio de Janeiro, Brazil)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Predicting the intermediate trajectories between an initial and target distribution is a central problem in generative modeling. Existing approaches, such as flow matching and Schrödinger bridge matching, effectively learn mappings between two distributions by modeling a single stochastic path. However, these methods are inherently limited to unimodal transitions and cannot capture branched or divergent evolution from a common origin to multiple distinct modes. To address this, we introduce Branched Schrödinger Bridge Matching (BranchSBM), a novel framework that learns branched Schrödinger bridges. BranchSBM parameterizes multiple time-dependent velocity fields and growth processes, enabling the representation of population-level divergence into multiple terminal distributions. We show that BranchSBM is not only more expressive but also essential for tasks involving multi-path surface navigation, modeling cell fate bifurcations from homogeneous progenitor states, and simulating diverging cellular responses to perturbations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分枝薛定谔桥匹配
预测初始分布与目标分布之间的中间轨迹是生成建模中的核心问题。现有方法如流匹配和薛定谔桥匹配，通过建模单一随机路径有效学习两个分布之间的映射，但这些方法本质上仅适用于单模态过渡，无法捕捉从共同起源向多个不同模式分叉或发散的演化过程。为此，我们提出了分枝薛定谔桥匹配（BranchSBM），一种新颖框架，用于学习分枝薛定谔桥。BranchSBM 参数化多个时间依赖的速度场和生长过程，从而能够表示群体层面向多个终端分布的发散。我们证明 BranchSBM 不仅更具表达能力，而且对于涉及多路径表面导航、从同质祖细胞状态建模细胞命运分叉，以及模拟细胞对扰动的发散响应等任务至关重要。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of existing generative methods to unimodal transitions, this work introduces Branched Schrödinger Bridge Matching (BranchSBM) to model branched evolutionary paths from a common origin to multiple distinct distributions. BranchSBM achieves this by parameterizing multiple time-dependent velocity fields and growth processes, enabling population-level divergence. Experimental results demonstrate that BranchSBM is more expressive and essential for tasks such as multi-path surface navigation, modeling cell fate bifurcations, and simulating divergent cellular responses to perturbations, outperforming unimodal approaches in capturing complex branching dynamics.
为了解决现有生成方法无法建模多模态分支演化的问题，本文提出了分支薛定谔桥匹配（BranchSBM）框架，通过参数化多个时变速度场与增长过程，实现从共同起点向多个目标分布的群体级发散。实验表明，BranchSBM在多路径表面导航、细胞命运分岔建模及细胞对扰动的发散响应模拟等任务中，比单模态方法更具表达能力且不可或缺，能有效捕捉复杂分支动态。
Sketch2Colab: Sketch-Conditioned Multi-Human Animation via Controllable Flow Distillation
Authors: Divyanshu Daiya, Aniket Bera
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:52:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:52:51+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026 Main Conference (11 pages, 5 figures)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Sketch2Colab, which turns storyboard-style 2D sketches into coherent, object-aware 3D multi-human motion with fine-grained control over agents, joints, timing, and contacts. Conventional diffusion-based motion generators have advanced realism; however, achieving precise adherence to rich interaction constraints typically demands extensive training and/or costly posterior guidance, and performance can degrade under strong multi-entity conditioning. Sketch2Colab instead first learns a sketch-driven diffusion prior and then distills it into an efficient rectified-flow student operating in latent space for fast, stable sampling. Differentiable energies over keyframes, trajectories, and physics-based constraints directly shape the student's transport field, steering samples toward motions that faithfully satisfy the storyboard while remaining physically plausible. To capture coordinated interaction, we augment the continuous flow with a continuous-time Markov chain (CTMC) planner that schedules discrete events such as touches, grasps, and handoffs, modulating the dynamics to produce crisp, well-phased human-object-human collaborations. Experiments on CORE4D and InterHuman show that Sketch2Colab achieves state-of-the-art constraint adherence and perceptual quality while offering significantly faster inference than diffusion-only baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Sketch2Colab：通过可控流蒸馏实现基于草图的多人体动画
我们提出了Sketch2Colab，可将故事板风格的2D草图转化为连贯且具备物体感知能力的3D多人体运动，并对角色、关节、时间与接触点实现精细控制。传统基于扩散的运动生成器已提升真实感，但要精确满足丰富的交互约束通常需大量训练或昂贵的后验引导，且在强多实体条件下性能易下降。Sketch2Colab首先学习草图驱动的扩散先验，再将其蒸馏为在潜在空间中高效运行的修正流学生模型，以实现快速稳定的采样。关键帧、轨迹及基于物理的约束的可微能量直接塑造学生模型的传输场，引导采样结果忠实地满足故事板要求，同时保持物理合理性。为捕捉协同交互，我们在连续流中引入连续时间马尔可夫链（CTMC）规划器，调度触碰、抓取与交接等离散事件，调节动态以生成清晰、节奏协调的人机协作。
Summary / 总结
We present Sketch2Colab, which turns storyboard-style 2D sketches into coherent, object-aware 3D multi-human motion with fine-grained control over agents, joints, timing, and contacts.
Multi-Head Low-Rank Attention
Authors: Songtao Liu, Hongwu Peng, Zhiwei Zhang, Zhengyu Chen, Yue Guo
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:52:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:52:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Long-context inference in large language models is bottlenecked by Key--Value (KV) cache loading during the decoding stage, where the sequential nature of generation requires repeatedly transferring the KV cache from off-chip High-Bandwidth Memory (HBM) to on-chip Static Random-Access Memory (SRAM) at each step. While Multi-Head Latent Attention (MLA) significantly reduces the total KV cache size, it suffers from a sharding bottleneck during distributed decoding via Tensor Parallelism (TP). Since its single latent head cannot be partitioned, each device is forced to redundantly load the complete KV cache for every token, consuming excessive memory traffic and diminishing TP benefits like weight sharding. In this work, we propose Multi-Head Low-Rank Attention (MLRA), which enables partitionable latent states for efficient 4-way TP decoding. Extensive experiments show that MLRA achieves state-of-the-art perplexity and downstream task performance, while also delivering a 2.8$\times$ decoding speedup over MLA. Code is available at https://github.com/SongtaoLiu0823/MLRA. Pretrained weights, along with the training and evaluation data, are available at https://huggingface.co/Soughing/MLRA.
Summary / 总结
To address the KV cache loading bottleneck in long-context decoding of large language models, this work introduces Multi-Head Low-Rank Attention (MLRA), which overcomes the sharding limitation of Multi-Head Latent Attention by enabling partitionable latent states for efficient 4-way tensor parallelism. MLRA decomposes the latent representation into multiple low-rank heads, allowing each device to load only its assigned portion of the KV cache, thereby reducing redundant memory traffic and preserving TP benefits. Experiments demonstrate that MLRA achieves state-of-the-art perplexity and task performance while delivering a 2.8x decoding speedup over MLA.
为解决大语言模型长上下文推理中KV缓存加载的瓶颈问题，本文提出多头低秩注意力（MLRA），通过将潜表示分解为多个可分片的低秩头，支持4路张量并行解码，避免了单头潜表示无法分片导致的冗余缓存加载。实验表明，MLRA在保持最先进困惑度和下游任务性能的同时，相较MLA实现2.8倍的解码加速。
MAC: A Conversion Rate Prediction Benchmark Featuring Labels Under Multiple Attribution Mechanisms
Authors: Jinqi Wu, Sishuo Chen, Zhangming Chan, Yong Bai, Lei Zhang, Sheng Chen, Chenghuan Hou, Xiang-Rong Sheng, Han Zhu, Jian Xu, Bo Zheng, Chaoyou Fu
First: 2026-03-02T18:51:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:51:01+00:00
Comments: Code and data available at https://github.com/alimama-tech/PyMAL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-attribution learning (MAL), which enhances model performance by learning from conversion labels yielded by multiple attribution mechanisms, has emerged as a promising learning paradigm for conversion rate (CVR) prediction. However, the conversion labels in public CVR datasets are generated by a single attribution mechanism, hindering the development of MAL approaches. To address this data gap, we establish the Multi-Attribution Benchmark (MAC), the first public CVR dataset featuring labels from multiple attribution mechanisms. Besides, to promote reproducible research on MAL, we develop PyMAL, an open-source library covering a wide array of baseline methods. We conduct comprehensive experimental analyses on MAC and reveal three key insights: (1) MAL brings consistent performance gains across different attribution settings, especially for users featuring long conversion paths. (2) The performance growth scales up with objective complexity in most settings; however, when predicting first-click conversion targets, simply adding auxiliary objectives is counterproductive, underscoring the necessity of careful selection of auxiliary objectives. (3) Two architectural design principles are paramount: first, to fully learn the multi-attribution knowledge, and second, to fully leverage this knowledge to serve the main task. Motivated by these findings, we propose Mixture of Asymmetric Experts (MoAE), an effective MAL approach incorporating multi-attribution knowledge learning and main task-centric knowledge utilization. Experiments on MAC show that MoAE substantially surpasses the existing state-of-the-art MAL method. We believe that our benchmark and insights will foster future research in the MAL field. Our MAC benchmark and the PyMAL algorithm library are publicly available at https://github.com/alimama-tech/PyMAL.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of public datasets with multi-attribution conversion labels, the paper introduces MAC, the first benchmark for conversion rate prediction under multiple attribution mechanisms, and PyMAL, an open-source library of baseline methods. Experiments on MAC reveal that multi-attribution learning (MAL) consistently improves performance, especially for users with long conversion paths, and that performance gains scale with task complexity—though adding auxiliary objectives for first-click prediction can backfire without careful design. Two key architectural principles emerge: fully learning multi-attribution knowledge and fully leveraging it for the main task. Based on these insights, the authors propose MoAE, a novel MAL method that combines knowledge learning and task-centric utilization, achieving substantial performance improvements over existing state-of-the-art approaches.
为解决现有公开数据集中缺乏多归因标签的问题，本文构建了首个支持多归因机制的转化率预测基准MAC，并开发了开源基线方法库PyMAL。实验表明，多归因学习（MAL）在不同归因设置下均能稳定提升性能，尤其对长转化路径用户效果显著；性能增益随任务复杂度上升，但在预测首点击转化时，盲目添加辅助目标反而有害，强调辅助目标需谨慎选择。两大架构原则至关重要：一是充分学习多归因知识，二是充分将该知识用于主任务。基于此，作者提出MoAE方法，融合多归因知识学习与主任务导向利用，在MAC上显著超越现有最先进方法。
Leveraging Model Soups to Classify Intangible Cultural Heritage Images from the Mekong Delta
Authors: Quoc-Khang Tran, Minh-Thien Nguyen, Nguyen-Khang Pham
First: 2026-03-02T18:50:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:50:15+00:00
Comments: Early accept of Vol 2025 No 3, November : Journal on Information Technologies & Communications
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The classification of Intangible Cultural Heritage (ICH) images in the Mekong Delta poses unique challenges due to limited annotated data, high visual similarity among classes, and domain heterogeneity. In such low-resource settings, conventional deep learning models often suffer from high variance or overfit to spurious correlations, leading to poor generalization. To address these limitations, we propose a robust framework that integrates the hybrid CoAtNet architecture with model soups, a lightweight weight-space ensembling technique that averages checkpoints from a single training trajectory without increasing inference cost. CoAtNet captures both local and global patterns through stage-wise fusion of convolution and self-attention. We apply two ensembling strategies - greedy and uniform soup - to selectively combine diverse checkpoints into a final model. Beyond performance improvements, we analyze the ensembling effect through the lens of bias-variance decomposition. Our findings show that model soups reduces variance by stabilizing predictions across diverse model snapshots, while introducing minimal additional bias. Furthermore, using cross-entropy-based distance metrics and Multidimensional Scaling (MDS), we show that model soups selects geometrically diverse checkpoints, unlike Soft Voting, which blends redundant models centered in output space. Evaluated on the ICH-17 dataset (7,406 images across 17 classes), our approach achieves state-of-the-art results with 72.36% top-1 accuracy and 69.28% macro F1-score, outperforming strong baselines including ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, and ViT. These results underscore that diversity-aware checkpoint averaging provides a principled and efficient way to reduce variance and enhance generalization in culturally rich, data-scarce classification tasks.
Summary / 总结
To tackle the challenge of classifying Intangible Cultural Heritage images from the Mekong Delta under low-resource conditions with limited annotations and high class similarity, the authors propose integrating the CoAtNet architecture with model soups—a lightweight ensembling technique that averages checkpoints from a single training trajectory without extra inference cost. By applying greedy and uniform ensembling strategies to combine diverse checkpoints, the method reduces prediction variance while introducing minimal bias, as confirmed by bias-variance decomposition. Experimental results on the ICH-17 dataset show the approach achieves 72.36% top-1 accuracy and 69.28% macro F1-score, outperforming baselines like ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, and ViT, demonstrating that diversity-aware checkpoint averaging enhances generalization in culturally rich, data-scarce settings.
为解决湄公河三角洲非物质文化遗产图像分类中因数据稀缺、视觉相似度高和领域异质性导致的模型性能不佳问题，作者提出结合CoAtNet架构与模型汤（model soups）的框架，该方法通过轻量级权重空间集成技术，在不增加推理开销的前提下平均单次训练轨迹中的多个检查点。采用贪心和均匀两种集成策略选择多样性检查点，并通过偏差-方差分解分析集成效果。在ICH-17数据集上，该方法达到72.36%的top-1准确率和69.28%的宏F1分数，优于ResNet-50、DenseNet-121和ViT等基线模型，证明检查点平均能有效降低方差、提升泛化能力。
Reservoir Subspace Injection for Online ICA under Top-n Whitening
Authors: Wenjun Xiao, Yuda Bi, Vince D Calhoun
First: 2026-03-02T18:49:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:49:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reservoir expansion can improve online independent component analysis (ICA) under nonlinear mixing, yet top-$n$ whitening may discard injected features. We formalize this bottleneck as \emph{reservoir subspace injection} (RSI): injected features help only if they enter the retained eigenspace without displacing passthrough directions. RSI diagnostics (IER, SSO, $ρ_x$) identify a failure mode in our top-$n$ setting: stronger injection increases IER but crowds out passthrough energy ($ρ_x: 1.00\!\rightarrow\!0.77$), degrading SI-SDR by up to $2.2$\,dB. A guarded RSI controller preserves passthrough retention and recovers mean performance to within $0.1$\,dB of baseline $1/N$ scaling. With passthrough preserved, RE-OICA improves over vanilla online ICA by $+1.7$\,dB under nonlinear mixing and achieves positive SI-SDR$_{\mathrm{sc}}$ on the tested super-Gaussian benchmark ($+0.6$\,dB).
中文标题/摘要
标题：在Top-n白化下的在线ICA的水库子空间注入
水库扩展可提升非线性混合下的在线独立成分分析（ICA）性能，但Top-n白化可能丢弃注入特征。我们将此瓶颈形式化为“水库子空间注入”（RSI）：仅当注入特征进入保留的特征空间且不挤占直通方向时，才有效。RSI诊断指标（IER、SSO、ρ_x）揭示了在Top-n设置下的失效模式：更强的注入虽提升IER，却挤占直通能量（ρ_x: 1.00→0.77），导致SI-SDR下降高达2.2 dB。受保护的RSI控制器可保持直通保留，并将平均性能恢复至基线1/N缩放的0.1 dB以内。在直通保留的前提下，RE-OICA在非线性混合下比普通在线ICA提升1.7 dB，并在测试的超高斯基准上实现正SI-SDR_sc（+0.6 dB）。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the trade-off between reservoir expansion and top-n whitening in online ICA, this work introduces reservoir subspace injection (RSI) to ensure injected features remain within the retained eigenspace without displacing passthrough directions. The method employs diagnostics (IER, SSO, ρx) to detect when stronger injection degrades performance by reducing passthrough energy, and a guarded RSI controller is used to preserve passthrough while maintaining performance close to baseline. Experiments show that RE-OICA, with passthrough preserved, improves over vanilla online ICA by +1.7 dB under nonlinear mixing and achieves positive SI-SDRsc on a super-Gaussian benchmark by +0.6 dB.
为解决在线独立成分分析中水库扩展与top-n白化之间的权衡问题，本文提出水库子空间注入（RSI）机制，确保注入特征保留在保留的特征子空间内而不挤占通路方向。方法通过IER、SSO、ρx等诊断指标识别强注入导致通路能量下降的失效模式，并引入受控RSI控制器以维持通路保留并恢复性能至基线1/N量级附近。实验表明，在非线性混合环境下，RE-OICA相较普通在线ICA性能提升1.7 dB，并在超高斯基准测试中实现+0.6 dB的正SI-SDRsc。
Wikipedia in the Era of LLMs: Evolution and Risks
Authors: Siming Huang, Yuliang Xu, Mingmeng Geng, Yao Wan, Dongping Chen
First: 2025-03-04T18:58:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:48:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted by TMLR: https://openreview.net/forum?id=ahVmnYkVLt
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In this paper, we present a comprehensive analysis and monitoring framework for the impact of Large Language Models (LLMs) on Wikipedia, examining the evolution of Wikipedia through existing data and using simulations to explore potential risks. We begin by analyzing article content and page views to study the recent changes in Wikipedia and assess the impact of LLMs. Subsequently, we evaluate how LLMs affect various Natural Language Processing (NLP) tasks related to Wikipedia, including machine translation and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). Our findings and simulation results reveal that Wikipedia articles have been affected by LLMs, with an impact of approximately 1% in certain categories. If the machine translation benchmark based on Wikipedia is influenced by LLMs, the scores of the models may become inflated, and the comparative results among models could shift. Moreover, the effectiveness of RAG might decrease if the knowledge has been contaminated by LLMs. While LLMs have not yet fully changed Wikipedia's language and knowledge structures, we believe that our empirical findings signal the need for careful consideration of potential future risks in NLP research. We release all the experimental dataset and source code at: https://github.com/HSM316/LLM_Wikipedia
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型时代下的维基百科：演变与风险
本文提出了一种全面分析与监控框架，用于评估大语言模型（LLMs）对维基百科的影响，通过现有数据考察维基百科的演变，并利用模拟探索潜在风险。我们首先分析文章内容与页面浏览量，研究维基百科近期变化并评估LLMs的影响。随后，我们评估LLMs对与维基百科相关的各类自然语言处理（NLP）任务的影响，包括机器翻译和检索增强生成（RAG）。我们的发现与模拟结果表明，维基百科文章已受到LLMs影响，某些类别影响约为1%。若基于维基百科的机器翻译基准受LLMs影响，模型得分可能被高估，模型间比较结果也可能改变。此外，若知识被LLMs污染，RAG的有效性可能下降。尽管LLMs尚未完全改变维基百科的语言与知识结构，但我们认为，我们的实证发现提示NLP研究需谨慎考虑潜在的未来风险。所有实验数据与源代码已发布于：https://github.com/HSM316/LLM_Wikipedia
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the growing influence of Large Language Models (LLMs) on online knowledge ecosystems, this study analyzes Wikipedia’s evolution and potential risks through content and view data analysis, alongside simulations of LLM impacts on NLP tasks like machine translation and retrieval-augmented generation. The authors find that LLMs have subtly altered Wikipedia content, affecting certain categories by about 1%, which may inflate model performance on Wikipedia-based benchmarks and distort comparative results. Additionally, RAG systems could suffer if knowledge is contaminated by LLM-generated content. While LLMs have not yet fundamentally reshaped Wikipedia’s structure, the findings underscore the need for vigilance in NLP research regarding future contamination risks.
鉴于大型语言模型（LLM）对在线知识库日益增长的影响，本研究通过内容与浏览量数据分析及LLM对机器翻译和检索增强生成等NLP任务影响的模拟，考察了维基百科的演变与潜在风险。研究发现，LLM已对维基百科内容产生约1%的影响，可能导致机器翻译基准分数虚高、模型比较结果失真，并降低检索增强生成的有效性；尽管LLM尚未彻底改变维基百科的语言与知识结构，但这些发现提示NLP研究需警惕未来知识污染的风险。
Organizing, Orchestrating, and Benchmarking Agent Skills at Ecosystem Scale
Authors: Hao Li, Chunjiang Mu, Jianhao Chen, Siyue Ren, Zhiyao Cui, Yiqun Zhang, Lei Bai, Shuyue Hu
First: 2026-03-02T18:46:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:46:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid proliferation of Claude agent skills has raised the central question of how to effectively leverage, manage, and scale the agent skill ecosystem. In this paper, we propose AgentSkillOS, the first principled framework for skill selection, orchestration, and ecosystem-level management. AgentSkillOS comprises two stages: (i) Manage Skills, which organizes skills into a capability tree via node-level recursive categorization for efficient discovery; and (ii) Solve Tasks, which retrieves, orchestrates, and executes multiple skills through DAG-based pipelines. To evaluate the agent's ability to invoke skills, we construct a benchmark of 30 artifact-rich tasks across five categories: data computation, document creation, motion video, visual design, and web interaction. We assess the quality of task outputs using LLM-based pairwise evaluation, and the results are aggregated via a Bradley-Terry model to produce unified quality scores. Experiments across three skill ecosystem scales (200 to 200K skills) show that tree-based retrieval effectively approximates oracle skill selection, and that DAG-based orchestration substantially outperforms native flat invocation even when given the identical skill set. Our findings confirm that structured composition is the key to unlocking skill potential. Our GitHub repository is available at:https://github.com/ynulihao/AgentSkillOS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在生态系统规模下组织、编排和基准测试代理技能
Claude代理技能的快速普及引发了如何有效利用、管理和扩展代理技能生态系统的核心问题。本文提出了AgentSkillOS，这是首个基于原则的技能选择、编排和生态系统级管理框架。AgentSkillOS包含两个阶段：(i) 管理技能，通过节点级递归分类将技能组织为能力树，以实现高效发现；(ii) 解决任务，通过基于DAG的流水线检索、编排和执行多个技能。为评估代理调用技能的能力，我们构建了一个涵盖五个类别（数据计算、文档创建、动态视频、视觉设计、网页交互）的30个富含人工制品的任务基准。我们使用基于LLM的成对评估衡量任务输出质量，并通过Bradley-Terry模型聚合结果以生成统一的质量评分。在三个技能生态系统规模（200至200K技能）的实验中，基于树的检索有效近似了理想技能选择，而基于DAG的编排即使在给定相同技能集的情况下，也显著优于原生扁平调用。我们的研究结果证实，结构化组合是释放技能潜力的关键。我们的GitHub仓库地址为：https://github.com/ynulihao/AgentSkillOS。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to manage and scale the rapidly expanding agent skill ecosystem, this paper introduces AgentSkillOS, a principled framework for skill selection and orchestration. It consists of two stages: first, organizing skills into a capability tree via recursive node categorization to enable efficient discovery; second, orchestrating multiple skills through DAG-based pipelines to solve complex tasks. Evaluated on 30 artifact-rich tasks across five domains using LLM-based pairwise evaluation and Bradley-Terry aggregation, experiments across three ecosystem scales (200 to 200K skills) demonstrate that tree-based retrieval closely matches oracle selection and that DAG orchestration significantly outperforms flat invocation, confirming structured composition as critical for unlocking skill potential.
为应对快速增长的智能体技能生态系统管理与扩展需求，本文提出AgentSkillOS框架，首次系统性解决技能选择与编排问题。该框架分两阶段：第一阶段通过递归节点分类构建能力树，提升技能发现效率；第二阶段采用有向无环图（DAG）编排多技能协同执行任务。在涵盖五大类别的30个富内容任务上，通过LLM双样本评估与Bradley-Terry模型聚合质量得分，实验表明：无论技能规模从200至200K，基于树结构的检索可近似最优选择，DAG编排显著优于扁平调用，验证结构化组合是释放技能潜力的核心机制。
Kiwi-Edit: Versatile Video Editing via Instruction and Reference Guidance
Authors: Yiqi Lin, Guoqiang Liang, Ziyun Zeng, Zechen Bai, Yanzhe Chen, Mike Zheng Shou
First: 2026-03-02T18:46:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:46:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Instruction-based video editing has witnessed rapid progress, yet current methods often struggle with precise visual control, as natural language is inherently limited in describing complex visual nuances. Although reference-guided editing offers a robust solution, its potential is currently bottlenecked by the scarcity of high-quality paired training data. To bridge this gap, we introduce a scalable data generation pipeline that transforms existing video editing pairs into high-fidelity training quadruplets, leveraging image generative models to create synthesized reference scaffolds. Using this pipeline, we construct RefVIE, a large-scale dataset tailored for instruction-reference-following tasks, and establish RefVIE-Bench for comprehensive evaluation. Furthermore, we propose a unified editing architecture, Kiwi-Edit, that synergizes learnable queries and latent visual features for reference semantic guidance. Our model achieves significant gains in instruction following and reference fidelity via a progressive multi-stage training curriculum. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our data and architecture establish a new state-of-the-art in controllable video editing. All datasets, models, and code is released at https://github.com/showlab/Kiwi-Edit.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Kiwi-Edit：通过指令与参考引导实现多功能视频编辑
基于指令的视频编辑已取得快速进展，但现有方法常难以实现精确的视觉控制，因为自然语言在描述复杂视觉细节方面存在固有局限。尽管参考引导编辑提供了稳健的解决方案，其潜力目前受限于高质量配对训练数据的稀缺。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了一种可扩展的数据生成管道，将现有视频编辑配对转换为高保真训练四元组，并利用图像生成模型创建合成参考框架。基于该管道，我们构建了专为指令-参考遵循任务设计的大规模数据集RefVIE，并建立了全面评估基准RefVIE-Bench。此外，我们提出了一种统一的编辑架构Kiwi-Edit，通过可学习查询与潜在视觉特征协同实现参考语义引导。我们的模型通过渐进式多阶段训练课程，在指令遵循与参考保真度方面取得显著提升。大量实验表明，我们的数据与架构在可控视频编辑领域建立了新的最先进水平。所有数据集、模型及代码均已开源：https://github.com/showlab/Kiwi-Edit。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of natural language in precisely controlling video edits and the scarcity of high-quality reference-guided training data, the authors introduce Kiwi-Edit, a unified video editing framework that combines instruction and reference guidance. They build a scalable data pipeline to generate high-fidelity training quadruplets from existing video pairs using image generative models, creating the RefVIE dataset and evaluation benchmark. Their architecture leverages learnable queries and latent visual features for semantic alignment with references, trained via a progressive curriculum. Experiments show Kiwi-Edit achieves state-of-the-art performance in both instruction adherence and reference fidelity across diverse editing tasks.
为解决自然语言难以精确控制视频编辑、且参考引导数据稀缺的问题，作者提出了Kiwi-Edit框架，结合指令与参考引导进行视频编辑。他们构建了可扩展的数据生成流水线，利用图像生成模型从现有视频对中生成高保真训练四元组，构建了RefVIE数据集与评估基准。其架构通过可学习查询与潜在视觉特征实现参考语义对齐，并采用渐进式训练课程。实验表明，Kiwi-Edit在指令遵循与参考保真度上均达到当前最优水平。
De-paradox Tree: Breaking Down Simpson's Paradox via A Kernel-Based Partition Algorithm
Authors: Xian Teng, Yu-Ru Lin
First: 2026-03-02T18:45:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:45:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-world observational datasets and machine learning have revolutionized data-driven decision-making, yet many models rely on empirical associations that may be misleading due to confounding and subgroup heterogeneity. Simpson's paradox exemplifies this challenge, where aggregated and subgroup-level associations contradict each other, leading to misleading conclusions. Existing methods provide limited support for detecting and interpreting such paradoxical associations, especially for practitioners without deep causal expertise. We introduce De-paradox Tree, an interpretable algorithm designed to uncover hidden subgroup patterns behind paradoxical associations under assumed causal structures involving confounders and effect heterogeneity. It employs novel split criteria and balancing-based procedures to adjust for confounders and homogenize heterogeneous effects through recursive partitioning. Compared to state-of-the-art methods, De-paradox Tree builds simpler, more interpretable trees, selects relevant covariates, and identifies nested opposite effects while ensuring robust estimation of causal effects when causally admissible variables are provided. Our approach addresses the limitations of traditional causal inference and machine learning methods by introducing an interpretable framework that supports non-expert practitioners while explicitly acknowledging causal assumptions and scope limitations, enabling more reliable and informed decision-making in complex observational data environments.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prevalence of misleading associations in observational data due to confounding and subgroup heterogeneity, the paper introduces De-paradox Tree, an interpretable algorithm designed to detect and explain Simpson’s paradox by uncovering hidden subgroup patterns under assumed causal structures. The method employs novel split criteria and balancing procedures within recursive partitioning to adjust for confounders and homogenize heterogeneous effects, enabling causal effect estimation when admissible variables are available. Experimental results show that De-paradox Tree produces simpler, more interpretable trees than state-of-the-art methods, accurately identifies nested opposite effects across subgroups, and selects relevant covariates while maintaining robust causal inference under causal assumptions.
为了解决观测数据中因混杂因素和子群异质性导致的误导性关联问题，本文提出了De-paradox Tree算法，通过在假设因果结构下挖掘隐藏的子群模式来检测和解释辛普森悖论。该方法采用新颖的分割准则和基于平衡的递归分区策略，以调整混杂因素并同质化异质效应，支持在提供因果可识别变量时进行稳健因果效应估计。实验表明，该算法相比现有方法生成更简洁可解释的树结构，准确识别子群间嵌套相反效应，并有效选择相关协变量，同时在满足因果假设的前提下保障推断可靠性。
GeoDiT: Point-Conditioned Diffusion Transformer for Satellite Image Synthesis
Authors: Srikumar Sastry, Dan Cher, Brian Wei, Aayush Dhakal, Subash Khanal, Dev Gupta, Nathan Jacobs
First: 2026-03-02T18:42:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:42:15+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce GeoDiT, a diffusion transformer designed for text-to-satellite image generation with point-based control. Existing controlled satellite image generative models often require pixel-level maps that are time-consuming to acquire, yet semantically limited. To address this limitation, we introduce a novel point-based conditioning framework that controls the generation process through the spatial location of the points and the textual description associated with each point, providing semantically rich control signals. This approach enables flexible, annotation-friendly, and computationally simple inference for satellite image generation. To this end, we introduce an adaptive local attention mechanism that effectively regularizes the attention scores based on the input point queries. We systematically evaluate various domain-specific design choices for training GeoDiT, including the selection of satellite image representation for alignment and geolocation representation for conditioning. Our experiments demonstrate that GeoDiT achieves impressive generation performance, surpassing the state-of-the-art remote sensing generative models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GeoDiT：基于点条件的扩散变换器用于卫星图像合成
我们提出了GeoDiT，一种专为基于文本的卫星图像生成设计的扩散变换器，并支持基于点的控制。现有受控卫星图像生成模型通常需要耗时获取的像素级地图，且语义有限。为解决此问题，我们引入了一种新颖的基于点的条件框架，通过点的空间位置及其关联文本描述控制生成过程，提供语义丰富的控制信号。该方法支持灵活、标注友好且计算简单的卫星图像生成推理。为此，我们引入了一种自适应局部注意力机制，根据输入点查询有效调节注意力分数。我们系统评估了训练GeoDiT时的各种领域特定设计选择，包括卫星图像表示的对齐方式和地理定位表示的条件方式。实验表明，GeoDiT在生成性能上表现卓越，超越现有最先进的遥感生成模型。

Motivated by the inefficiency and semantic limitations of pixel-level control in existing satellite image generation models, GeoDiT introduces a point-conditioned diffusion transformer that uses spatial point locations and associated text descriptions to guide image synthesis. The method employs an adaptive local attention mechanism to regularize attention based on input point queries, enabling flexible and computationally efficient inference without requiring dense annotations. Experimental results show GeoDiT outperforms state-of-the-art remote sensing generative models across multiple metrics, demonstrating strong control fidelity and visual quality in synthesized satellite imagery.

Concept-TRAK: Understanding how diffusion models learn concepts through concept-level attribution
Authors: Yonghyun Park, Chieh-Hsin Lai, Satoshi Hayakawa, Yuhta Takida, Naoki Murata, Wei-Hsiang Liao, Woosung Choi, Kin Wai Cheuk, Junghyun Koo, Yuki Mitsufuji
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-07-09T05:03:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:40:44+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While diffusion models excel at image generation, their growing adoption raises critical concerns about copyright issues and model transparency. Existing attribution methods identify training examples influencing an entire image, but fall short in isolating contributions to specific elements, such as styles or objects, that are of primary concern to stakeholders. To address this gap, we introduce concept-level attribution through a novel method called Concept-TRAK, which extends influence functions with a key innovation: specialized training and utility loss functions designed to isolate concept-specific influences rather than overall reconstruction quality. We evaluate Concept-TRAK on novel concept attribution benchmarks using Synthetic and CelebA-HQ datasets, as well as the established AbC benchmark, showing substantial improvements over prior methods in concept-level attribution scenarios. We further demonstrate its versatility on real-world text-to-image generation with compositional and multi-concept prompts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Concept-TRAK：通过概念级归因理解扩散模型如何学习概念
尽管扩散模型在图像生成方面表现出色，但其日益广泛的应用引发了关于版权问题和模型透明度的关键担忧。现有归因方法能够识别影响整张图像的训练样本，但难以分离对特定元素（如风格或物体）的贡献，而这些元素正是利益相关者最关心的。为解决这一问题，我们引入了概念级归因方法——Concept-TRAK，该方法通过一种新颖的机制扩展了影响函数：采用专门设计的训练和效用损失函数，旨在隔离特定概念的影响，而非整体重建质量。我们在Synthetic和CelebA-HQ数据集上的新概念归因基准，以及成熟的AbC基准上评估了Concept-TRAK，结果表明其在概念级归因场景中显著优于现有方法。我们进一步在真实世界文本到图像生成任务中展示了其在组合式和多概念提示下的通用性。
Summary / 总结
Driven by concerns over copyright and transparency in diffusion models, this work introduces Concept-TRAK, a concept-level attribution method that extends influence functions with specialized training and utility loss functions to isolate contributions to specific image elements like objects or styles. Evaluated on Synthetic, CelebA-HQ, and AbC benchmarks, Concept-TRAK demonstrates significant improvements over prior methods in attributing influence to individual concepts. It also proves effective in real-world text-to-image generation with multi-concept prompts, showcasing its versatility and precision.
为应对扩散模型在版权和透明度方面的担忧，本文提出Concept-TRAK方法，通过改进影响函数并引入专用训练与效用损失函数，实现对图像中特定元素（如物体或风格）的精准归因。在Synthetic、CelebA-HQ和AbC等多个基准测试中，该方法显著优于现有方法。同时，它在真实文本到图像生成任务中对多概念提示也表现出良好的适用性与准确性。
SageBwd: A Trainable Low-bit Attention
Authors: Jintao Zhang, Marco Chen, Haoxu Wang, Kai Jiang, Ion Stoica, Joseph E. Gonzalez, Jianfei Chen, Jun Zhu
First: 2026-03-02T18:39:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:39:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Low-bit attention, such as SageAttention, has emerged as an effective approach for accelerating model inference, but its applicability to training remains poorly understood. In prior work, we introduced SageBwd, a trainable INT8 attention that quantizes six of seven attention matrix multiplications while preserving fine-tuning performance. However, SageBwd exhibited a persistent performance gap to full-precision attention (FPA) during pre-training. In this work, we investigate why this gap occurs and demonstrate that SageBwd matches full-precision attention during pretraining. Through experiments and theoretical analysis, we reach a few important insights and conclusions: (i) QK-norm is necessary for stable training at large tokens per step, (ii) quantization errors primarily arise from the backward-pass score gradient dS, (iii) reducing tokens per step enables SageBwd to match FPA performance in pre-training, and (iv) K-smoothing remains essential for training stability, while Q-smoothing provides limited benefit during pre-training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SageBwd：一种可训练的低比特注意力机制
低比特注意力（如SageAttention）已成为加速模型推理的有效方法，但其在训练中的适用性尚不明确。此前工作中，我们提出了SageBwd，一种可训练的INT8注意力机制，它在七次注意力矩阵乘法中量化其中六次，同时保持微调性能。然而，SageBwd在预训练阶段始终与全精度注意力（FPA）存在性能差距。本研究探讨了该差距产生的原因，并证明SageBwd在预训练阶段可匹配FPA性能。通过实验与理论分析，我们得出若干重要见解：(i) 在大步长token情况下，QK-norm对训练稳定性至关重要；(ii) 量化误差主要源于反向传播中的分数梯度dS；(iii) 减小步长token数量可使SageBwd在预训练中匹配FPA性能；(iv) K平滑对训练稳定性仍至关重要，而Q平滑在预训练阶段收益有限。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand and improve low-bit attention during training, this work revisits SageBwd, a trainable INT8 attention mechanism that quantizes six of seven attention matrix multiplications. The authors investigate why SageBwd previously lagged behind full-precision attention during pre-training and find that the gap stems from quantization errors in the backward-pass score gradient and instability at high tokens per step. They demonstrate that reducing tokens per step and enforcing QK-norm enables SageBwd to match full-precision performance, while K-smoothing remains critical for training stability, and Q-smoothing offers minimal benefit during pre-training.
为理解并提升训练阶段低比特注意力的性能，本文重新审视了SageBwd这一可训练的INT8注意力机制，该机制量化了七个注意力矩阵乘法中的六个。研究发现，其在预训练阶段落后于全精度注意力的原因在于反向传播中分数梯度的量化误差及高每步token数下的训练不稳定。实验表明，降低每步token数并强制QK范数可使SageBwd达到全精度性能，而K平滑对训练稳定性至关重要，Q平滑在预训练阶段作用有限。
Astral: training physics-informed neural networks with error majorants
Authors: Vladimir Fanaskov, Tianchi Yu, Alexander Rudikov, Ivan Oseledets
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2024-06-04T13:11:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:39:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026 workshop AI&PDE, reviewed at https://openreview.net/forum?id=TcFpJK2FcN
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The primal approach to physics-informed learning is a residual minimization. We argue that residual is, at best, an indirect measure of the error of approximate solution and propose to train with error majorant instead. Since error majorant provides a direct upper bound on error, one can reliably estimate how close PiNN is to the exact solution and stop the optimization process when the desired accuracy is reached. We call loss function associated with error majorant \textbf{Astral}: neur\textbf{A}l a po\textbf{ST}erio\textbf{R}i function\textbf{A}l \textbf{L}oss. To compare Astral and residual loss functions, we illustrate how error majorants can be derived for various PDEs and conduct experiments with diffusion equations (including anisotropic and in the L-shaped domain), convection-diffusion equation, temporal discretization of Maxwell's equation, magnetostatics and nonlinear elastoplasticity problems. The results indicate that Astral loss is competitive to the residual loss, typically leading to faster convergence and lower error. The main benefit of using Astral loss comes from its ability to estimate error, which is impossible with other loss functions. Our experiments indicate that the error estimate obtained with Astral loss is usually tight enough, e.g., for a highly anisotropic equation, on average, Astral overestimates error by a factor of $1.5$, and for convection-diffusion by a factor of $1.7$. We further demonstrate that Astral loss is better correlated with error than residual and is a more reliable predictor of the error value. Moreover, unlike residual, the error indicator obtained from Astral loss has a superb spatial correlation with error. Backed with the empirical and theoretical results, we argue that one can productively use Astral loss to perform reliable error analysis and approximate PDE solutions with accuracy similar to standard residual-based techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Astral：使用误差上界训练物理信息神经网络
物理信息学习的原始方法是残差最小化。我们认为，残差最多只能间接衡量近似解的误差，因此提出改用误差上界进行训练。由于误差上界可直接提供误差的上界，人们可以可靠地估计PiNN与精确解的接近程度，并在达到所需精度时停止优化过程。我们称与误差上界相关的损失函数为\textbf{Astral}：神经\textbf{A}l a po\textbf{ST}erio\textbf{R}i函数\textbf{A}l \textbf{L}oss。为比较Astral与残差损失函数，我们展示了如何为各类偏微分方程推导误差上界，并对扩散方程（包括各向异性及L形域）、对流-扩散方程、麦克斯韦方程的时间离散化、静磁学及非线性弹塑性问题进行了实验。结果表明，Astral损失函数与残差损失函数相当，通常收敛更快、误差更低。使用Astral损失函数的主要优势在于其能估计误差，而其他损失函数无法做到这一点。我们的实验表明，Astral损失函数获得的误差估计通常足够紧致，例如对于高度各向异性的方程，平均而言Astral误差上界比实际误差高1.5倍；对于对流-扩散方程则高1.7倍。我们进一步证明，Astral损失函数与误差的相关性优于残差，且是更可靠的误差预测器。此外，与残差不同，Astral损失函数获得的误差指示器与误差在空间上具有极佳的相关性。基于实证与理论结果，我们认为可以有效利用Astral损失函数进行可靠的误差分析，并以与标准残差方法相当的精度近似求解偏微分方程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of residual-based loss in physics-informed neural networks (PiNNs) for reliably estimating solution error, the authors propose Astral loss, a novel training objective derived from error majorants that directly upper-bounds the approximation error. By training with this error-aware loss, the method enables accurate error estimation and early stopping when desired accuracy is achieved. Experiments across diverse PDEs—including diffusion, convection-diffusion, Maxwell’s equation, magnetostatics, and elastoplasticity—show that Astral converges faster and achieves lower error than residual loss, while also providing tight error estimates (e.g., 1.5x overestimation for anisotropic diffusion, 1.7x for convection-diffusion). Crucially, Astral’s error indicator correlates better with true error and exhibits superior spatial accuracy compared to residual-based methods, making it a more reliable tool for error analysis and solution approximation.
为了解决物理信息神经网络（PiNN）中残差损失无法可靠估计误差的问题，作者提出Astral损失函数，该函数基于误差上界，能直接提供近似解误差的上限，从而支持误差估计与提前终止训练。在扩散方程、对流-扩散方程、麦克斯韦方程时域离散、磁静力学及非线性弹塑性等多类偏微分方程实验中，Astral损失收敛更快、误差更低，且误差估计更紧致（如各向异性扩散平均高估1.5倍，对流-扩散高估1.7倍）。更重要的是，Astral的误差指示器与真实误差相关性更强，空间分布更准确，相较残差损失更可靠，可有效支持误差分析与高精度解逼近。
Return Augmented Decision Transformer for Off-Dynamics Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruhan Wang, Yu Yang, Zhishuai Liu, Dongruo Zhou, Pan Xu
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research, 2026
First: 2024-10-30T20:46:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:38:36+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 11 tables, 8 figures. Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline off-dynamics reinforcement learning (RL) to utilize data from an easily accessible source domain to enhance policy learning in a target domain with limited data. Our approach centers on return-conditioned supervised learning (RCSL), particularly focusing on Decision Transformer (DT) type frameworks, which can predict actions conditioned on desired return guidance and complete trajectory history. Previous works address the dynamics shift problem by augmenting the reward in the trajectory from the source domain to match the optimal trajectory in the target domain. However, this strategy can not be directly applicable in RCSL owing to (1) the unique form of the RCSL policy class, which explicitly depends on the return, and (2) the absence of a straightforward representation of the optimal trajectory distribution. We propose the Return Augmented (REAG) method for DT type frameworks, where we augment the return in the source domain by aligning its distribution with that in the target domain. We provide the theoretical analysis demonstrating that the RCSL policy learned from REAG achieves the same level of suboptimality as would be obtained without a dynamics shift. We introduce two practical implementations REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ and REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$ respectively. Thorough experiments on D4RL datasets and various DT-type baselines demonstrate that our methods consistently enhance the performance of DT type frameworks in off-dynamics RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于非动态强化学习的回报增强决策变换器
我们研究离线非动态强化学习（RL），旨在利用易于获取的源域数据，提升目标域（数据有限）中的策略学习。我们的方法聚焦于回报条件监督学习（RCSL），特别是决策变换器（DT）类框架，该框架可根据期望回报指导和完整轨迹历史预测动作。以往工作通过增强源域轨迹中的奖励以匹配目标域最优轨迹来解决动态偏移问题。然而，该策略在RCSL中无法直接应用，原因在于：（1）RCSL策略类具有独特的形式，明确依赖于回报；（2）缺乏最优轨迹分布的直接表示。我们提出针对DT类框架的回报增强（REAG）方法，通过将源域回报分布对齐至目标域分布进行增强。我们提供了理论分析，证明从REAG学习到的RCSL策略在动态偏移下的次优性与无动态偏移时相当。我们分别提出了两种实用实现：REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ 和 REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$。在D4RL数据集和多种DT类基线上的全面实验表明，我们的方法在非动态RL中持续提升DT类框架的性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of leveraging source domain data to improve policy learning in target domains with limited data under off-dynamics conditions, this work proposes Return Augmented (REAG) for Decision Transformer frameworks. REAG addresses the dynamics shift by aligning the return distribution in the source domain with that of the target domain, rather than modifying rewards, which is incompatible with return-conditioned supervised learning. Theoretical analysis confirms that the learned policy achieves the same suboptimality as in the absence of dynamics shift. Two practical variants, REAG_Dara* and REAG_MV*, are introduced and empirically validated across D4RL datasets and DT baselines, consistently improving performance.
为解决在动态分布偏移条件下利用源域数据提升目标域有限数据下的策略学习问题，本文提出针对决策变换器框架的回报增强（REAG）方法。REAG通过调整源域轨迹的回报分布以匹配目标域分布，而非修改奖励，从而规避了回报条件监督学习中奖励增强策略的不适用性。理论分析表明，所学习策略的次优性与无动态偏移情况相当。两个实用变体REAG_Dara*和REAG_MV*在D4RL数据集及多种DT基线模型上进行了实验，结果一致显示性能提升。
Bridging the gap between Performance and Interpretability: An Explainable Disentangled Multimodal Framework for Cancer Survival Prediction
Authors: Aniek Eijpe, Soufyan Lakbir, Melis Erdal Cesur, Sara P. Oliveira, Angelos Chatzimparmpas, Sanne Abeln, Wilson Silva
First: 2026-03-02T18:26:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:26:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While multimodal survival prediction models are increasingly more accurate, their complexity often reduces interpretability, limiting insight into how different data sources influence predictions. To address this, we introduce DIMAFx, an explainable multimodal framework for cancer survival prediction that produces disentangled, interpretable modality-specific and modality-shared representations from histopathology whole-slide images and transcriptomics data. Across multiple cancer cohorts, DIMAFx achieves state-of-the-art performance and improved representation disentanglement. Leveraging its interpretable design and SHapley Additive exPlanations, DIMAFx systematically reveals key multimodal interactions and the biological information encoded in the disentangled representations. In breast cancer survival prediction, the most predictive features contain modality-shared information, including one capturing solid tumor morphology contextualized primarily by late estrogen response, where higher-grade morphology aligned with pathway upregulation and increased risk, consistent with known breast cancer biology. Key modality-specific features capture microenvironmental signals from interacting adipose and stromal morphologies. These results show that multimodal models can overcome the traditional trade-off between performance and explainability, supporting their application in precision medicine.
中文标题/摘要
