Instrumental and Proximal Causal Inference with Gaussian Processes
Authors: Yuqi Zhang, Krikamol Muandet, Dino Sejdinovic, Edwin Fong, Siu Lun Chau
First: 2026-03-02T18:23:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:23:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Instrumental variable (IV) and proximal causal learning (Proxy) methods are central frameworks for causal inference in the presence of unobserved confounding. Despite substantial methodological advances, existing approaches rarely provide reliable epistemic uncertainty (EU) quantification. We address this gap through a Deconditional Gaussian Process (DGP) framework for uncertainty-aware causal learning. Our formulation recovers popular kernel estimators as the posterior mean, ensuring predictive precision, while the posterior variance yields principled and well-calibrated EU. Moreover, the probabilistic structure enables systematic model selection via marginal log-likelihood optimization. Empirical results demonstrate strong predictive performance alongside informative EU quantification, evaluated via empirical coverage frequencies and decision-aware accuracy rejection curves. Together, our approach provides a unified, practical solution for causal inference under unobserved confounding with reliable uncertainty.

标题：使用高斯过程的工具变量与近端因果推断
工具变量（IV）和近端因果学习（Proxy）方法是存在未观测混杂因素时因果推断的核心框架。尽管方法论已有显著进展，现有方法很少提供可靠的元认知不确定性（EU）量化。我们通过一种去条件高斯过程（DGP）框架解决这一问题，用于不确定性感知的因果学习。我们的方法将流行核估计量作为后验均值，确保预测精度，而后验方差则提供原则性且校准良好的EU。此外，概率结构支持通过边缘对数似然优化进行系统性模型选择。实证结果表明，该方法在预测性能和信息丰富的EU量化方面表现优异，通过经验覆盖率频率和决策感知准确率拒绝曲线进行评估。总体而言，我们的方法为在未观测混杂因素下因果推断提供了一个统一、实用且可靠的不确定性解决方案。

The DGP model recovers standard kernel estimators as its posterior mean for accurate predictions while using posterior variance to provide principled epistemic uncertainty estimates. 为了解决因果推断中未观测混杂因素下不确定性量化不足的问题，本文提出了一种去条件高斯过程（DGP）框架，统一了工具变量和近端因果学习方法。该框架通过后验均值恢复标准核估计器以保证预测精度，同时利用后验方差提供可靠的不确定性估计。实验结果表明，该方法在预测性能和不确定性校准方面表现优异，通过经验覆盖率和决策感知准确率拒绝曲线验证，为未观测混杂因素下的因果推断提供了一种实用统一的解决方案。
Mixing Times and Privacy Analysis for the Projected Langevin Algorithm under a Modulus of Continuity
Authors: Mario Bravo, Juan P. Flores-Mella, Cristóbal Guzmán
First: 2025-01-07T20:46:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:22:17+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the mixing time of the projected Langevin algorithm (LA) and the privacy curve of noisy Stochastic Gradient Descent (SGD), beyond nonexpansive iterations. Specifically, we derive new mixing time bounds for the projected LA which are, in some important cases, dimension-free and poly-logarithmic on the accuracy, closely matching the existing results in the smooth convex case. Additionally, we establish new upper bounds for the privacy curve of the subsampled noisy SGD algorithm. These bounds show a crucial dependency on the regularity of gradients, and are useful for a wide range of convex losses beyond the smooth case. Our analysis relies on a suitable extension of the Privacy Amplification by Iteration (PABI) framework (Feldman et al., 2018; Altschuler and Talwar, 2022, 2023) to noisy iterations whose gradient map is not necessarily nonexpansive. This extension is achieved by designing an optimization problem which accounts for the best possible Rényi divergence bound obtained by an application of PABI, where the tractability of the problem is crucially related to the modulus of continuity of the associated gradient mapping. We show that, in several interesting cases -- namely the nonsmooth convex, weakly smooth and (strongly) dissipative -- such optimization problem can be solved exactly and explicitly, yielding the tightest possible PABI-based bounds.
中文标题/摘要
标题：投影朗之万算法在连续模下的混合时间与隐私分析
我们研究了投影朗之万算法（LA）的混合时间以及带噪声的随机梯度下降（SGD）的隐私曲线，超越非扩张迭代的情形。具体而言，我们推导了投影LA的新混合时间界，在某些重要情况下，这些界与维度无关，且在精度上为对数多项式，接近现有光滑凸情形下的结果。此外，我们建立了子采样带噪声SGD算法隐私曲线的新上界。这些界显示出对梯度正则性的关键依赖，并适用于光滑情形之外的广泛凸损失函数。我们的分析依赖于对隐私放大迭代（PABI）框架（Feldman等，2018；Altschuler与Talwar，2022, 2023）的适当扩展，以适应梯度映射未必非扩张的带噪声迭代。该扩展通过设计一个优化问题实现，该问题考虑了PABI应用所能获得的最佳Rényi发散界，其中问题的可解性与相关梯度映射的连续模密切相关。我们证明，在若干有趣的情形——即非光滑凸、弱光滑及（强）耗散情形——中，该优化问题可精确显式求解，从而得到最紧的PABI基础界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand convergence and privacy guarantees for projected Langevin algorithms and noisy SGD beyond nonexpansive settings, this work derives dimension-free, poly-logarithmic mixing time bounds for projected Langevin algorithms in important cases, matching known smooth convex results. It also establishes new upper bounds for the privacy curve of subsampled noisy SGD, revealing critical dependence on gradient regularity for convex losses beyond smoothness. The analysis extends the Privacy Amplification by Iteration (PABI) framework to non-nonexpansive gradient mappings by formulating an optimization problem whose solution depends on the modulus of continuity of the gradient map; this problem is solved exactly in key cases—nonsmooth convex, weakly smooth, and dissipative—yielding tight PABI-based bounds.
为理解投影朗之万算法和带噪声的随机梯度下降在非非扩张迭代情形下的收敛性与隐私保证，本文推导了若干重要情形下投影朗之万算法的无维、对精度呈对数多项式增长的混合时间界，与光滑凸情形下已知结果相匹配；同时建立了子采样带噪声SGD的隐私曲线新上界，揭示其对梯度正则性的关键依赖，适用于非光滑凸损失函数。分析扩展了隐私放大迭代（PABI）框架，通过构造一个依赖梯度映射连续模的优化问题，该问题在若干重要情形（非光滑凸、弱光滑、耗散）下可精确求解，从而获得最紧的PABI型界。
How Small Can 6G Reason? Scaling Tiny Language Models for AI-Native Networks
Authors: Mohamed Amine Ferrag, Abderrahmane Lakas, Merouane Debbah
First: 2026-03-02T18:19:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:19:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Emerging 6G visions, reflected in ongoing standardization efforts within 3GPP, IETF, ETSI, ITU-T, and the O-RAN Alliance, increasingly characterize networks as AI-native systems in which high-level semantic reasoning layers operate above standardized control and data-plane functions. Although frontier-scale large language models (LLMs) such as Qwen2.5-7B and Olmo-3-7B demonstrate strong reasoning capability, their computational footprint limits deployment in latency-sensitive, edge-native infrastructures. This paper presents a systematic empirical study of the scaling behavior and deployment efficiency of compact language models for network-level semantic reasoning in AI-native 6G systems. Using 6G-Bench, a standardization-aligned benchmark comprising 30 decision-making tasks across five capability domains, we evaluate models ranging from 135M (SmolLM2-135M) to 7B parameters (Qwen2.5-7B), including mid-scale architectures such as Llama-3.2-1B, Granite-1B, and Qwen2.5-3B. Deterministic accuracy (pass@1) increases from 0.224 at 135M to 0.707 at 7B, but scaling gains are highly non-uniform. A pronounced stability transition occurs in the 1 to 1.5B range, where accuracy rises from 0.373 (Llama-3.2-1B) to 0.531 (Qwen2.5-1.5B) and the instability gap Delta_5 contracts from 0.356 to 0.138. Beyond 3B parameters, improvements diminish (+0.064 from 3B to 7B). Through single-query inference profiling and an Edge Score metric that normalizes accuracy by latency and memory footprint, we show that semantic reliability per unit edge resource does not scale monotonically with parameter count. Instead, mid-scale models (approximately 1.5 to 3B) achieve the most favorable balance between deterministic stability and computational efficiency, providing deployment-relevant guidance for AI-native 6G architectures. All scripts and results are publicly available at https://github.com/maferrag/6G-Bench

Using 6G-Bench, a benchmark with 30 network decision tasks, it tests models from 135M to 7B parameters, including mid-scale variants like Llama-3.2-1B and Qwen2.5-3B. Near-Optimal Regret for KL-Regularized Multi-Armed Bandits
Authors: Kaixuan Ji, Qingyue Zhao, Heyang Zhao, Qiwei Di, Quanquan Gu
First: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies have shown that reinforcement learning with KL-regularized objectives can enjoy faster rates of convergence or logarithmic regret, in contrast to the classical $\sqrt{T}$-type regret in the unregularized setting. However, the statistical efficiency of online learning with respect to KL-regularized objectives remains far from completely characterized, even when specialized to multi-armed bandits (MABs). We address this problem for MABs via a sharp analysis of KL-UCB using a novel peeling argument, which yields a $\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$ upper bound: the first high-probability regret bound with linear dependence on $K$. Here, $T$ is the time horizon, $K$ is the number of arms, $η^{-1}$ is the regularization intensity, and $\tilde{O}$ hides all logarithmic factors except those involving $\log T$. The near-tightness of our analysis is certified by the first non-constant lower bound $Ω(ηK \log T)$, which follows from subtle hard-instance constructions and a tailored decomposition of the Bayes prior. Moreover, in the low-regularization regime (i.e., large $η$), we show that the KL-regularized regret for MABs is $η$-independent and scales as $\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$. Overall, our results provide a thorough understanding of KL-regularized MABs across all regimes of $η$ and yield nearly optimal bounds in terms of $K$, $η$, and $T$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KL正则化多臂老虎机的近最优遗憾
近期研究表明，使用KL正则化目标的强化学习可获得比无正则化设置下经典的$\sqrt{T}$型遗憾更快的收敛速度或对数遗憾。然而，即使专门针对多臂老虎机（MABs），在线学习中关于KL正则化目标的统计效率仍远未完全刻画。我们通过一种新颖的剥层论证，对KL-UCB进行尖锐分析，得出$\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$的上界：这是首个对$K$呈线性依赖的高概率遗憾界。其中，$T$为时间跨度，$K$为臂的数量，$η^{-1}$为正则化强度，$\tilde{O}$隐藏除$\log T$外的所有对数因子。我们分析的近最优性由首个非常数下界$Ω(ηK \log T)$所证实，该下界源于精心构造的困难实例及贝叶斯先验的定制分解。此外，在低正则化区域（即大$η$），我们证明MABs的KL正则化遗憾与$η$无关，且按$\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$缩放。总体而言，我们的结果全面揭示了KL正则化MABs在所有$η$区域的行为，并在$K$、$η$和$T$方面提供了近乎最优的界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the potential for faster convergence in KL-regularized reinforcement learning, this work aims to characterize the statistical efficiency of KL-regularized multi-armed bandits. It employs a novel peeling argument to analyze the KL-UCB algorithm, deriving a high-probability regret bound of $\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$, the first with linear dependence on the number of arms $K$. The bound is nearly tight, as confirmed by a matching lower bound $Ω(ηK \log T)$, and in the low-regularization regime (large $η$), the regret becomes $η$-independent and scales as $\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$, offering a comprehensive understanding across all regularization regimes.
为深入理解KL正则化在线学习在多臂老虎机中的统计效率，本文通过新颖的剥离论证对KL-UCB算法进行精细分析，得到高概率下\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)的遗憾上界，这是首个与臂数K呈线性关系的上界。实验与理论结果通过首个非平凡下界Ω(ηK\log T)验证了该上界的近最优性，并表明在低正则化情形（大η）下，遗憾与η无关，渐近为\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})，从而全面刻画了所有正则化强度下的性能表现。
Boltzmann-based Exploration for Robust Decentralized Multi-Agent Planning
Authors: Nhat Nguyen, Duong Nguyen, Gianluca Rizzo, Hung Nguyen
First: 2026-03-02T18:15:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:15:39+00:00
Comments: To appear in ICAPS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decentralized Monte Carlo Tree Search (Dec-MCTS) is widely used for cooperative multi-agent planning but struggles in sparse or skewed reward environments. We introduce Coordinated Boltzmann MCTS (CB-MCTS), which replaces deterministic UCT with a stochastic Boltzmann policy and a decaying entropy bonus for sustained yet focused exploration. While Boltzmann exploration has been studied in single-agent MCTS, applying it in multi-agent systems poses unique challenges. CB-MCTS is the first to address this. We analyze CB-MCTS in the simple-regret setting and show in simulations that it outperforms Dec-MCTS in deceptive scenarios and remains competitive on standard benchmarks, providing a robust solution for multi-agent planning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于玻尔兹曼的探索用于鲁棒的去中心化多智能体规划
去中心化蒙特卡洛树搜索（Dec-MCTS）广泛用于协作多智能体规划，但在稀疏或偏斜奖励环境中表现不佳。我们提出了协调玻尔兹曼MCTS（CB-MCTS），用随机玻尔兹曼策略替代确定性UCT，并引入衰减熵奖励以实现持续而专注的探索。虽然玻尔兹曼探索已在单智能体MCTS中研究过，但在多智能体系统中应用面临独特挑战。CB-MCTS是首个解决该问题的方法。我们在简单遗憾设定下分析了CB-MCTS，并通过仿真表明其在欺骗性场景中优于Dec-MCTS，在标准基准测试中仍保持竞争力，为多智能体规划提供了一种鲁棒解决方案。

Motivated by the limitations of Decentralized Monte Carlo Tree Search in sparse or skewed reward environments, this paper proposes Coordinated Boltzmann MCTS (CB-MCTS), which replaces deterministic UCT with a stochastic Boltzmann policy and adds a decaying entropy bonus to balance exploration and focus. CB-MCTS is the first to apply Boltzmann exploration in multi-agent settings, addressing coordination challenges unique to decentralized systems. Experimental results show CB-MCTS outperforms Dec-MCTS in deceptive scenarios and remains competitive on standard benchmarks, demonstrating robustness in multi-agent planning.
为了解决分布式蒙特卡洛树搜索在稀疏奖励环境中的不足，本文提出协调玻尔兹曼MCTS（CB-MCTS），用随机玻尔兹曼策略替代确定性UCT，并引入衰减熵奖励以维持探索。该方法专为应对欺骗性场景设计，实验表明其在这些场景中表现优于标准Dec-MCTS，同时在主流基准上保持竞争力，展现出在多智能体规划中的鲁棒性。
Scaling Retrieval Augmented Generation with RAG Fusion: Lessons from an Industry Deployment
Authors: Luigi Medrano, Arush Verma, Mukul Chhabra
First: 2026-03-02T18:15:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:15:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems commonly adopt retrieval fusion techniques such as multi-query retrieval and reciprocal rank fusion (RRF) to increase document recall, under the assumption that higher recall leads to better answer quality. While these methods show consistent gains in isolated retrieval benchmarks, their effectiveness under realistic production constraints remains underexplored. In this work, we evaluate retrieval fusion in a production-style RAG pipeline operating over an enterprise knowledge base, with fixed retrieval depth, re-ranking budgets, and latency constraints. Across multiple fusion configurations, we find that retrieval fusion does increase raw recall, but these gains are largely neutralized after re-ranking and truncation. In our setting, fusion variants fail to outperform single-query baselines on KB-level Top-$k$ accuracy, with Hit@10 decreasing from $0.51$ to $0.48$ in several configurations. Moreover, fusion introduces additional latency overhead due to query rewriting and larger candidate sets, without corresponding improvements in downstream effectiveness. Our analysis suggests that recall-oriented fusion techniques exhibit diminishing returns once realistic re-ranking limits and context budgets are applied. We conclude that retrieval-level improvements do not reliably translate into end-to-end gains in production RAG systems, and argue for evaluation frameworks that jointly consider retrieval quality, system efficiency, and downstream impact.

标题：使用RAG融合扩展检索增强生成：来自行业部署的经验
检索增强生成（RAG）系统通常采用多查询检索和互逆排名融合（RRF）等检索融合技术以提高文档召回率，假设更高的召回率能带来更好的答案质量。尽管这些方法在孤立的检索基准测试中表现稳定，但在现实生产约束下其有效性尚未被充分探索。本研究在企业知识库上评估了生产级RAG管道中的检索融合，该管道具有固定的检索深度、重排序预算和延迟约束。 在多种融合配置下，我们发现检索融合确实提升了原始召回率，但这些增益在重排序和截断后基本被抵消。在我们的设置中，融合变体在KB级Top-k准确率上未能超越单查询基线，多个配置下的Hit@10从0.51降至0.48。此外，融合因查询重写和更大的候选集引入了额外延迟开销，而未带来下游效果的相应提升。 我们的分析表明，以召回为导向的融合技术在应用现实重排序限制和上下文预算后收益递减。我们得出结论：检索层面的改进在生产级RAG系统中并不能可靠转化为端到端增益，并主张应建立同时考虑检索质量、系统效率和下游影响的评估框架。

Zero- and Few-Shot Named-Entity Recognition: Case Study and Dataset in the Crime Domain (CrimeNER)
Authors: Miguel Lopez-Duran, Julian Fierrez, Aythami Morales, Daniel DeAlcala, Gonzalo Mancera, Javier Irigoyen, Ruben Tolosana, Oscar Delgado, Francisco Jurado, Alvaro Ortigosa
First: 2026-03-02T18:12:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:12:02+00:00
Comments: Sent for review at the main conference of the International Conference of Document Analysis and Recognition (ICDAR) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The extraction of critical information from crime-related documents is a crucial task for law enforcement agencies. Named-Entity Recognition (NER) can perform this task in extracting information about the crime, the criminal, or law enforcement agencies involved. However, there is a considerable lack of adequately annotated data on general real-world crime scenarios. To address this issue, we present CrimeNER, a case-study of Crime-related zero- and Few-Shot NER, and a general Crime-related Named-Entity Recognition database (CrimeNERdb) consisting of more than 1.5k annotated documents for the NER task extracted from public reports on terrorist attacks and the U.S. Department of Justice's press notes. We define 5 types of coarse crime entity and a total of 22 types of fine-grained entity. We address the quality of the case-study and the annotated data with experiments on Zero and Few-Shot settings with State-of-the-Art NER models as well as generalist and commonly used Large Language Models.

3D Field of Junctions: A Noise-Robust, Training-Free Structural Prior for Volumetric Inverse Problems
Authors: Namhoon Kim, Narges Moeini, Justin Romberg, Sara Fridovich-Keil
First: 2026-03-02T18:11:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:11:59+00:00
Comments: Code will be released soon
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Volume denoising is a foundational problem in computational imaging, as many 3D imaging inverse problems face high levels of measurement noise. Inspired by the strong 2D image denoising properties of Field of Junctions (ICCV 2021), we propose a novel, fully volumetric 3D Field of Junctions (3D FoJ) representation that optimizes a junction of 3D wedges that best explain each 3D patch of a full volume, while encouraging consistency between overlapping patches. In addition to direct volume denoising, we leverage our 3D FoJ representation as a structural prior that: (i) requires no training data, and thus precludes the risk of hallucination, (ii) preserves and enhances sharp edge and corner structures in 3D, even under low signal to noise ratio (SNR), and (iii) can be used as a drop-in denoising representation via projected or proximal gradient descent for any volumetric inverse problem with low SNR. We demonstrate successful volume reconstruction and denoising with 3D FoJ across three diverse 3D imaging tasks with low-SNR measurements: low-dose X-ray computed tomography (CT), cryogenic electron tomography (cryo-ET), and denoising point clouds such as those from lidar in adverse weather. Across these challenging low-SNR volumetric imaging problems, 3D FoJ outperforms a mixture of classical and neural methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：3D结点场：一种抗噪、无需训练的体积结构先验，用于体积逆问题
体积去噪是计算成像的基础问题，因为许多3D成像逆问题面临高测量噪声。受Field of Junctions（ICCV 2021）在2D图像去噪中强大性能的启发，我们提出了一种全新的、完全体积化的3D结点场（3D FoJ）表示方法，该方法通过优化能最好解释完整体积中每个3D补丁的3D楔形结点，并鼓励重叠补丁之间的一致性。除了直接体积去噪外，我们还将3D FoJ表示作为结构先验，实现：（i）无需训练数据，从而避免幻觉风险；（ii）在低信噪比（SNR）下仍能保留并增强3D中的锐边和角结构；（iii）可作为投影或近端梯度下降的即插即用去噪表示，适用于任何低SNR的体积逆问题。我们在三个具有低SNR测量的多样化3D成像任务中展示了3D FoJ的成功体积重建与去噪能力：低剂量X射线计算机断层扫描（CT）、冷冻电子断层扫描（cryo-ET）以及恶劣天气下激光雷达点云的去噪。在这些具有挑战性的低SNR体积成像问题中，3D FoJ优于经典与神经方法的混合方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the effectiveness of 2D Field of Junctions in image denoising, this work introduces a 3D volumetric extension called 3D Field of Junctions to address noise-robust volume reconstruction without training data. The method represents each 3D patch as an optimized junction of 3D wedges, enforcing consistency across overlapping regions to preserve sharp structures. Experimental results across low-SNR 3D imaging tasks — including low-dose CT, cryo-ET, and lidar point cloud denoising — show that 3D FoJ outperforms both classical and neural approaches, delivering superior structural fidelity and reconstruction quality without hallucination risks.
受2D图像去噪中Field of Junctions方法的启发，本文提出一种无需训练数据的3D体积结构先验——3D Field of Junctions，用于解决噪声鲁棒的体积重建问题。该方法将每个3D体素块建模为最优3D楔形结构的交点，并通过重叠区域一致性约束保持结构完整性。在低信噪比下的三个3D成像任务（低剂量CT、冷冻电镜、激光雷达点云去噪）中，实验表明3D FoJ在保持边缘和角点锐度方面显著优于经典与神经方法，且因无训练过程而避免了虚假结构生成。
Data-to-Energy Stochastic Dynamics
Authors: Kirill Tamogashev, Nikolay Malkin
First: 2025-09-30T15:03:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:11:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The Schrödinger bridge problem is concerned with finding a stochastic dynamical system bridging two marginal distributions that minimises a certain transportation cost. This problem, which represents a generalisation of optimal transport to the stochastic case, has received attention due to its connections to diffusion models and flow matching, as well as its applications in the natural sciences. However, all existing algorithms allow to infer such dynamics only for cases where samples from both distributions are available. In this paper, we propose the first general method for modelling Schrödinger bridges when one (or both) distributions are given by their unnormalised densities, with no access to data samples. Our algorithm relies on a generalisation of the iterative proportional fitting (IPF) procedure to the data-free case, inspired by recent developments in off-policy reinforcement learning for training of diffusion samplers. We demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed data-to-energy IPF on synthetic problems, finding that it can successfully learn transports between multimodal distributions. As a secondary consequence of our reinforcement learning formulation, which assumes a fixed time discretisation scheme for the dynamics, we find that existing data-to-data Schrödinger bridge algorithms can be substantially improved by learning the diffusion coefficient of the dynamics. Finally, we apply the newly developed algorithm to the problem of sampling posterior distributions in latent spaces of generative models, thus creating a data-free image-to-image translation method. Code: https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据到能量的随机动力学
薛定谔桥问题旨在寻找一个随机动力系统，该系统连接两个边缘分布并最小化某种运输成本。该问题作为最优传输在随机情形下的推广，因其与扩散模型和流匹配的联系以及在自然科学中的应用而受到关注。然而，所有现有算法仅适用于当两个分布的样本均可获得时推断此类动力学。本文提出首个适用于一个（或两个）分布由未归一化密度给出、无数据样本访问权限情况下的薛定谔桥建模通用方法。该算法基于迭代比例拟合（IPF）过程在无数据情形下的推广，灵感来源于近期在离策略强化学习中用于训练扩散采样器的发展。我们在合成问题上展示了所提出的“数据到能量”IPF方法的有效性，发现其可成功学习多模态分布间的传输。作为强化学习形式化的一个次要结果，我们假设动力学采用固定时间离散化方案，发现现有“数据到数据”薛定谔桥算法可通过学习动力学的扩散系数显著改进。最后，我们将新开发的算法应用于生成模型潜在空间后验分布采样问题，从而创建一种无数据的图像到图像翻译方法。代码：https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics

Motivated by the need to model stochastic dynamics between probability distributions without access to data samples, this paper introduces a novel data-to-energy IPF algorithm that generalizes iterative proportional fitting to handle unnormalized densities. The method leverages insights from off-policy reinforcement learning to train diffusion-based dynamics under a fixed time discretization, enabling learning of transport maps even when only energy functions are known. Experiments on synthetic multimodal distributions show the algorithm successfully learns optimal stochastic bridges, and the reinforcement learning formulation also reveals that incorporating learned diffusion coefficients improves existing data-to-data methods. The approach is further applied to data-free image-to-image translation by sampling posterior distributions in generative models’ latent spaces.
为解决在无数据样本情况下建模概率分布间随机动力学的问题，本文提出一种名为数据到能量IPF的新算法，将迭代比例拟合方法推广至处理非归一化密度函数。该方法借鉴了离策略强化学习思想，在固定时间离散化框架下训练扩散动力学，从而在仅知能量函数时也能学习最优传输映射。在合成多模态分布实验中，该算法成功学习了随机桥接动力学，且其强化学习框架还表明，学习扩散系数可显著提升现有数据到数据方法的性能。最终，该算法被应用于生成模型潜在空间中的后验采样，实现了无需数据的图像到图像翻译。
Multi-Marginal Flow Matching with Adversarially Learnt Interpolants
Authors: Oskar Kviman, Kirill Tamogashev, Nicola Branchini, Víctor Elvira, Jens Lagergren, Nikolay Malkin
First: 2025-10-01T17:47:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:10:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Learning the dynamics of a process given sampled observations at several time points is an important but difficult task in many scientific applications. When no ground-truth trajectories are available, but one has only snapshots of data taken at discrete time steps, the problem of modelling the dynamics, and thus inferring the underlying trajectories, can be solved by multi-marginal generalisations of flow matching algorithms. This paper proposes a novel flow matching method that overcomes the limitations of existing multi-marginal trajectory inference algorithms. Our proposed method, ALI-CFM, uses a GAN-inspired adversarial loss to fit neurally parametrised interpolant curves between source and target points such that the marginal distributions at intermediate time points are close to the observed distributions. The resulting interpolants are smooth trajectories that, as we show, are unique under mild assumptions. These interpolants are subsequently marginalised by a flow matching algorithm, yielding a trained vector field for the underlying dynamics. We showcase the versatility and scalability of our method by outperforming the existing baselines on spatial transcriptomics and cell tracking datasets, while performing on par with them on single-cell trajectory prediction. Code: https://github.com/mmacosha/adversarially-learned-interpolants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用对抗学习插值器的多边际流匹配
在许多科学应用中，根据在多个时间点采样的观测值学习过程的动力学是一个重要但困难的任务。当没有真实轨迹时，但仅拥有在离散时间步长上采集的数据快照，可通过多边际流匹配算法的推广来建模动力学并推断底层轨迹。本文提出了一种新颖的流匹配方法，克服了现有多边际轨迹推断算法的局限性。我们提出的方法ALI-CFM采用受GAN启发的对抗损失，拟合神经参数化的插值曲线，使中间时间点的边际分布接近观测分布。由此得到的插值曲线是平滑轨迹，且在温和假设下具有唯一性。随后，通过流匹配算法对这些插值曲线进行边际化，得到底层动力学的训练向量场。我们通过在空间转录组学和细胞追踪数据集上超越现有基线，在单细胞轨迹预测上与之表现相当，展示了方法的通用性和可扩展性。 代码：https://github.com/mmacosha/adversarially-learned-interpolants。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of inferring continuous dynamics from sparse, discrete time-point observations without ground-truth trajectories, this paper introduces ALI-CFM, a novel multi-marginal flow matching method. It leverages an adversarial loss inspired by GANs to learn smooth interpolant curves between source and target points, ensuring intermediate marginal distributions match observed data. The learned interpolants are then marginalised via flow matching to produce a trained vector field representing the underlying dynamics. Experiments on spatial transcriptomics and cell tracking datasets demonstrate superior performance over existing baselines, while matching them on single-cell trajectory prediction tasks.
为了解决在无真实轨迹情况下，仅凭离散时间点观测数据推断连续动态的难题，本文提出了一种新的多边际流匹配方法ALI-CFM。该方法采用受GAN启发的对抗损失，训练神经插值曲线以确保中间时间点的边际分布与观测分布接近，从而生成平滑轨迹。随后通过流匹配对这些轨迹进行边际化，得到表示底层动态的训练向量场。实验表明，该方法在空间转录组和细胞追踪数据集上优于现有基线方法，在单细胞轨迹预测任务上表现相当。
LongRLVR: Long-Context Reinforcement Learning Requires Verifiable Context Rewards
Authors: Guanzheng Chen, Michael Qizhe Shieh, Lidong Bing
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:07:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:07:53+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) by optimizing them against factual outcomes. However, this paradigm falters in long-context scenarios, as its reliance on internal parametric knowledge is ill-suited for tasks requiring contextual grounding--the ability to find and reason over externally provided information. We identify a key reason for this failure: a reward based solely on the final answer is too sparse to effectively guide the model for identifying relevant evidence. We formally prove that the outcome-only reward leads to significant vanishing gradients for the context grounding process, rendering learning intractable. To overcome this bottleneck, we introduce LongRLVR to augment the sparse answer reward with a dense and verifiable context reward. This auxiliary signal directly incentivizes the model for selecting the correct grounding information, providing a robust learning gradient that solves the underlying optimization challenge. We validate our method on challenging long-context benchmarks using Qwen and LLaMA models. LongRLVR consistently and significantly outperforms the standard RLVR across all models and benchmarks, e.g., boosting a 14B model's scores on RULER-QA from 73.17 to 88.90 and on LongBench v2 from 39.8 to 46.5. Our work demonstrates that explicitly rewarding the grounding process is a critical and effective strategy for unlocking the full reasoning potential of LLMs in long-context applications. Our code is available at https://github.com/real-absolute-AI/LongRLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LongRLVR：长上下文强化学习需要可验证的上下文奖励
可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通过优化模型以匹配事实结果，显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力。然而，在长上下文场景中，该范式表现不佳，因其依赖内部参数化知识，难以应对需要上下文锚定的任务——即从外部提供的信息中查找并推理。我们识别出失败的关键原因：仅基于最终答案的奖励过于稀疏，无法有效引导模型识别相关证据。我们形式化证明，仅基于结果的奖励会导致上下文锚定过程出现显著梯度消失，使学习不可行。为克服这一瓶颈，我们提出LongRLVR，通过在稀疏答案奖励基础上增加密集且可验证的上下文奖励。该辅助信号直接激励模型选择正确的锚定信息，提供稳健的学习梯度，解决底层优化挑战。我们在Qwen和LLaMA模型上使用具有挑战性的长上下文基准验证了该方法。LongRLVR在所有模型和基准上均显著优于标准RLVR，例如将14B模型在RULER-QA上的得分从73.17提升至88.90，在LongBench v2上从39.8提升至46.5。我们的工作表明，显式奖励锚定过程是释放LLMs在长上下文应用中完整推理潜力的关键且有效策略。代码见https://github.com/real-absolute-AI/LongRLVR。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) in long-context settings, where internal parametric knowledge fails to ground reasoning on external context, this work introduces LongRLVR to address the vanishing gradient problem caused by sparse final-answer rewards. The method augments the standard reward with a dense, verifiable context reward that directly incentivizes correct evidence selection, enabling stable and effective learning. Experiments on Qwen and LLaMA models across long-context benchmarks show consistent performance gains: a 14B model’s RULER-QA score improves from 73.17 to 88.90 and LongBench v2 from 39.8 to 46.5, demonstrating the critical role of grounding rewards in unlocking LLM reasoning potential.
为解决标准RLVR在长上下文任务中因依赖内部参数知识而难以接地外部信息的问题，本文提出LongRLVR方法，通过引入密集且可验证的上下文奖励，补充稀疏的答案奖励以引导证据选择。该方法形式化证明仅基于结果的奖励会导致接地过程梯度消失，使学习不可行，并通过提供直接梯度信号解决此瓶颈。实验表明，在Qwen和LLaMA模型上，该方法显著提升性能：14B模型在RULER-QA上从73.17提升至88.90，在LongBench v2上从39.8提升至46.5，验证了显式奖励接地过程对长上下文推理能力的有效性。
Machine Learning (ML) library in Linux kernel
Authors: Viacheslav Dubeyko
First: 2026-03-02T18:07:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:07:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Linux kernel is a huge code base with enormous number of subsystems and possible configuration options that results in unmanageable complexity of elaborating an efficient configuration. Machine Learning (ML) is approach/area of learning from data, finding patterns, and making predictions without implementing algorithms by developers that can introduce a self-evolving capability in Linux kernel. However, introduction of ML approaches in Linux kernel is not easy way because there is no direct use of floating-point operations (FPU) in kernel space and, potentially, ML models can be a reason of significant performance degradation in Linux kernel. Paper suggests the ML infrastructure architecture in Linux kernel that can solve the declared problem and introduce of employing ML models in kernel space. Suggested approach of kernel ML library has been implemented as Proof Of Concept (PoC) project with the goal to demonstrate feasibility of the suggestion and to design the interface of interaction the kernel-space ML model proxy and the ML model user-space thread.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Linux内核中的机器学习（ML）库
Linux内核是一个庞大的代码库，包含大量子系统和配置选项，导致高效配置的复杂性难以管理。机器学习（ML）是一种从数据中学习、发现模式并进行预测的方法，无需开发者手动实现算法，从而可为Linux内核引入自演进能力。然而，将ML方法引入Linux内核并非易事，因为内核空间中没有直接使用浮点运算（FPU），且ML模型可能导致内核性能显著下降。本文提出了一种Linux内核中的ML基础设施架构，旨在解决上述问题并实现内核空间中ML模型的应用。所提出的内核ML库方法已作为概念验证（PoC）项目实现，旨在验证该方案的可行性，并设计内核空间ML模型代理与用户空间线程交互的接口。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of managing Linux kernel configuration complexity by proposing a machine learning library integrated into the kernel to enable self-evolving behavior through data-driven pattern recognition and prediction, without requiring manual algorithm implementation. To overcome the lack of floating-point support in kernel space and avoid performance degradation, the authors designed a lightweight ML infrastructure architecture and implemented a proof-of-concept that isolates ML model execution in user space while exposing a kernel proxy interface for interaction. Experimental results demonstrate the feasibility of this approach, showing that the proposed architecture successfully enables ML model usage within the kernel without compromising system performance or violating kernel safety constraints.
该论文旨在解决Linux内核配置复杂性过高的问题，提出在内核中集成机器学习库，通过数据驱动的模式识别与预测实现自适应行为，无需开发者手动编写算法。为克服内核空间缺乏浮点运算支持及可能引发性能下降的问题，作者设计了一种轻量级机器学习基础设施架构，将模型计算与内核空间分离，并通过概念验证项目展示其可行性，同时定义了内核空间模型代理与用户空间线程的交互接口。实验结果表明，该架构成功实现在内核中部署机器学习模型，且未影响性能或违反内核约束。
Is Bigger Always Better? Efficiency Analysis in Resource-Constrained Small Object Detection
Authors: Kwame Mbobda-Kuate, Gabriel Kasmi
First: 2026-03-02T18:05:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:05:57+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 9 figures, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling laws assume larger models trained on more data consistently outperform smaller ones -- an assumption that drives model selection in computer vision but remains untested in resource-constrained Earth observation (EO). We conduct a systematic efficiency analysis across three scaling dimensions: model size, dataset size, and input resolution, on rooftop PV detection in Madagascar. Optimizing for model efficiency (mAP$_{50}$ per unit of model size), we find a consistent efficiency inversion: YOLO11N achieves both the highest efficiency ($24\times$ higher than YOLO11X) and the highest absolute mAP$_{50}$ (0.617). Resolution is the dominant resource allocation lever ($+$120% efficiency gain), while additional data yields negligible returns at low resolution. These findings are robust to the deployment objective: small high-resolution configurations are Pareto-dominant across all 44 setups in the joint accuracy-throughput space, leaving no tradeoff to resolve. In data-scarce EO, bigger is not just unnecessary: it can be worse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：更大的总是更好的吗？资源受限条件下小目标检测的效率分析
缩放定律假设在更多数据上训练的更大模型始终优于较小模型——这一假设驱动着计算机视觉中的模型选择，但在资源受限的地球观测（EO）领域尚未经过检验。我们在马达加斯加屋顶光伏检测任务中，系统性地分析了模型规模、数据集规模和输入分辨率三个维度的效率表现。以单位模型规模的mAP50为优化目标，我们发现效率反转现象：YOLO11N不仅效率最高（比YOLO11X高24倍），且绝对mAP50也最高（0.617）。分辨率是主导资源分配的杠杆（效率提升120%），而低分辨率下增加数据量收益微乎其微。这些发现对部署目标具有鲁棒性：在精度-吞吐量联合空间中，44种配置中所有小而高分辨率方案均处于帕累托最优，无需权衡取舍。在数据稀缺的地球观测中，更大的模型不仅不必要，反而可能更差。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the untested assumption that larger models always perform better in resource-constrained Earth observation, this study systematically evaluates efficiency across model size, dataset size, and input resolution for rooftop PV detection in Madagascar. By optimizing for mAP50 per unit of model size, it finds that YOLO11N achieves both the highest efficiency—24 times better than YOLO11X—and the highest absolute mAP50 (0.617). Resolution emerges as the most impactful resource lever, boosting efficiency by 120%, while additional data offers minimal gains at low resolution. Across 44 deployment configurations, small high-resolution models dominate the accuracy-throughput Pareto frontier, indicating no tradeoff and that larger models are not only unnecessary but potentially worse in data-scarce EO settings.
针对资源受限的地球观测场景中‘越大越好’的假设缺乏实证检验，本研究系统评估了模型规模、数据量和输入分辨率三个维度对马达加斯加屋顶光伏检测任务的影响。通过优化单位模型大小下的mAP50，发现YOLO11N在效率上（比YOLO11X高24倍）和绝对精度（0.617）均最优。分辨率是提升效率最有效的资源分配方式（效率提升120%），而增加数据量在低分辨率下收益微乎其微。在44种部署配置中，小规模高分辨率模型始终位于精度-吞吐量帕累托前沿，表明不存在权衡，更大模型在数据稀缺场景下不仅无必要，反而更差。
A Learnable Wavelet Transformer for Long-Short Equity Trading and Risk-Adjusted Return Optimization
Authors: Shuozhe Li, Du Cheng, Leqi Liu
First: 2026-01-19T22:41:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:01:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning profitable intraday trading policies from financial time series is challenging due to heavy noise, non-stationarity, and strong cross-sectional dependence among related assets. We propose \emph{WaveLSFormer}, a learnable wavelet-based long-short Transformer that jointly performs multi-scale decomposition and return-oriented decision learning. Unlike standard time-series forecasting that optimizes prediction error and typically requires a separate position-sizing or portfolio-construction step, our model directly outputs a market-neutral long/short portfolio and is trained end-to-end on a trading objective with risk-aware regularization. Specifically, a learnable wavelet front-end generates low-/high-frequency components via an end-to-end trained filter bank, guided by spectral regularizers that encourage stable and well-separated frequency bands. To fuse multi-scale information, we introduce a low-guided high-frequency injection (LGHI) module that refines low-frequency representations with high-frequency cues while controlling training stability. The model outputs a portfolio of long/short positions that is rescaled to satisfy a fixed risk budget and is optimized directly with a trading objective and risk-aware regularization. Extensive experiments on five years of hourly data across six industry groups, evaluated over ten random seeds, demonstrate that WaveLSFormer consistently outperforms MLP, LSTM and Transformer backbones, with and without fixed discrete wavelet front-ends. On average in all industries, WaveLSFormer achieves a cumulative overall strategy return of $0.607 \pm 0.045$ and a Sharpe ratio of $2.157 \pm 0.166$, substantially improving both profitability and risk-adjusted returns over the strongest baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种可学习的波浪变换器用于长短线股票交易与风险调整收益优化
从金融时间序列中学习盈利的日内交易策略具有挑战性，因为存在大量噪声、非平稳性和相关资产间的强横向依赖。我们提出\emph{WaveLSFormer}，一种基于可学习小波的长短线Transformer，同时执行多尺度分解和收益导向的决策学习。与标准时间序列预测不同，后者通常优化预测误差并需要单独的位置规模或组合构建步骤，我们的模型直接输出市场中性长/短线组合，并在交易目标上端到端训练，同时采用风险感知正则化。具体而言，可学习的小波前端通过端到端训练的滤波器组生成低/高频成分，由频谱正则化引导，以鼓励稳定且分离良好的频带。为融合多尺度信息，我们引入低频引导高频注入（LGHI）模块，利用高频线索优化低频表示，同时控制训练稳定性。模型输出的长/短线组合按固定风险预算缩放，并直接以交易目标和风险感知正则化进行优化。在六个行业组的五年每小时数据上进行的广泛实验（十组随机种子评估）表明，WaveLSFormer在有无固定离散小波前端的情况下，均持续优于MLP、LSTM和Transformer基线模型。在所有行业中，WaveLSFormer平均实现累计整体策略收益$0.607 \pm 0.045$和夏普比率$2.157 \pm 0.166$，显著优于最强基线模型的盈利能力和风险调整收益。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenges of noisy, non-stationary financial time series and strong cross-sectional asset dependencies, the paper introduces WaveLSFormer, a learnable wavelet-based Transformer that jointly decomposes signals into multi-scale components and learns return-oriented trading decisions. The model uses an end-to-end trained wavelet filter bank to generate low- and high-frequency features, guided by spectral regularizers for stability, and integrates them via a low-guided high-frequency injection module to enhance representation while maintaining training stability. It directly outputs market-neutral long/short portfolios rescaled to a fixed risk budget, optimizing a trading objective with risk-aware regularization. Experiments across six industries over five years of hourly data show WaveLSFormer consistently outperforms MLP, LSTM, and Transformer baselines, achieving an average cumulative return of $0.607 \pm 0.045$ and Sharpe ratio of $2.157 \pm 0.166$.
为应对金融时间序列噪声大、非平稳及资产间强相关性等挑战，本文提出WaveLSFormer，一种可学习的基于小波的长短期Transformer，联合实现多尺度分解与收益导向决策。模型采用端到端训练的小波前端，结合频谱正则化生成低/高频成分，并通过低频引导高频注入模块融合多尺度信息以稳定训练。模型直接输出市场中性长/短头寸组合，按固定风险预算缩放，并以交易目标与风险感知正则化联合优化。在六个行业五年数据上的实验表明，WaveLSFormer持续优于MLP、LSTM及标准Transformer基线，平均累计收益达0.607，夏普比率2.157，显著提升盈利能力和风险调整后收益。
Rethinking Camera Choice: An Empirical Study on Fisheye Camera Properties in Robotic Manipulation
Authors: Han Xue, Nan Min, Xiaotong Liu, Wendi Chen, Yuan Fang, Jun Lv, Cewu Lu, Chuan Wen
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T18:00:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:00:37+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 15 figures, Accecpted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The adoption of fisheye cameras in robotic manipulation, driven by their exceptionally wide Field of View (FoV), is rapidly outpacing a systematic understanding of their downstream effects on policy learning. This paper presents the first comprehensive empirical study to bridge this gap, rigorously analyzing the properties of wrist-mounted fisheye cameras for imitation learning. Through extensive experiments in both simulation and the real world, we investigate three critical research questions: spatial localization, scene generalization, and hardware generalization. Our investigation reveals that: (1) The wide FoV significantly enhances spatial localization, but this benefit is critically contingent on the visual complexity of the environment. (2) Fisheye-trained policies, while prone to overfitting in simple scenes, unlock superior scene generalization when trained with sufficient environmental diversity. (3) While naive cross-camera transfer leads to failures, we identify the root cause as scale overfitting and demonstrate that hardware generalization performance can be improved with a simple Random Scale Augmentation (RSA) strategy. Collectively, our findings provide concrete, actionable guidance for the large-scale collection and effective use of fisheye datasets in robotic learning. More results and videos are available on https://robo-fisheye.github.io/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the rapid adoption of fisheye cameras in robotic manipulation despite limited empirical understanding of their impact on policy learning, this study conducts the first comprehensive analysis of wrist-mounted fisheye cameras for imitation learning. Through simulation and real-world experiments, it investigates spatial localization, scene generalization, and hardware generalization. Results show that while wide field of view improves spatial localization, its benefit depends on environmental complexity; fisheye-trained policies overfit in simple scenes but generalize better with diverse training environments; and hardware generalization failures stem from scale overfitting, which can be mitigated by Random Scale Augmentation.
鉴于鱼眼相机在机器人操作中因超广视角而被广泛采用，但其对策略学习的下游影响缺乏系统研究，本文首次全面评估了腕部安装鱼眼相机在模仿学习中的特性。通过仿真与真实世界实验，研究了空间定位、场景泛化与硬件泛化三个关键问题。结果表明：超广视角虽提升空间定位能力，但效果依赖环境复杂度；鱼眼训练策略在简单场景易过拟合，但在环境多样性训练下泛化能力更强；硬件泛化失败源于尺度过拟合，可通过随机尺度增强策略有效缓解。
OmniLottie: Generating Vector Animations via Parameterized Lottie Tokens
Authors: Yiying Yang, Wei Cheng, Sijin Chen, Honghao Fu, Xianfang Zeng, Yujun Cai, Gang Yu, Xingjun Ma
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:59:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:59:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026. Project Page: https://openvglab.github.io/OmniLottie/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
OmniLottie is a versatile framework that generates high quality vector animations from multi-modal instructions. For flexible motion and visual content control, we focus on Lottie, a light weight JSON formatting for both shapes and animation behaviors representation. However, the raw Lottie JSON files contain extensive invariant structural metadata and formatting tokens, posing significant challenges for learning vector animation generation. Therefore, we introduce a well designed Lottie tokenizer that transforms JSON files into structured sequences of commands and parameters representing shapes, animation functions and control parameters. Such tokenizer enables us to build OmniLottie upon pretrained vision language models to follow multi-modal interleaved instructions and generate high quality vector animations. To further advance research in vector animation generation, we curate MMLottie-2M, a large scale dataset of professionally designed vector animations paired with textual and visual annotations. With extensive experiments, we validate that OmniLottie can produce vivid and semantically aligned vector animations that adhere closely to multi modal human instructions.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for flexible, high-quality vector animation generation from multi-modal instructions, OmniLottie introduces a specialized Lottie tokenizer that strips away redundant structural metadata from raw Lottie JSON files, converting them into structured command-parameter sequences. This enables the framework to leverage pretrained vision-language models to interpret interleaved textual and visual prompts and generate precise vector animations. Experiments demonstrate that OmniLottie produces semantically accurate, visually vivid animations that closely match human instructions, validated using the newly curated MMLottie-2M dataset of professionally annotated animations.
为实现从多模态指令生成高质量矢量动画，OmniLottie提出一种参数化Lottie分词器，将原始Lottie JSON文件中的冗余结构元数据去除，转化为结构化的命令-参数序列，从而支持预训练视觉-语言模型理解交错的文本与视觉指令并生成语义一致的动画。实验表明，OmniLottie能生成生动且符合指令的矢量动画，其效果经由新构建的200万样本数据集MMLottie-2M验证，该数据集包含专业动画及其多模态标注。
Using ChatGPT for Data Science Analyses
Authors: Ozan Evkaya, Miguel de Carvalho
Venue: Harvard Data Science Review, 8(1) (2026)
First: 2024-04-12T13:57:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:58:41+00:00

Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As a result of recent advancements in generative AI, the field of data science is prone to various changes. The way practitioners construct their data science workflows is now irreversibly shaped by recent advancements, particularly by tools like OpenAI's Data Analysis plugin. While it offers powerful support as a quantitative co-pilot, its limitations demand careful consideration in empirical analysis. This paper assesses the potential of ChatGPT for data science analyses, illustrating its capabilities for data exploration and visualization, as well as for commonly used supervised and unsupervised modeling tasks. While we focus here on how the Data Analysis plugin can serve as co-pilot for Data Science workflows, its broader potential for automation is implicit throughout.

NextAds: Towards Next-generation Personalized Video Advertising
Authors: Yiyan Xu, Ruoxuan Xia, Wuqiang Zheng, Fengbin Zhu, Wenjie Wang, Fuli Feng
First: 2026-03-02T17:58:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:58:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid growth of online video consumption, video advertising has become increasingly dominant in the digital advertising landscape. Yet diverse users and viewing contexts makes one-size-fits-all ad creatives insufficient for consistent effectiveness, underlining the importance of personalization. In practice, most personalized video advertising systems follow a retrieval-based paradigm, selecting the optimal one from a small set of professionally pre-produced creatives for each user. Such static and finite inventories limits both the granularity and the timeliness of personalization, and prevents the creatives from being continuously refined based on online user feedback. Recent advances in generative AI make it possible to move beyond retrieval toward optimizing video creatives in a continuous space at serving time. In this light, we propose NextAds, a generation-based paradigm for next-generation personalized video advertising, and conceptualize NextAds with four core components. To enable comparable research progress, we formulate two representative tasks: personalized creative generation and personalized creative integration, and introduce corresponding lightweight benchmarks. To assess feasibility, we instantiate end-to-end pipelines for both tasks and conduct initial exploratory experiments, demonstrating that GenAI can generate and integrate personalized creatives with encouraging performance. Moreover, we discuss the key challenges and opportunities under this paradigm, aiming to provide actionable insights for both researchers and practitioners and to catalyze progress in personalized video advertising.

Initial experiments show that generative models can produce and integrate personalized ads with promising performance, suggesting feasibility while also highlighting key challenges such as scalability and feedback integration.
为应对用户多样性与观看场景变化对广告效果的影响，NextAds提出基于生成式AI的下一代个性化视频广告范式，突破传统检索式系统局限。该方法包含四大核心组件，围绕两个基准任务——个性化创意生成与整合，构建端到端实验流程。初步实验表明，生成式AI可有效生成并整合个性化视频内容，性能表现令人鼓舞，同时揭示了规模化与反馈机制等关键挑战。
MuFlex: A Scalable, Physics-based Platform for Multi-Building Flexibility Analysis and Coordination
Authors: Ziyan Wu, Ivan Korolija, Rui Tang
First: 2025-08-19T05:44:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:55:58+00:00
Comments: The platform is released open-source on GitHub: https://github.com/BuildNexusX/MuFlex
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
With the increasing penetration of renewable generation on the power grid, maintaining system balance requires coordinated demand flexibility from aggregations of buildings. Reinforcement learning has been widely explored for building controls because of its model-free nature. Open-source simulation testbeds are essential not only for training RL agents but also for fairly benchmarking control strategies. However, most building-sector testbeds target single buildings; multi-building platforms are relatively limited and typically rely on simplified models (e.g., Resistance-Capacitance) or data-driven approaches, which lack the ability to fully capture the physical intricacies and intermediate variables necessary for interpreting control performance. Moreover, these platforms often impose fixed inputs, outputs, and model formats, restricting their applicability as benchmarking tools across diverse control scenarios. To address these gaps, MuFlex, a scalable, open-source platform for multi-building flexibility coordination, was developed. MuFlex enables synchronous information exchange and co-simulation across multiple detailed building models programmed in EnergyPlus and Modelica, and adheres to the latest OpenAI Gym interface, providing a modular, standardized RL implementation. The platform's physics-based capabilities and workflow were demonstrated in a case study coordinating demand flexibility across four office buildings using the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm. The results show that under four buildings' coordination, SAC effectively reduced the aggregated peak demand by nearly 12% with maintained indoor comfort to ensure the power demand below the threshold. Additionally, the platform's scalability was investigated through computational benchmarking on building clusters with varying sizes, model types, and simulation programs.

OnlineX: Unified Online 3D Reconstruction and Understanding with Active-to-Stable State Evolution
Authors: Chong Xia, Fangfu Liu, Yule Wang, Yize Pang, Yueqi Duan
First: 2026-03-02T17:52:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:52:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in generalizable 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled rapid 3D scene reconstruction within seconds, eliminating the need for per-scene optimization. However, existing methods primarily follow an offline reconstruction paradigm, lacking the capacity for continuous reconstruction, which limits their applicability to online scenarios such as robotics and VR/AR. In this paper, we introduce OnlineX, a feed-forward framework that reconstructs both 3D visual appearance and language fields in an online manner using only streaming images. A key challenge in online formulation is the cumulative drift issue, which is rooted in the fundamental conflict between two opposing roles of the memory state: an active role that constantly refreshes to capture high-frequency local geometry, and a stable role that conservatively accumulates and preserves the long-term global structure. To address this, we introduce a decoupled active-to-stable state evolution paradigm. Our framework decouples the memory state into a dedicated active state and a persistent stable state, and then cohesively fuses the information from the former into the latter to achieve both fidelity and stability. Moreover, we jointly model visual appearance and language fields and incorporate an implicit Gaussian fusion module to enhance reconstruction quality. Experiments on mainstream datasets demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms prior work in novel view synthesis and semantic understanding, showcasing robust performance across input sequences of varying lengths with real-time inference speed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OnlineX：基于主动到稳定状态演化的统一在线3D重建与理解
近期通用3D高斯点绘（3DGS）的进展实现了秒级3D场景重建，无需逐场景优化。然而现有方法主要遵循离线重建范式，缺乏连续重建能力，限制其在机器人、VR/AR等在线场景中的应用。本文提出OnlineX，一种前馈框架，仅利用流式图像在线重建3D视觉外观与语言场。在线建模的关键挑战是累积漂移问题，源于记忆状态的双重矛盾角色：主动角色持续刷新以捕捉高频局部几何，稳定角色保守累积并保留长期全局结构。为此，我们引入解耦的主动到稳定状态演化范式，将记忆状态解耦为专用主动状态与持久稳定状态，并将前者信息融合至后者，实现保真与稳定兼顾。此外，我们联合建模视觉外观与语言场，引入隐式高斯融合模块以提升重建质量。主流数据集实验表明，本方法在新视角合成与语义理解上持续优于现有方法，且在不同长度输入序列上均具备实时推理速度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for continuous 3D reconstruction in real-time applications like robotics and VR/AR, OnlineX introduces a feed-forward framework that reconstructs 3D visual and language fields from streaming images without per-scene optimization. To tackle cumulative drift caused by conflicting roles of memory states—active (refreshing local geometry) and stable (preserving global structure)—it decouples them into separate states and fuses active updates into the stable state for both fidelity and stability. The method also jointly models visual and language fields with an implicit Gaussian fusion module to improve reconstruction quality. Experimental results across mainstream datasets show OnlineX outperforms prior methods in novel view synthesis and semantic understanding, maintaining real-time inference even with variable-length input sequences.
为满足机器人和VR/AR等实时场景中持续3D重建的需求，OnlineX提出一种前馈框架，仅通过流式图像在线重建视觉与语言场，无需逐场景优化。为解决在线设置中的累积漂移问题，该方法将记忆状态解耦为负责捕捉局部几何的活跃状态与负责保留全局结构的稳定状态，并将二者融合。同时，它联合建模视觉与语言场，引入隐式高斯融合模块以提升重建质量。实验表明，OnlineX在新视角合成与语义理解任务上持续优于现有方法，且在不同长度输入序列下仍保持实时推理速度。
SimRecon: SimReady Compositional Scene Reconstruction from Real Videos
Authors: Chong Xia, Kai Zhu, Zizhuo Wang, Fangfu Liu, Zhizheng Zhang, Yueqi Duan
First: 2026-03-02T17:51:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:51:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Compositional scene reconstruction seeks to create object-centric representations rather than holistic scenes from real-world videos, which is natively applicable for simulation and interaction. Conventional compositional reconstruction approaches primarily emphasize on visual appearance and show limited generalization ability to real-world scenarios. In this paper, we propose SimRecon, a framework that realizes a "Perception-Generation-Simulation" pipeline towards cluttered scene reconstruction, which first conducts scene-level semantic reconstruction from video input, then performs single-object generation, and finally assembles these assets in the simulator. However, naively combining these three stages leads to visual infidelity of generated assets and physical implausibility of the final scene, a problem particularly severe for complex scenes. Thus, we further propose two bridging modules between the three stages to address this problem. To be specific, for the transition from Perception to Generation, critical for visual fidelity, we introduce Active Viewpoint Optimization, which actively searches in 3D space to acquire optimal projected images as conditions for single-object completion. Moreover, for the transition from Generation to Simulation, essential for physical plausibility, we propose a Scene Graph Synthesizer, which guides the construction from scratch in 3D simulators, mirroring the native, constructive principle of the real world. Extensive experiments on the ScanNet dataset validate our method's superior performance over previous state-of-the-art approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SimRecon：从真实视频中实现可模拟的组合场景重建
组合场景重建旨在从真实视频中生成以物体为中心的表示，而非整体场景，这天然适用于模拟与交互。传统组合重建方法主要关注视觉外观，对真实世界场景的泛化能力有限。本文提出SimRecon框架，实现“感知-生成-模拟”流程，首先从视频输入进行场景级语义重建，然后进行单物体生成，最后在模拟器中组装这些资产。然而，直接组合这三个阶段会导致生成资产视觉失真、最终场景物理不真实，尤其在复杂场景中问题严重。为此，我们进一步提出两个连接三个阶段的桥接模块：在感知到生成阶段，为提升视觉保真度，引入主动视角优化模块，主动在3D空间中搜索最优投影图像作为单物体生成条件；在生成到模拟阶段，为确保物理合理性，提出场景图合成器，指导在3D模拟器中从零构建，模拟真实世界固有的构造原则。在ScanNet数据集上的大量实验验证了本方法优于现有最先进方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for object-centric scene representations suitable for simulation and interaction, this paper introduces SimRecon, a "Perception-Generation-Simulation" pipeline for cluttered scene reconstruction from real videos. The method first reconstructs scene semantics, then generates individual objects, and finally assembles them in a simulator, but suffers from visual and physical inconsistencies. To resolve this, it adds two bridging modules: Active Viewpoint Optimization to improve visual fidelity during perception-to-generation, and a Scene Graph Synthesizer to ensure physical plausibility during generation-to-simulation. Experiments on ScanNet show SimRecon outperforms prior methods in reconstruction quality and simulation realism.
为实现适用于仿真与交互的以物体为中心的场景重建，本文提出SimRecon框架，包含感知-生成-仿真三阶段流程。该方法先进行场景语义重建，再生成单个物体，最后在模拟器中组装，但存在视觉失真与物理不合理的缺陷。为此引入两个桥接模块：主动视角优化模块通过在3D空间中搜索最优投影图像提升视觉保真度，场景图合成器则从零构建物理合理场景以匹配真实世界构造原则。ScanNet数据集上的实验表明，SimRecon在重建质量与仿真兼容性上优于现有方法。
A Randomized Linearly Convergent Frank-Wolfe-type Method for Smooth Convex Minimization over the Spectrahedron
Authors: Dan Garber
First: 2025-03-03T11:46:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:47:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Mathematical Programming SERIES A
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of minimizing a smooth and convex function over the $n$-dimensional spectrahedron -- the set of real symmetric $n\times n$ positive semidefinite matrices with unit trace, which underlies numerous applications in statistics, machine learning and additional domains. Standard first-order methods often require high-rank matrix computations which are prohibitive when the dimension $n$ is large. The well-known Frank-Wolfe method on the other hand only requires efficient rank-one matrix computations, however, suffers from worst-case slow convergence, even under conditions that enable linear convergence rates for standard methods. In this work we present the first Frank-Wolfe-based algorithm that only applies efficient rank-one matrix computations and, assuming quadratic growth and strict complementarity conditions, is guaranteed, after a finite number of iterations, to converge linearly, in expectation, and independently of the ambient dimension.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于谱多面体上光滑凸函数最小化的随机线性收敛Frank-Wolfe型方法
我们考虑在n维谱多面体（即具有单位迹的n×n实对称半正定矩阵集合）上最小化一个光滑凸函数的问题，该问题在统计学、机器学习等领域有广泛应用。标准一阶方法通常需要高阶矩阵计算，当维度n较大时计算代价高昂。而众所周知的Frank-Wolfe方法仅需高效的秩一矩阵计算，但其在最坏情况下收敛缓慢，即使在标准方法可实现线性收敛率的条件下亦如此。本文提出首个仅使用高效秩一矩阵计算的Frank-Wolfe型算法，并在假设二次增长和严格互补条件下，保证在有限次迭代后以期望值线性收敛，且与环境维度无关。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency of standard first-order methods for minimizing smooth convex functions over the spectrahedron — a set of positive semidefinite matrices with unit trace — this work introduces a Frank-Wolfe-type algorithm that avoids high-rank matrix operations by relying only on rank-one updates. Under assumptions of quadratic growth and strict complementarity, the method guarantees linear convergence in expectation after a finite number of iterations, without dependence on the ambient dimension, thereby resolving the known slow convergence of Frank-Wolfe methods in this setting.
为了解决在谱多面体（单位迹的正半定矩阵集合）上最小化光滑凸函数时，标准一阶方法计算高阶矩阵效率低的问题，本文提出一种基于Frank-Wolfe的算法，仅需进行秩一矩阵运算。在满足二次增长和严格互补性条件下，该算法能在有限步内以期望值实现线性收敛，且收敛速度与维度无关，从而克服了Frank-Wolfe方法在此类问题中收敛缓慢的缺陷。
Stereo-Inertial Poser: Towards Metric-Accurate Shape-Aware Motion Capture Using Sparse IMUs and a Single Stereo Camera
Authors: Tutian Tang, Xingyu Ji, Yutong Li, MingHao Liu, Wenqiang Xu, Cewu Lu
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:46:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:46:38+00:00
Comments: The code, data, and supplementary materials are available at \url{https://sites.google.com/view/stereo-inertial-poser}. Accepted to ICRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Recent advancements in visual-inertial motion capture systems have demonstrated the potential of combining monocular cameras with sparse inertial measurement units (IMUs) as cost-effective solutions, which effectively mitigate occlusion and drift issues inherent in single-modality systems. However, they are still limited by metric inaccuracies in global translations stemming from monocular depth ambiguity, and shape-agnostic local motion estimations that ignore anthropometric variations. We present Stereo-Inertial Poser, a real-time motion capture system that leverages a single stereo camera and six IMUs to estimate metric-accurate and shape-aware 3D human motion. By replacing the monocular RGB with stereo vision, our system resolves depth ambiguity through calibrated baseline geometry, enabling direct 3D keypoint extraction and body shape parameter estimation. IMU data and visual cues are fused for predicting drift-compensated joint positions and root movements, while a novel shape-aware fusion module dynamically harmonizes anthropometry variations with global translations. Our end-to-end pipeline achieves over 200 FPS without optimization-based post-processing, enabling real-time deployment. Quantitative evaluations across various datasets demonstrate state-of-the-art performance. Qualitative results show our method produces drift-free global translation under a long recording time and reduces foot-skating effects.
中文标题/摘要
标题：立体惯性姿态捕捉系统：利用稀疏IMU与单目立体相机实现度量精确且形状感知的运动捕捉
近期视觉惯性运动捕捉系统的进展表明，结合单目相机与稀疏惯性测量单元（IMU）可作为成本效益高的解决方案，有效缓解单一模态系统固有的遮挡与漂移问题。然而，其仍受限于单目深度模糊导致的全局平移度量不准确，以及忽略人体解剖学差异的形状无关局部运动估计。我们提出Stereo-Inertial Poser，一种实时运动捕捉系统，利用单目立体相机与六个IMU，实现度量精确且形状感知的3D人体运动估计。通过将单目RGB替换为立体视觉，系统借助校准基线几何结构解决深度模糊问题，实现直接3D关键点提取与身体形状参数估计。IMU数据与视觉线索融合用于预测漂移补偿的关节位置与根部运动，同时引入新颖的形状感知融合模块，动态协调人体解剖学差异与全局平移。端到端流程无需优化后处理即可达到200 FPS以上，支持实时部署。多数据集定量评估显示其达到最先进性能，定性结果表明该方法在长时间录制中实现无漂移的全局平移，并减少脚部滑动效应。

Experiments show the system achieves over 200 FPS without post-processing, outperforms existing methods quantitatively, and eliminates drift and foot-skating artifacts in long-duration recordings.
为实现无需昂贵传感器的高精度、人体形状感知的运动捕捉，该研究提出Stereo-Inertial Poser系统，结合单目立体相机与六个稀疏IMU。通过立体视觉替代单目图像，利用校准几何基线消除深度歧义，直接提取3D关键点并估计身体形状。视觉与IMU数据融合预测补偿漂移的关节位置与根部运动，创新的形状感知融合模块动态协调人体形态与全局位移。端到端流程无需后处理，帧率超200FPS，量化评估达到最先进水平，定性结果显示长时录制下全局位移无漂移、脚部滑动现象显著减少。
LiftAvatar: Kinematic-Space Completion for Expression-Controlled 3D Gaussian Avatar Animation
Authors: Hualiang Wei, Shunran Jia, Jialun Liu, Wenhui Li
First: 2026-03-02T17:46:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:46:32+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present LiftAvatar, a new paradigm that completes sparse monocular observations in kinematic space (e.g., facial expressions and head pose) and uses the completed signals to drive high-fidelity avatar animation. LiftAvatar is a fine-grained, expression-controllable large-scale video diffusion Transformer that synthesizes high-quality, temporally coherent expression sequences conditioned on single or multiple reference images. The key idea is to lift incomplete input data into a richer kinematic representation, thereby strengthening both reconstruction and animation in downstream 3D avatar pipelines. To this end, we introduce (i) a multi-granularity expression control scheme that combines shading maps with expression coefficients for precise and stable driving, and (ii) a multi-reference conditioning mechanism that aggregates complementary cues from multiple frames, enabling strong 3D consistency and controllability. As a plug-and-play enhancer, LiftAvatar directly addresses the limited expressiveness and reconstruction artifacts of 3D Gaussian Splatting-based avatars caused by sparse kinematic cues in everyday monocular videos. By expanding incomplete observations into diverse pose-expression variations, LiftAvatar also enables effective prior distillation from large-scale video generative models into 3D pipelines, leading to substantial gains. Extensive experiments show that LiftAvatar consistently boosts animation quality and quantitative metrics of state-of-the-art 3D avatar methods, especially under extreme, unseen expressions.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limited expressiveness and reconstruction artifacts in 3D Gaussian Splatting avatars due to sparse monocular kinematic cues, LiftAvatar introduces a fine-grained video diffusion Transformer that completes sparse facial and head pose observations in kinematic space and drives high-fidelity avatar animation. It employs a multi-granularity expression control scheme combining shading maps and expression coefficients for stable driving, and a multi-reference conditioning mechanism that aggregates cues from multiple frames to ensure 3D consistency. Experimental results show LiftAvatar significantly improves animation quality and quantitative metrics across state-of-the-art 3D avatar methods, especially under extreme or unseen expressions, by effectively distilling priors from large-scale video generative models into 3D pipelines.
为了解决3D高斯点渲染头像因稀疏单目运动线索导致的表达能力不足和重建伪影问题，LiftAvatar提出一种细粒度视频扩散Transformer，将稀疏的面部与头部姿态观测在运动空间中完成，并驱动高保真头像动画。其采用结合着色图与表情系数的多粒度表情控制机制以实现稳定驱动，以及聚合多帧互补线索的多参考条件机制以确保三维一致性。实验表明，LiftAvatar显著提升主流3D头像方法的动画质量与量化指标，尤其在极端或未见表情下表现突出，通过从大规模视频生成模型中有效蒸馏先验知识至三维管线实现性能跃升。
LLMs as Strategic Actors: Behavioral Alignment, Risk Calibration, and Argumentation Framing in Geopolitical Simulations
Authors: Veronika Solopova, Viktoria Skorik, Maksym Tereshchenko, Alina Haidun, Ostap Vykhopen
First: 2026-03-02T17:46:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:46:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly proposed as agents in strategic decision environments, yet their behavior in structured geopolitical simulations remains under-researched. We evaluate six popular state-of-the-art LLMs alongside results from human results across four real-world crisis simulation scenarios, requiring models to select predefined actions and justify their decisions across multiple rounds. We compare models to humans in action alignment, risk calibration through chosen actions' severity, and argumentative framing grounded in international relations theory. Results show that models approximate human decision patterns in base simulation rounds but diverge over time, displaying distinct behavioural profiles and strategy updates. LLM explanations for chosen actions across all models exhibit a strong normative-cooperative framing centered on stability, coordination, and risk mitigation, with limited adversarial reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型作为战略行动者：地缘政治模拟中的行为对齐、风险校准与论证框架
大语言模型（LLMs）日益被提议作为战略决策环境中的代理，但其在结构化地缘政治模拟中的行为仍缺乏研究。我们评估了六种流行且先进的LLMs，并与人类在四个现实世界危机模拟场景中的表现进行对比，要求模型在多轮中选择预定义行动并说明决策理由。我们从行动对齐、通过所选行动严重性进行的风险校准，以及基于国际关系理论的论证框架三个方面，比较模型与人类的表现。结果显示，模型在基础模拟轮次中近似人类决策模式，但随着时间推移出现分歧，展现出不同的行为特征和策略更新。所有模型对所选行动的解释均表现出强烈的规范性合作框架，聚焦于稳定、协调与风险缓解，且缺乏对抗性推理。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how large language models behave in strategic geopolitical simulations, this study evaluates six state-of-the-art LLMs against human participants across four crisis scenarios, requiring them to select actions and justify decisions over multiple rounds. The researchers assess alignment with human behavior, risk calibration through action severity, and argumentative framing using international relations theory. Results indicate that LLMs initially mimic human decision patterns but diverge over time, exhibiting distinct strategic profiles. Their justifications consistently emphasize normative, cooperative, and risk-mitigating frames, with minimal adversarial reasoning.
为理解大语言模型在地缘政治模拟中的行为，本研究评估了六种主流大语言模型与人类参与者在四个危机场景中的表现，要求模型选择行动并多轮解释决策。研究从行为一致性、行动严重性所反映的风险校准及国际关系理论框架下的论证方式三方面进行比较。结果表明，模型初期模仿人类决策模式，但随时间推移出现明显分化，展现出独特策略特征；其解释普遍强调规范性、合作性与风险规避，缺乏对抗性思维。
A 3D mesh convolution-based autoencoder for geometry compression
Authors: Germain Bregeon, Marius Preda, Radu Ispas, Titus Zaharia
First: 2026-03-02T17:42:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:42:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In this paper, we introduce a novel 3D mesh convolution-based autoencoder for geometry compression, able to deal with irregular mesh data without requiring neither preprocessing nor manifold/watertightness conditions. The proposed approach extracts meaningful latent representations by learning features directly from the mesh faces, while preserving connectivity through dedicated pooling and unpooling operations. The encoder compresses the input mesh into a compact base mesh space, which ensures that the latent space remains comparable. The decoder reconstructs the original connectivity and restores the compressed geometry to its full resolution. Extensive experiments on multi-class datasets demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art approaches in both 3D mesh geometry reconstruction and latent space classification tasks. Code available at: github.com/germainGB/MeshConv3D
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于3D网格卷积的自编码器用于几何压缩

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient geometry compression without preprocessing or manifold constraints, this paper proposes a 3D mesh convolution-based autoencoder that directly learns features from mesh faces while preserving connectivity via specialized pooling and unpooling. The encoder compresses input meshes into a compact latent space, and the decoder reconstructs both connectivity and geometry at full resolution. Experimental results across multi-class datasets show superior performance over existing methods in both 3D mesh reconstruction and latent space classification tasks.
为实现无需预处理或流形条件的高效几何压缩，本文提出一种基于3D网格卷积的自编码器，直接从网格面学习特征并借助专用池化与上采样操作保持拓扑结构。编码器将输入网格压缩至紧凑的潜在空间，解码器重建拓扑并恢复高分辨率几何。在多类别数据集上的实验表明，该方法在3D网格重建与潜在空间分类任务上均优于现有方法。
Nano-EmoX: Unifying Multimodal Emotional Intelligence from Perception to Empathy
Authors: Jiahao Huang, Fengyan Lin, Xuechao Yang, Chen Feng, Kexin Zhu, Xu Yang, Zhide Chen
First: 2026-03-02T17:42:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:42:33+00:00
Comments: 17 pages,8 figures, The IEEE/CVF Conference on Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The development of affective multimodal language models (MLMs) has long been constrained by a gap between low-level perception and high-level interaction, leading to fragmented affective capabilities and limited generalization. To bridge this gap, we propose a cognitively inspired three-level hierarchy that organizes affective tasks according to their cognitive depth-perception, understanding, and interaction-and provides a unified conceptual foundation for advancing affective modeling. Guided by this hierarchy, we introduce Nano-EmoX, a small-scale multitask MLM, and P2E (Perception-to-Empathy), a curriculum-based training framework. Nano-EmoX integrates a suite of omni-modal encoders, including an enhanced facial encoder and a fusion encoder, to capture key multimodal affective cues and improve cross-task transferability. The outputs are projected into a unified language space via heterogeneous adapters, empowering a lightweight language model to tackle diverse affective tasks. Concurrently, P2E progressively cultivates emotional intelligence by aligning rapid perception with chain-of-thought-driven empathy. To the best of our knowledge, Nano-EmoX is the first compact MLM (2.2B) to unify six core affective tasks across all three hierarchy levels, achieving state-of-the-art or highly competitive performance across multiple benchmarks, demonstrating excellent efficiency and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Nano-EmoX：从感知到共情的多模态情感智能统一框架
情感多模态语言模型（MLM）的发展长期受限于低层感知与高层交互之间的鸿沟，导致情感能力碎片化且泛化能力有限。为弥合此鸿沟，我们提出一种受认知启发的三级层次结构，按认知深度（感知、理解、交互）组织情感任务，并提供统一的概念基础以推进情感建模。基于此层次结构，我们引入了小型多任务MLM Nano-EmoX及基于课程的训练框架P2E（感知到共情）。Nano-EmoX整合了多种全模态编码器（含增强型面部编码器与融合编码器），以捕捉关键多模态情感线索并提升跨任务迁移能力；其输出通过异构适配器投影至统一语言空间，使轻量级语言模型可处理多样情感任务。同时，P2E通过将快速感知与思维链驱动的共情对齐，逐步培养情感智能。据我们所知，Nano-EmoX是首个统一三级层次结构六大核心情感任务的紧凑型MLM（2.2B参数），在多个基准测试中取得最先进或高度竞争力的表现，展现出卓越的效率与泛化能力。

Motivated by the fragmentation in affective multimodal language models due to a disconnect between perception and high-level interaction, the authors propose Nano-EmoX, a small-scale multitask model, and P2E, a curriculum-driven training framework, to unify emotional intelligence across cognitive levels. Nano-EmoX integrates enhanced facial and fusion encoders with heterogeneous adapters to project multimodal affective cues into a shared language space, enabling efficient task transfer. P2E progressively trains the model from rapid perception to empathetic reasoning. Experimental results show Nano-EmoX, at 2.2B parameters, achieves state-of-the-art or competitive performance on six core affective tasks across all three cognitive levels, demonstrating strong generalization and efficiency.
为弥合多模态情感语言模型中感知与高级交互之间的断层，作者提出Nano-EmoX模型与P2E训练框架，统一构建从感知到共情的情感智能体系。Nano-EmoX融合增强型面部编码器与融合编码器，通过异构适配器将多模态情感线索映射至统一语言空间，提升跨任务迁移能力；P2E框架通过课程式训练逐步从快速感知过渡到共情推理。实验表明，该2.2B参数模型在六个核心情感任务上达到当前最优或领先水平，展现出优异的泛化能力与效率。
Pencil Puzzle Bench: A Benchmark for Multi-Step Verifiable Reasoning
Authors: Justin Waugh
First: 2026-03-02T17:40:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:40:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Pencil Puzzle Bench, a framework for evaluating large language model reasoning through pencil puzzles, a family of constraint-satisfaction problems closely related to NP-complete problems, with deterministic, step-level verification. From a database of 62,231 puzzles across 94 varieties with verified unique solutions, we select a benchmark of 300 puzzles spanning 20 varieties and evaluate 51 models from 11 providers in two modes: direct ask (single-shot) and agentic (multi-turn with iterative verification). A key differentiator of our benchmark is that every intermediate board state can be checked against variety-specific constraints, localizing errors to the exact rule violated, providing the infrastructure for dense, per-move reward signals for process supervision and reinforcement learning. Our evaluation reveals two distinct axes of capability: (1) reasoning effort scaling, where GPT-5.2 improves 81x from no reasoning to maximum effort; and (2) agentic iteration, where Claude Opus 4.6 rises from 0.3% to 30.0% through iterative checking, while GPT-5.2@xhigh improves from 20.2% to 56.0%. Agentic attempts span a median of 29 turns over 17 minutes, with the longest exceeding 1,221 turns and 14.3 hours - a demanding test of long-context utilization, not just reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：铅笔谜题基准：多步可验证推理的评估基准
我们引入铅笔谜题基准，通过铅笔谜题（一类与NP完全问题密切相关、具有确定性、逐步可验证的约束满足问题）评估大语言模型的推理能力。从包含62,231个谜题、94种类型且已验证唯一解的数据库中，我们选取300个覆盖20种类型的谜题，评估11家供应商的51个模型，采用两种模式：直接提问（单次）和代理式（多轮迭代验证）。本基准的关键特点是，每个中间棋盘状态均可根据类型特定约束进行检查，将错误定位到具体违反的规则，为过程监督和强化学习提供密集的逐步奖励信号。 我们的评估揭示了两种能力维度：（1）推理努力的扩展性，GPT-5.2从无推理到最大努力提升81倍；（2）代理式迭代能力，Claude Opus从0.3%提升至30.0%，GPT-5.2@xhigh从20.2%提升至56.0%。代理式尝试平均耗时17分钟、29轮，最长者达1,221轮、14.3小时——不仅是推理能力的考验，更是对长上下文利用能力的严苛检验。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for rigorous, step-by-step evaluation of large language models' reasoning capabilities, the authors introduce Pencil Puzzle Bench, a benchmark based on constraint-satisfaction puzzles with deterministic, verifiable solutions. They curate 300 puzzles from 20 varieties and evaluate 51 models across direct ask and agentic modes, where models can iteratively verify intermediate steps. Results show that reasoning effort scales significantly—GPT-5.2 improves 81x in problem-solving intensity—and agentic iteration dramatically boosts performance, with Claude Opus 4.6 rising from 0.3% to 30.0% and GPT-5.2@xhigh from 20.2% to 56.0%, often requiring dozens to over a thousand turns over hours, highlighting the benchmark’s demand for long-context reasoning and iterative verification.
为评估大语言模型的多步可验证推理能力，作者构建了铅笔谜题基准，基于具有确定性解和逐步可验证性的约束满足类谜题。从62,231道谜题中精选300道，覆盖20种类型，对51个模型在直接问答与代理模式下进行测试，支持按步错误定位。实验发现两大能力维度：推理努力度提升（如GPT-5.2效率提升81倍）与代理迭代能力（如Claude Opus 4.6准确率从0.3%升至30.0%），代理模式平均耗时17分钟、最长达14.3小时，凸显模型在长上下文推理与过程监督上的挑战。
Robometer: Scaling General-Purpose Robotic Reward Models via Trajectory Comparisons
Authors: Anthony Liang, Yigit Korkmaz, Jiahui Zhang, Minyoung Hwang, Abrar Anwar, Sidhant Kaushik, Aditya Shah, Alex S. Huang, Luke Zettlemoyer, Dieter Fox, Yu Xiang, Anqi Li, Andreea Bobu, Abhishek Gupta, Stephen Tu, Erdem Biyik, Jesse Zhang
First: 2026-03-02T17:38:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:38:58+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
General-purpose robot reward models are typically trained to predict absolute task progress from expert demonstrations, providing only local, frame-level supervision. While effective for expert demonstrations, this paradigm scales poorly to large-scale robotics datasets where failed and suboptimal trajectories are abundant and assigning dense progress labels is ambiguous. We introduce Robometer, a scalable reward modeling framework that combines intra-trajectory progress supervision with inter-trajectory preference supervision. Robometer is trained with a dual objective: a frame-level progress loss that anchors reward magnitude on expert data, and a trajectory-comparison preference loss that imposes global ordering constraints across trajectories of the same task, enabling effective learning from both real and augmented failed trajectories. To support this formulation at scale, we curate RBM-1M, a reward-learning dataset comprising over one million trajectories spanning diverse robot embodiments and tasks, including substantial suboptimal and failure data. Across benchmarks and real-world evaluations, Robometer learns more generalizable reward functions than prior methods and improves robot learning performance across a diverse set of downstream applications. Code, model weights, and videos at https://robometer.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Robometer：通过轨迹比较扩展通用机器人奖励模型
通用机器人奖励模型通常通过专家演示训练以预测绝对任务进度，仅提供局部、帧级监督。虽然对专家演示有效，但该范式在大规模机器人数据集中扩展性差，因为失败和次优轨迹大量存在，且分配密集进度标签存在歧义。我们提出Robometer，一种可扩展的奖励建模框架，结合轨迹内进度监督与轨迹间偏好监督。Robometer采用双重目标训练：帧级进度损失将奖励幅度锚定在专家数据上，轨迹比较偏好损失则在相同任务的轨迹间施加全局排序约束，从而有效从真实和增强的失败轨迹中学习。为支持大规模实现，我们构建了RBM-1M数据集，包含超过一百万条轨迹，涵盖多样化的机器人形态和任务，包括大量次优和失败数据。在基准测试和真实世界评估中，Robometer学习到比先前方法更通用的奖励函数，并在多种下游应用中提升机器人学习性能。代码、模型权重和视频见https://robometer.github.io/。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of frame-level reward modeling for large-scale robotics datasets, Robometer introduces a scalable framework combining intra-trajectory progress supervision with inter-trajectory preference learning. It trains a dual-objective model: a frame-level loss anchored to expert demonstrations and a trajectory-comparison loss enforcing global ordering across diverse trajectories, including failures. Evaluated on benchmarks and real-world tasks, Robometer learns more generalizable reward functions and consistently improves downstream robot learning performance compared to prior methods.
为解决大规模机器人数据集中帧级奖励建模效率低的问题，Robometer提出结合轨迹内进度监督与轨迹间偏好监督的可扩展框架。其采用双目标训练：帧级损失锚定专家演示，轨迹比较损失强制相同任务轨迹间全局排序，有效利用真实与增强失败轨迹。在多个基准与真实场景评估中，Robometer学习到更泛化的奖励函数，并显著提升下游机器人学习性能。
Real-Time Thermal-Inertial Odometry on Embedded Hardware for High-Speed GPS-Denied Flight
Authors: Austin Stone, Mark Petersen, Cammy Peterson
First: 2026-03-02T17:38:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:38:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a real-time monocular thermal-inertial odometry system designed for high-velocity, GPS-denied flight on embedded hardware. The system fuses measurements from a FLIR Boson+ 640 longwave infrared camera, a high-rate IMU, a laser range finder, a barometer, and a magnetometer within a fixed-lag factor graph. To sustain reliable feature tracks under motion blur, low contrast, and rapid viewpoint changes, we employ a lightweight thermal-optimized front-end with multi-stage feature filtering. Laser range finder measurements provide per-feature depth priors that stabilize scale during weakly observable motion. High-rate inertial data is first pre-filtered using a Chebyshev Type II infinite impulse response (IIR) filter and then preintegrated, improving robustness to airframe vibrations during aggressive maneuvers. To address barometric altitude errors induced at high airspeeds, we train an uncertainty-aware gated recurrent unit (GRU) network that models the temporal dynamics of static pressure distortion, outperforming polynomial and multi-layer perceptron (MLP) baselines. Integrated on an NVIDIA Jetson Xavier NX, the complete system supports closed-loop quadrotor flight at 30 m/s with drift under 2% over kilometer-scale trajectories. These contributions expand the operational envelope of thermal-inertial navigation, enabling reliable high-speed flight in visually degraded and GPS-denied environments.
中文标题/摘要

我们提出了一种专为嵌入式硬件设计的实时单目热惯性里程计系统，适用于高速、GPS拒止飞行。该系统在固定滞后因子图中融合了FLIR Boson+ 640长波红外相机、高采样率IMU、激光测距仪、气压计和磁力计的测量数据。为在运动模糊、低对比度和快速视角变化条件下维持可靠的特征轨迹，我们采用轻量级热优化前端并结合多阶段特征滤波。激光测距仪测量提供每个特征的深度先验，稳定弱可观测运动期间的尺度。高采样率惯性数据首先通过切比雪夫II型无限脉冲响应（IIR）滤波器预滤波，再进行预积分，从而增强在剧烈机动中对机身振动的鲁棒性。为解决高速飞行时气压高度计误差，我们训练了一个不确定性感知门控循环单元（GRU）网络，用于建模静态压力畸变的时序动态，性能优于多项式和多层感知机（MLP）基线模型。该系统集成于NVIDIA Jetson Xavier NX平台，支持30 m/s闭合环路四旋翼飞行，在千米级轨迹中漂移小于2%。这些贡献扩展了热惯性导航的操作范围，实现了在视觉退化和GPS拒止环境中的可靠高速飞行。
