Recursive Models for Long-Horizon Reasoning
Authors: Chenxiao Yang, Nathan Srebro, Zhiyuan Li
First: 2026-03-02T17:37:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:37:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern language models reason within bounded context, an inherent constraint that poses a fundamental barrier to long-horizon reasoning. We identify recursion as a core principle for overcoming this barrier, and propose recursive models as a minimal realization, where the model can recursively invoke itself to solve subtasks in isolated contexts. We prove that any computable problem admits a recursive decomposition in which each subtask requires only exponentially smaller active context than standard autoregressive models; this strictly surpasses any context management approach confined to a single sequence, such as summarization. We further generalize our framework to modern agentic systems with arbitrary context processing and control flows, and prove that recursive models can achieve optimal power within this broader class. Experimentally, we train a 3B model to reason recursively and evaluate on Boolean satisfiability, a task requiring long-horizon combinatorial search, where it significantly outperforms frontier LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于长时程推理的递归模型
现代语言模型在有界上下文中进行推理，这是固有的限制，构成了长时程推理的根本障碍。我们识别出递归是克服这一障碍的核心原则，并提出递归模型作为最小实现方式，即模型可递归调用自身以在隔离上下文中解决子任务。我们证明，任何可计算问题都存在一种递归分解，其中每个子任务所需的活跃上下文规模仅为标准自回归模型的指数级更小；这严格优于仅限于单个序列的上下文管理方法，如摘要。我们进一步将框架推广到现代代理系统，支持任意上下文处理和控制流，并证明递归模型在此更广泛类别中可实现最优性能。实验上，我们训练了一个3B模型进行递归推理，并在布尔可满足性任务（需进行长时程组合搜索）上评估，结果显著优于前沿大语言模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inherent limitation of modern language models in handling long-horizon reasoning due to bounded context, the paper proposes recursive models that enable self-invocation to solve subtasks in isolated contexts. The method formally proves that any computable problem can be decomposed recursively such that each subtask requires exponentially less active context than standard autoregressive models, surpassing single-sequence context management techniques. Experiments show that a 3B recursive model significantly outperforms frontier LLMs on Boolean satisfiability, a task demanding long-horizon combinatorial search, demonstrating the efficacy of recursive decomposition.
鉴于现代语言模型因上下文受限难以进行长程推理，本文提出递归模型，通过自我调用在隔离上下文中解决子任务以突破此限制。方法证明任何可计算问题均可递归分解，使每个子任务所需活跃上下文呈指数级小于标准自回归模型，超越单序列上下文管理方法。实验表明，3B规模的递归模型在需要长程组合搜索的布尔可满足性任务上显著优于前沿大语言模型，验证了递归分解在复杂推理中的有效性。
SPARE: Single-Pass Annotation with Reference-Guided Evaluation for Automatic Process Supervision and Reward Modelling
Authors: Md Imbesat Hassan Rizvi, Xiaodan Zhu, Iryna Gurevych
Venue: AAAI 2026 Oral
First: 2025-06-18T14:37:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:34:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted to AAAI 2026 (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Process or step-wise supervision has played a crucial role in advancing complex multi-step reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, efficient, high-quality automated process annotation remains a significant challenge. To address this, we introduce Single-Pass Annotation with Reference-Guided Evaluation (SPARE), a novel structured framework that enables efficient per-step annotation by jointly aligning solution steps to reference solutions and determine its accuracy with explicit reasoning in single generation. We demonstrate SPARE's effectiveness across four diverse datasets spanning mathematical reasoning (GSM8K, MATH), multi-hop question answering (MuSiQue-Ans), and spatial reasoning (SpaRP), showing consistent improvements in two applications: (1) training Process Reward Models (PRMs) for ranking and aggregating multiple generations, and (2) fine-tuning models via offline reinforcement learning for greedy decoding. On ProcessBench, SPARE demonstrates data-efficient out-of-distribution generalization, using only $\sim$16% of training samples compared to human-labeled and other synthetically trained baselines. Additionally, it achieves competitive performance with MCTS-based methods while offering 2.3$\times$ speedup in terms of total token count. Manual analysis reveals complementary precision-recall characteristics with MCTS approaches, suggesting potential for ensemble methods. These results establish SPARE as a practical and scalable solution for automatic process supervision in LLM reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARE：基于参考引导评估的单次标注框架，用于大语言模型自动过程监督与奖励建模
分步监督在提升大语言模型（LLMs）复杂多步推理能力方面发挥了关键作用。然而，高效且高质量的自动化过程标注仍是一个重大挑战。为此，我们提出了单次标注与参考引导评估（SPARE），一种新颖的结构化框架，通过联合对齐解题步骤与参考解，并在单次生成中显式推理以确定其准确性，实现高效逐步标注。我们在四个多样化的数据集（数学推理：GSM8K、MATH；多跳问答：MuSiQue-Ans；空间推理：SpaRP）上验证了SPARE的有效性，展示了其在两项应用中的持续改进：（1）训练过程奖励模型（PRMs）以排序和聚合多个生成结果；（2）通过离线强化学习微调模型以实现贪心解码。在ProcessBench上，SPARE仅使用约16%的训练样本，即实现了优于人工标注及其他合成训练基线的数据高效分布外泛化能力。此外，SPARE在性能上与基于MCTS的方法具有竞争力，同时总token数方面快2.3倍。人工分析显示，其与MCTS方法在精确率-召回率特性上互补，暗示可结合使用。这些结果确立了SPARE作为大语言模型推理中自动过程监督的实用且可扩展解决方案。

Motivated by the need for efficient, high-quality automated annotation of step-wise reasoning in LLMs, SPARE introduces a single-pass framework that jointly aligns generated solution steps with reference solutions and evaluates their correctness through explicit reasoning in one generation. Evaluated across four datasets including GSM8K, MATH, MuSiQue-Ans, and SpaRP, SPARE consistently improves performance in two applications: training Process Reward Models for ranking generations and fine-tuning models via offline reinforcement learning. On ProcessBench, it achieves data-efficient out-of-distribution generalization using only ~16% of training samples compared to human-labeled baselines, and matches MCTS-based methods in accuracy while reducing total token usage by 2.3x. Manual analysis shows complementary precision-recall behavior, hinting at potential for ensemble use.
为提升大语言模型的多步推理能力，SPARE提出一种单次生成的结构化框架，通过联合对齐步骤解与参考答案并显式评估其准确性，实现高效自动化过程标注。在GSM8K、MATH、MuSiQue-Ans和SpaRP四个数据集上，SPARE在训练过程奖励模型和离线强化学习微调中均表现更优。在ProcessBench上，仅用约16%训练样本即实现优于人工标注基线的分布外泛化能力，同时在准确率上媲美MCTS方法，但总token消耗减少2.3倍，且与MCTS方法具有互补的精确率-召回率特性，提示可结合使用。
ARCANE -- Early Detection of Interplanetary Coronal Mass Ejections
Authors: H. T. Rüdisser, G. Nguyen, J. Le Louëdec, E. E. Davies, C. Möstl
Venue: Rüdisser, H. T., Nguyen, G., Le Louëdec, J., Davies, E. E., & Möstl, C. (2026). ARCANE--Early detection of Interplanetary Coronal Mass Ejections. Space Weather, 24, e2025SW004537
First: 2025-05-14T13:17:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:33:27+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 10 figures, 1 table, submitted to AGU Space Weather on 14 May 2025, revised 17 October 2025, accepted 01 December 2025, published 23 February 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interplanetary coronal mass ejections (ICMEs) are major drivers of space weather disturbances, posing risks to both technological infrastructure and human activities. Automatic detection of ICMEs in solar wind in situ data is essential for early warning systems. While several methods have been proposed to identify these structures in time series data, robust real-time detection remains a significant challenge. In this work, we present ARCANE - the first framework explicitly designed for early ICME detection in streaming solar wind data under realistic operational constraints, enabling event identification without requiring observation of the full structure. Our approach evaluates the strengths and limitations of detection models by comparing a machine learning-based method to a threshold-based baseline. The ResUNet++ model, previously validated on science data, significantly outperforms the baseline, particularly in detecting high-impact events, while retaining solid performance on lower-impact cases. Notably, we find that using real-time solar wind (RTSW) data instead of high-resolution science data leads to only minimal performance degradation. Despite the challenges of operational settings, our detection pipeline achieves an F1-Score of 0.37, with an average detection delay of 24.5% of the event's duration while processing only a minimal portion of the event data. As more data becomes available, the performance increases significantly. These results mark a substantial step forward in automated space weather monitoring and lay the groundwork for enhanced real-time forecasting capabilities.
Summary / 总结
Driven by the need for early warning of space weather threats from interplanetary coronal mass ejections (ICMEs), this study introduces ARCANE, the first real-time detection framework for ICMEs in streaming solar wind data under operational constraints. It compares a machine learning model (ResUNet++) with a traditional threshold-based method, finding that ResUNet++ significantly outperforms the baseline—especially for high-impact events—while maintaining reasonable accuracy for lower-impact cases. Using real-time solar wind data instead of high-resolution science data causes only minor performance loss. The system achieves an F1-Score of 0.37 with a 24.5% average detection delay, processing only a small portion of event data, and performance improves as more data becomes available.
为应对行星际日冕物质抛射（ICME）对空间天气造成的威胁，本研究提出ARCANE框架，首次实现对流式太阳风数据中ICME的实时早期检测，并满足实际运行约束。该框架对比了机器学习模型（ResUNet++）与传统阈值方法，结果显示ResUNet++在高影响事件检测上显著优于基线，同时在低影响事件上仍保持良好性能。使用实时太阳风数据替代高分辨率科学数据仅导致轻微性能下降。系统在仅处理事件数据一小部分的情况下，实现0.37的F1分数，平均检测延迟为事件时长的24.5%，且随着数据量增加，性能显著提升。
Distributions as Actions: A Unified Framework for Diverse Action Spaces
Authors: Jiamin He, A. Rupam Mahmood, Martha White
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-19T21:19:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:30:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a novel reinforcement learning (RL) framework that treats parameterized action distributions as actions, redefining the boundary between agent and environment. This reparameterization makes the new action space continuous, regardless of the original action type (discrete, continuous, hybrid, etc.). Under this new parameterization, we develop a generalized deterministic policy gradient estimator, Distributions-as-Actions Policy Gradient (DA-PG), which has lower variance than the gradient in the original action space. Although learning the critic over distribution parameters poses new challenges, we introduce Interpolated Critic Learning (ICL), a simple yet effective strategy to enhance learning, supported by insights from bandit settings. Building on TD3, a strong baseline for continuous control, we propose a practical actor-critic algorithm, Distributions-as-Actions Actor-Critic (DA-AC). Empirically, DA-AC achieves competitive performance in various settings across discrete, continuous, and hybrid control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布作为动作：一种统一的多样化动作空间框架
我们提出了一种新颖的强化学习（RL）框架，将参数化动作分布视为动作，重新定义了智能体与环境之间的边界。这种重参数化使新的动作空间无论原始动作类型（离散、连续、混合等）均变为连续。在此新参数化下，我们开发了一种广义确定性策略梯度估计器——分布作为动作策略梯度（DA-PG），其梯度方差低于原始动作空间中的梯度。尽管在分布参数上学习批评器带来了新挑战，我们引入了插值批评器学习（ICL），这是一种简单而有效的策略，通过借鉴多臂老虎机设置的见解加以支持。基于TD3（连续控制领域的强基线），我们提出了一种实用的演员-批评者算法——分布作为动作演员-批评者（DA-AC）。实证表明，DA-AC在离散、连续和混合控制的各种场景中均表现出竞争力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to unify diverse action spaces in reinforcement learning, this work redefines actions as parameterized distributions, enabling a continuous action space regardless of original action type. It introduces DA-PG, a policy gradient estimator with lower variance under this reparameterization, and ICL, a critic learning strategy inspired by bandit theory to address challenges in learning over distribution parameters. Empirically, the resulting DA-AC algorithm, built on TD3, achieves competitive performance across discrete, continuous, and hybrid control tasks.
为统一强化学习中的多样化动作空间，该研究提出将参数化动作分布视为动作，从而构建与原始动作类型无关的连续动作空间。方法上引入了DA-PG，一种方差更低的广义确定性策略梯度估计器，并提出ICL策略，利用多臂老虎机理论提升分布参数化批评者的训练效果。实验表明，基于TD3构建的DA-AC算法在离散、连续及混合控制任务中均表现优异。
Orchestrating Multimodal DNN Workloads in Wireless Neural Processing
Authors: Sai Xu, Kai-Kit Wong, Yanan Du, Hyundong Shin
First: 2026-03-02T17:25:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:25:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In edge inference, wireless resource allocation and accelerator-level deep neural network (DNN) scheduling have yet to be co-optimized in an end-to-end manner. The lack of coordination between wireless transmission and accelerator-level DNN execution prevents efficient overlap, leading to higher end-to-end inference latency. To address this issue, this paper investigates multimodal DNN workload orchestration in wireless neural processing (WNP), a paradigm that integrates wireless transmission and multi-core accelerator execution into a unified end-to-end pipeline. First, we develop a unified communication-computation model for multimodal DNN execution and formulate the corresponding optimization problem. Second, we propose O-WiN, a framework that orchestrates DNN workloads in WNP through two tightly coupled stages: simulation-based optimization and runtime execution. Third, we develop two algorithms, RTFS and PACS. RTFS schedules communication and computation sequentially, whereas PACS interleaves them to enable pipeline parallelism by overlapping wireless data transfer with accelerator-level DNN execution. Simulation results demonstrate that PACS significantly outperforms RTFS under high modality heterogeneity by better masking wireless latency through communication-computation overlap, thereby highlighting the effectiveness of communication-computation pipelining in accelerating multimodal DNN execution in WNP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无线神经处理中多模态DNN任务的编排
在边缘推理中，无线资源分配与加速器级深度神经网络（DNN）调度尚未实现端到端协同优化。无线传输与加速器级DNN执行之间的缺乏协调导致无法高效重叠，从而增加端到端推理延迟。为解决此问题，本文研究了无线神经处理（WNP）中的多模态DNN任务编排，该范式将无线传输与多核加速器执行整合为统一的端到端流水线。首先，我们为多模态DNN执行构建统一的通信-计算模型并制定相应优化问题。其次，我们提出O-WiN框架，通过两个紧密耦合阶段——基于仿真的优化与运行时执行——编排WNP中的DNN任务。第三，我们开发了两种算法：RTFS和PACS。RTFS按顺序调度通信与计算，而PACS通过交错二者以实现流水线并行，使无线数据传输与加速器级DNN执行重叠。仿真结果表明，在高模态异构性条件下，PACS通过通信-计算重叠更有效地掩蔽无线延迟，显著优于RTFS，凸显了通信-计算流水线在加速WNP中多模态DNN执行方面的有效性。
Summary / 总结
To address the inefficiency in edge inference caused by the lack of coordination between wireless transmission and accelerator-level DNN execution, this paper introduces wireless neural processing (WNP) as a unified end-to-end paradigm. It develops a communication-computation model and proposes O-WiN, a framework with two stages: simulation-based optimization and runtime execution. Two algorithms, RTFS and PACS, are designed—RTFS schedules sequentially while PACS interleaves communication and computation to enable pipeline parallelism. Experimental results show PACS significantly reduces end-to-end latency under high modality heterogeneity by better overlapping wireless transfer with DNN execution, demonstrating the effectiveness of pipelining.
为解决无线传输与加速器级DNN执行缺乏协同导致的边缘推理效率低下问题，本文提出无线神经处理（WNP）统一端到端范式。构建通信-计算模型并设计O-WiN框架，包含仿真优化与运行时执行两个阶段。提出RTFS与PACS两种算法，RTFS顺序调度，PACS交错调度以实现计算与通信并行。实验表明，在高模态异构场景下，PACS通过更优的通信-计算重叠显著降低端到端延迟，验证了流水线并行的有效性。
Generative Enzyme Design Guided by Functionally Important Sites and Small-Molecule Substrates
Authors: Zhenqiao Song, Yunlong Zhao, Wenxian Shi, Wengong Jin, Yang Yang, Lei Li
First: 2024-05-13T21:48:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:25:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Enzymes are genetically encoded biocatalysts capable of accelerating chemical reactions. How can we automatically design functional enzymes? In this paper, we propose EnzyGen, an approach to learn a unified model to design enzymes across all functional families. Our key idea is to generate an enzyme's amino acid sequence and their three-dimensional (3D) coordinates based on functionally important sites and substrates corresponding to a desired catalytic function. These sites are automatically mined from enzyme databases. EnzyGen consists of a novel interleaving network of attention and neighborhood equivariant layers, which captures both long-range correlation in an entire protein sequence and local influence from nearest amino acids in 3D space. To learn the generative model, we devise a joint training objective, including a sequence generation loss, a position prediction loss and an enzyme-substrate interaction loss. We further construct EnzyBench, a dataset with 3157 enzyme families, covering all available enzymes within the protein data bank (PDB). Experimental results show that our EnzyGen consistently achieves the best performance across all 323 testing families, surpassing the best baseline by 10.79% in terms of substrate binding affinity. These findings demonstrate EnzyGen's superior capability in designing well-folded and effective enzymes binding to specific substrates with high affinities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于功能重要位点和小分子底物引导的生成酶设计
酶是基因编码的生物催化剂，能够加速化学反应。我们如何自动设计功能酶？本文提出EnzyGen方法，旨在学习一个统一模型，以设计涵盖所有功能家族的酶。我们的核心思想是：根据目标催化功能所对应的结构功能重要位点和底物，生成酶的氨基酸序列及其三维坐标。这些位点自动从酶数据库中挖掘。EnzyGen由一种新颖的注意力与邻域等变层交错网络构成，能够捕捉整个蛋白质序列中的长程相关性以及三维空间中邻近氨基酸的局部影响。为学习生成模型，我们设计了一个联合训练目标，包括序列生成损失、位置预测损失和酶-底物相互作用损失。我们进一步构建了EnzyBench数据集，包含3157个酶家族，覆盖了蛋白质数据银行（PDB）中所有可用的酶。实验结果表明，EnzyGen在全部323个测试家族中均取得最佳性能，其底物结合亲和力比最佳基线高出10.79%。这些结果证明了EnzyGen在设计具有良好折叠结构且能高亲和力结合特定底物的有效酶方面具有优越能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to automatically design functional enzymes, this paper introduces EnzyGen, a unified generative model that designs enzyme sequences and 3D structures based on functionally important sites and substrates mined from databases. The method employs an interleaving network combining attention and neighborhood equivariant layers to capture both global sequence correlations and local 3D spatial influences. A joint training objective incorporating sequence generation, position prediction, and enzyme-substrate interaction losses enables comprehensive learning. Evaluated on EnzyBench—a dataset of 3157 enzyme families—the model outperforms all baselines across 323 test families, achieving a 10.79% improvement in substrate binding affinity, demonstrating its effectiveness in generating well-folded, high-affinity enzymes.
为实现功能酶的自动设计，本文提出EnzyGen模型，该模型基于从数据库中自动挖掘的功能重要位点和底物，生成酶的氨基酸序列及其三维结构。模型采用注意力与邻域等变层交织的架构，兼顾序列长程依赖与局部三维空间影响。通过联合训练目标（含序列生成、位置预测与酶-底物相互作用损失），EnzyGen在包含323个酶家族的EnzyBench数据集上全面超越现有基线，底物结合亲和力提升10.79%，证明其在生成结构合理、高亲和力酶方面具有优越性能。
ACDC: Adaptive Curriculum Planning with Dynamic Contrastive Control for Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning in Robotic Manipulation
Authors: Xuerui Wang, Guangyu Ren, Tianhong Dai, Bintao Hu, Shuangyao Huang, Wenzhang Zhang, Hengyan Liu
First: 2026-03-02T17:23:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:23:09+00:00
Comments: 13 pages (including references and appendix), 12 figures. Accepted to ICAPS 2026. Code available at https://github.com/Xuerui-Wang-oss/Adaptive-Curriculum-Learning-and-Dynamic-Contrastive-Control
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Goal-conditioned reinforcement learning has shown considerable potential in robotic manipulation; however, existing approaches remain limited by their reliance on prioritizing collected experience, resulting in suboptimal performance across diverse tasks. Inspired by human learning behaviors, we propose a more comprehensive learning paradigm, ACDC, which integrates multidimensional Adaptive Curriculum (AC) Planning with Dynamic Contrastive (DC) Control to guide the agent along a well-designed learning trajectory. More specifically, at the planning level, the AC component schedules the learning curriculum by dynamically balancing diversity-driven exploration and quality-driven exploitation based on the agent's success rate and training progress. At the control level, the DC component implements the curriculum plan through norm-constrained contrastive learning, enabling magnitude-guided experience selection aligned with the current curriculum focus. Extensive experiments on challenging robotic manipulation tasks demonstrate that ACDC consistently outperforms the state-of-the-art baselines in both sample efficiency and final task success rate.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ACDC：面向机器人操作目标条件强化学习的自适应课程规划与动态对比控制
目标条件强化学习在机器人操作中展现出巨大潜力，但现有方法受限于对收集经验的优先级处理，导致在多样化任务中表现不佳。受人类学习行为启发，我们提出ACDC框架，融合多维自适应课程（AC）规划与动态对比（DC）控制，引导智能体沿精心设计的学习轨迹进步。具体而言，在规划层面，AC模块根据智能体的成功率和训练进度动态平衡以多样性驱动的探索与以质量驱动的利用，调度学习课程；在控制层面，DC模块通过范数约束对比学习实现课程计划，使经验选择与当前课程重点保持幅度引导的一致性。在多个具有挑战性的机器人操作任务上的广泛实验表明，ACDC在样本效率和最终任务成功率上均显著优于现有最先进基线方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of existing goal-conditioned reinforcement learning methods due to static experience prioritization, the paper introduces ACDC, a framework combining Adaptive Curriculum Planning and Dynamic Contrastive Control. The curriculum planner dynamically balances exploration and exploitation based on agent performance and training progress, while the contrastive control module selects experiences via norm-constrained contrastive learning to align with current learning objectives. Experiments on robotic manipulation tasks show ACDC achieves superior sample efficiency and higher final success rates compared to state-of-the-art baselines.
为了解决现有目标条件强化学习方法因经验优先策略僵化导致的效率低下问题，本文提出ACDC框架，融合自适应课程规划与动态对比控制，引导机器人操作学习。课程规划模块根据智能体表现与训练进度动态平衡探索与利用，对比控制模块通过范数约束对比学习选择与当前课程目标对齐的经验。在多个机器人操作任务上的实验表明，ACDC在样本效率和最终成功率上均优于现有最先进方法。
Goal Reaching with Eikonal-Constrained Hierarchical Quasimetric Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Vittorio Giammarino, Ahmed H. Qureshi
First: 2025-12-12T21:37:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:21:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (GCRL) mitigates the difficulty of reward design by framing tasks as goal reaching rather than maximizing hand-crafted reward signals. In this setting, the optimal goal-conditioned value function naturally forms a quasimetric, motivating Quasimetric RL (QRL), which constrains value learning to quasimetric mappings and enforces local consistency through discrete, trajectory-based constraints. We propose Eikonal-Constrained Quasimetric RL (Eik-QRL), a continuous-time reformulation of QRL based on the Eikonal Partial Differential Equation (PDE). This PDE-based structure makes Eik-QRL trajectory-free, requiring only sampled states and goals, while improving out-of-distribution generalization. We provide theoretical guarantees for Eik-QRL and identify limitations that arise under complex dynamics. To address these challenges, we introduce Eik-Hierarchical QRL (Eik-HiQRL), which integrates Eik-QRL into a hierarchical decomposition. Empirically, Eik-HiQRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline goal-conditioned navigation and yields consistent gains over QRL in manipulation tasks, matching temporal-difference methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于Eikonal约束的层次化拟度量强化学习
目标条件强化学习（GCRL）通过将任务建模为目标达成而非最大化人工设计的奖励信号，缓解了奖励设计的难度。在此设定下，最优目标条件价值函数自然形成拟度量，由此启发拟度量强化学习（QRL），其约束价值学习为拟度量映射，并通过离散、基于轨迹的约束强制局部一致性。我们提出基于Eikonal偏微分方程（PDE）的连续时间重述形式——Eikonal约束拟度量强化学习（Eik-QRL）。该PDE结构使Eik-QRL无需轨迹，仅需采样状态与目标即可，同时提升分布外泛化能力。我们为Eik-QRL提供理论保证，并指出其在复杂动力学下存在的局限性。为应对这些挑战，我们引入Eik-Hierarchical QRL（Eik-HiQRL），将Eik-QRL整合进层次分解框架。实验证明，Eik-HiQRL在离线目标条件导航任务中达到最先进性能，并在操作任务中相较QRL持续提升，性能可媲美时序差分方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to simplify reward design in goal-conditioned reinforcement learning, this work introduces Eikonal-Constrained Quasimetric RL (Eik-QRL), a continuous-time framework based on the Eikonal PDE that enforces quasimetric value functions without requiring trajectory data. Eik-QRL improves out-of-distribution generalization and is theoretically grounded, though it struggles under complex dynamics. To overcome this, Eik-Hierarchical QRL (Eik-HiQRL) is proposed, integrating Eik-QRL into a hierarchical structure. Experiments show Eik-HiQRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline navigation and consistently outperforms QRL in manipulation tasks, matching the performance of temporal-difference methods.
为提升目标条件强化学习中的泛化能力并减少对人工奖励函数的依赖，本文提出基于Eikonal偏微分方程的连续时间框架Eik-QRL，通过约束值函数为拟度量结构，无需轨迹数据即可实现更优的分布外泛化，但其在复杂动力学下表现受限。为此，引入层级结构Eik-HiQRL，将Eik-QRL嵌入层次分解中。实验表明，Eik-HiQRL在离线导航任务中达到最先进水平，在操作任务中持续优于标准QRL，性能可媲美时序差分方法。
Stochastic Multi-Armed Bandits with Limited Control Variates
Authors: Arun Verma, Manjesh Kumar Hanawal, Arun Rajkumar
First: 2026-03-02T17:20:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:20:46+00:00
Comments: Accepted at COMSNETS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Motivated by wireless networks where interference or channel state estimates provide partial insight into throughput, we study a variant of the classical stochastic multi-armed bandit problem in which the learner has limited access to auxiliary information. Recent work has shown that such auxiliary information, when available as control variates, can be used to get tighter confidence bounds, leading to lower regret. However, existing works assume that control variates are available in every round, which may not be realistic in several real-life scenarios. To address this, we propose UCB-LCV, an upper confidence bound (UCB) based algorithm that effectively combines the estimators obtained from rewards and control variates. When there is no control variate, UCB-LCV leads to a novel algorithm that we call UCB-NORMAL, outperforming its existing algorithms for the standard MAB setting with normally distributed rewards. Finally, we discuss variants of the proposed UCB-LCV that apply to general distributions and experimentally demonstrate that UCB-LCV outperforms existing bandit algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有限控制变量的随机多臂赌博机问题
受无线网络中干扰或信道状态估计可提供部分吞吐量信息的启发，我们研究了一种经典随机多臂赌博机问题的变体，其中学习者对辅助信息的访问受限。近期研究表明，当辅助信息以控制变量形式可用时，可获得更紧的置信界，从而降低遗憾。然而，现有工作假设控制变量在每轮均可用，这在某些现实场景中可能不现实。为此，我们提出UCB-LCV算法，一种基于置信上界（UCB）的方法，有效结合了来自奖励和控制变量的估计值。当无控制变量时，UCB-LCV导出一种新算法UCB-NORMAL，在标准MAB设置下（奖励服从正态分布），其性能优于现有算法。最后，我们讨论了适用于一般分布的UCB-LCV变体，并通过实验验证UCB-LCV优于现有赌博机算法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by real-world wireless networks where partial auxiliary information like interference or channel state estimates is available but not always reliable, this paper studies a stochastic multi-armed bandit problem with limited access to control variates. The authors propose UCB-LCV, an upper confidence bound algorithm that intelligently combines reward estimates with available control variates when present, and falls back to UCB-NORMAL—a novel algorithm for the standard MAB setting—when no control variates are available. Experimental results show that UCB-LCV consistently outperforms existing bandit algorithms, especially in scenarios where control variates are sparse, and also demonstrates strong performance under general reward distributions.
受无线网络中干扰或信道状态估计等部分辅助信息可用但不可靠的现实场景启发，本文研究了一种控制变差有限可用的随机多臂赌博机问题。作者提出UCB-LCV算法，该算法在控制变差可用时智能结合奖励与控制变差估计，在无控制变差时退化为UCB-NORMAL算法。实验表明，UCB-LCV在控制变差部分可用时仍能实现比现有算法更低的遗憾值，并在标准正态分布奖励的MAB场景中表现优于现有先进方法。
Recursive Think-Answer Process for LLMs and VLMs
Authors: Byung-Kwan Lee, Youngchae Chee, Yong Man Ro
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:20:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:20:10+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026 Findings, Project page: https://litcoderr.github.io/rtap_page/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Think-Answer reasoners such as DeepSeek-R1 have made notable progress by leveraging interpretable internal reasoning. However, despite the frequent presence of self-reflective cues like "Oops!", they remain vulnerable to output errors during single-pass inference. To address this limitation, we propose an efficient Recursive Think-Answer Process (R-TAP) that enables models to engage in iterative reasoning cycles and generate more accurate answers, going beyond conventional single-pass approaches. Central to this approach is a confidence generator that evaluates the certainty of model responses and guides subsequent improvements. By incorporating two complementary rewards-Recursively Confidence Increase Reward and Final Answer Confidence Reward-we show that R-TAP-enhanced models consistently outperform conventional single-pass methods for both large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs). Moreover, by analyzing the frequency of "Oops"-like expressions in model responses, we find that R-TAP-applied models exhibit significantly fewer self-reflective patterns, resulting in more stable and faster inference-time reasoning. We hope R-TAP pave the way evolving into efficient and elaborated methods to refine the reasoning processes of future AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型与视觉语言模型的递归思考-回答过程
如DeepSeek-R1等思考-回答推理器通过可解释的内部推理取得了显著进展。然而，尽管常出现类似“Oops!”的自我反思提示，它们在单次推理中仍易产生输出错误。为解决此局限，我们提出一种高效的递归思考-回答过程（R-TAP），使模型能进行迭代推理循环，生成更准确的答案，超越传统单次推理方法。该方法核心是置信度生成器，用于评估模型响应的确定性并引导后续改进。通过引入两种互补奖励——递归置信度提升奖励与最终答案置信度奖励——我们证明R-TAP增强模型在大语言模型（LLMs）和视觉语言模型（VLMs）上均持续优于传统单次方法。此外，通过分析模型响应中“Oops”类表达的频率，发现应用R-TAP的模型显著减少自我反思模式，推理过程更稳定且更快。我们希望R-TAP能为未来AI推理过程的高效化与精细化提供新路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of single-pass think-answer models that remain error-prone despite self-reflective cues like "Oops!", this work introduces Recursive Think-Answer Process (R-TAP), a method enabling iterative reasoning cycles to improve accuracy. R-TAP incorporates a confidence generator that evaluates response certainty and directs refinement, guided by two complementary rewards: Recursively Confidence Increase Reward and Final Answer Confidence Reward. Experimental results show R-TAP-enhanced models consistently outperform baseline single-pass methods on both LLMs and VLMs, while also reducing the frequency of self-reflective expressions, leading to more stable and faster inference.
为了解决单次推理中即使带有自我反思提示（如“Oops!”）仍易出错的问题，本文提出递归思考-回答过程（R-TAP），通过迭代推理循环提升准确性。该方法引入置信度生成器评估回答确定性，并结合两种奖励机制——递归置信度提升奖励与最终答案置信度奖励——引导模型优化。实验表明，R-TAP增强的模型在LLM和VLM上均显著优于传统单次推理方法，同时减少自我反思表达频率，实现更稳定、更快的推理过程。
OmniRet: Efficient and High-Fidelity Omni Modality Retrieval
Authors: Chuong Huynh, Manh Luong, Abhinav Shrivastava
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:19:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:19:55+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026. Project link: https://github.com/hmchuong/omniret
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multimodal retrieval is the task of aggregating information from queries across heterogeneous modalities to retrieve desired targets. State-of-the-art multimodal retrieval models can understand complex queries, yet they are typically limited to two modalities: text and vision. This limitation impedes the development of universal retrieval systems capable of comprehending queries that combine more than two modalities. To advance toward this goal, we present OmniRet, the first retrieval model capable of handling complex, composed queries spanning three key modalities: text, vision, and audio. Our OmniRet model addresses two critical challenges for universal retrieval: computational efficiency and representation fidelity. First, feeding massive token sequences from modality-specific encoders to Large Language Models (LLMs) is computationally inefficient. We therefore introduce an attention-based resampling mechanism to generate compact, fixed-size representations from these sequences. Second, compressing rich omni-modal data into a single embedding vector inevitably causes information loss and discards fine-grained details. We propose Attention Sliced Wasserstein Pooling to preserve these fine-grained details, leading to improved omni-modal representations. OmniRet is trained on an aggregation of approximately 6 million query-target pairs spanning 30 datasets. We benchmark our model on 13 retrieval tasks and a MMEBv2 subset. Our model demonstrates significant improvements on composed query, audio and video retrieval tasks, while achieving on-par performance with state-of-the-art models on others. Furthermore, we curate a new Audio-Centric Multimodal Benchmark (ACM). This new benchmark introduces two critical, previously missing tasks-composed audio retrieval and audio-visual retrieval to more comprehensively evaluate a model's omni-modal embedding capacity.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for universal multimodal retrieval systems capable of handling complex queries across text, vision, and audio, OmniRet introduces a novel approach to overcome computational inefficiency and representation fidelity challenges. It employs an attention-based resampling mechanism to generate compact fixed-size representations from modality-specific encoder outputs, and Attention Sliced Wasserstein Pooling to preserve fine-grained details during embedding compression. Trained on 6 million query-target pairs from 30 datasets, OmniRet achieves significant performance gains on composed query, audio, and video retrieval tasks while matching state-of-the-art results on others. Additionally, it introduces the Audio-Centric Multimodal Benchmark (ACM) to evaluate audio-visual and composed audio retrieval, previously underserved in multimodal benchmarks.
为应对现有模型仅支持文本与视觉模态、难以处理多模态复合查询的问题，作者提出OmniRet，首次实现文本、视觉与音频三模态统一检索。为解决长序列编码带来的计算开销，引入基于注意力的重采样机制生成固定长度表示；为避免压缩过程丢失细节，提出注意力切片Wasserstein池化方法以保留细粒度信息。模型在600万对查询-目标数据上训练，在13项任务中表现优异，尤其在复合查询、音频与视频检索任务上显著优于现有方法，其他任务与SOTA持平。同时，作者构建了音频中心多模态基准（ACM），新增复合音频与音视频检索任务，填补了评估音频模态能力的空白。
Selecting Optimal Variable Order in Autoregressive Ising Models
Authors: Shiba Biswal, Marc Vuffray, Andrey Y. Lokhov
First: 2026-02-23T22:15:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:18:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autoregressive models enable tractable sampling from learned probability distributions, but their performance critically depends on the variable ordering used in the factorization via complexities of the resulting conditional distributions. We propose to learn the Markov random field describing the underlying data, and use the inferred graphical model structure to construct optimized variable orderings. We illustrate our approach on two-dimensional image-like models where a structure-aware ordering leads to restricted conditioning sets, thereby reducing model complexity. Numerical experiments on Ising models with discrete data demonstrate that graph-informed orderings yield higher-fidelity generated samples compared to naive variable orderings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归Ising模型中最优变量顺序的选择
自回归模型可实现从学习到的概率分布中进行可处理的采样，但其性能高度依赖于因式分解中所采用的变量顺序，因为这会影响生成条件分布的复杂性。我们提出学习描述底层数据的马尔可夫随机场，并利用推断出的图模型结构构建优化的变量顺序。我们在二维图像类模型上展示了该方法，结构感知的排序可导致受限的条件集合，从而降低模型复杂度。在离散数据的Ising模型上的数值实验表明，基于图结构的排序相比朴素变量排序能生成更高保真度的样本。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sensitivity of autoregressive models to variable ordering, which affects conditional distribution complexity and sampling efficiency, this work proposes learning a Markov random field from data to guide the construction of optimal variable orderings. The method leverages the inferred graphical structure to define a structure-aware ordering that minimizes conditioning sets, thereby reducing model complexity. Experimental results on discrete Ising models show that graph-informed orderings produce higher-fidelity generated samples compared to naive orderings, demonstrating improved modeling performance.
该文指出自回归模型性能依赖于变量排序，而排序影响条件分布的复杂度。作者提出从数据中学习马尔可夫随机场以推断图结构，再据此构建优化的变量排序，从而减少条件集合。在二维图像类伊辛模型上的实验表明，基于图结构的排序生成样本质量优于随机或朴素排序，验证了该方法在提升建模效率和样本保真度方面的有效性。
HalluGuard: Demystifying Data-Driven and Reasoning-Driven Hallucinations in LLMs
Authors: Xinyue Zeng, Junhong Lin, Yujun Yan, Feng Guo, Liang Shi, Jun Wu, Dawei Zhou
Venue: ICLR
First: 2026-01-26T18:23:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:18:04+00:00
Comments: Accepted by The Fourteenth International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR'26)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The reliability of Large Language Models (LLMs) in high-stakes domains such as healthcare, law, and scientific discovery is often compromised by hallucinations. These failures typically stem from two sources: data-driven hallucinations and reasoning-driven hallucinations. However, existing detection methods usually address only one source and rely on task-specific heuristics, limiting their generalization to complex scenarios. To overcome these limitations, we introduce the Hallucination Risk Bound, a unified theoretical framework that formally decomposes hallucination risk into data-driven and reasoning-driven components, linked respectively to training-time mismatches and inference-time instabilities. This provides a principled foundation for analyzing how hallucinations emerge and evolve. Building on this foundation, we introduce HalluGuard, an NTK-based score that leverages the induced geometry and captured representations of the NTK to jointly identify data-driven and reasoning-driven hallucinations. We evaluate HalluGuard on 10 diverse benchmarks, 11 competitive baselines, and 9 popular LLM backbones, consistently achieving state-of-the-art performance in detecting diverse forms of LLM hallucinations. We open-source our proposed \model{} model at https://github.com/Susan571/HalluGuard-ICLR2026.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HalluGuard：揭开大语言模型中数据驱动与推理驱动幻觉的神秘面纱
在医疗、法律和科学发现等高风险领域，大语言模型（LLMs）的可靠性常因幻觉而受损。这些失败通常源于两类幻觉：数据驱动幻觉与推理驱动幻觉。然而，现有检测方法通常仅针对单一来源，并依赖任务特定启发式规则，难以推广至复杂场景。为克服此局限，我们提出“幻觉风险界”，一个统一的理论框架，将幻觉风险形式化分解为数据驱动与推理驱动两部分，分别关联训练时的不匹配与推理时的不稳定性，为分析幻觉的产生与演化提供理论基础。在此基础上，我们提出HalluGuard，一种基于NTK的评分方法，利用NTK诱导的几何结构与捕获的表示，联合识别数据驱动与推理驱动幻觉。我们在10个多样化基准、11个竞争基线及9个流行LLM架构上评估HalluGuard，始终在检测各类LLM幻觉方面取得最先进性能。我们开源模型代码于https://github.com/Susan571/HalluGuard-ICLR2026。
Summary / 总结
Driven by the need to reliably detect hallucinations in LLMs across high-stakes domains, this work introduces HalluGuard, a unified detection framework that decomposes hallucination risk into data-driven and reasoning-driven components using the Hallucination Risk Bound. It leverages the Neural Tangent Kernel (NTK) to capture geometric and representational properties during inference, enabling joint identification of both hallucination types. Evaluated across 10 benchmarks, 11 baselines, and 9 LLM backbones, HalluGuard consistently outperforms existing methods, demonstrating strong generalization and robustness to diverse hallucination patterns.
为提升大语言模型在医疗、法律等高风险领域中的可靠性，该研究提出HalluGuard框架，通过“幻觉风险界限”将幻觉风险分解为数据驱动与推理驱动两类，并基于神经切线核（NTK）的几何与表征特性，联合识别两类幻觉。在10个基准、11个基线模型和9个主流LLM架构上评估，HalluGuard持续优于现有方法，展现出对多样幻觉模式的强泛化能力与鲁棒性。
ClinConsensus: A Consensus-Based Benchmark for Evaluating Chinese Medical LLMs across Difficulty Levels
Authors: Xiang Zheng, Han Li, Wenjie Luo, Weiqi Zhai, Yiyuan Li, Chuanmiao Yan, Tianyi Tang, Yubo Ma, Kexin Yang, Dayiheng Liu, Hu Wei, Bing Zhao
First: 2026-03-02T17:17:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:17:18+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures,
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied to health management, showing promise across disease prevention, clinical decision-making, and long-term care. However, existing medical benchmarks remain largely static and task-isolated, failing to capture the openness, longitudinal structure, and safety-critical complexity of real-world clinical workflows. We introduce ClinConsensus, a Chinese medical benchmark curated, validated, and quality-controlled by clinical experts. ClinConsensus comprises 2500 open-ended cases spanning the full continuum of care--from prevention and intervention to long-term follow-up--covering 36 medical specialties, 12 common clinical task types, and progressively increasing levels of complexity. To enable reliable evaluation of such complex scenarios, we adopt a rubric-based grading protocol and propose the Clinically Applicable Consistency Score (CACS@k). We further introduce a dual-judge evaluation framework, combining a high-capability LLM-as-judge with a distilled, locally deployable judge model trained via supervised fine-tuning, enabling scalable and reproducible evaluation aligned with physician judgment. Using ClinConsensus, we conduct a comprehensive assessment of several leading LLMs and reveal substantial heterogeneity across task themes, care stages, and medical specialties. While top-performing models achieve comparable overall scores, they differ markedly in reasoning, evidence use, and longitudinal follow-up capabilities, and clinically actionable treatment planning remains a key bottleneck. We release ClinConsensus as an extensible benchmark to support the development and evaluation of medical LLMs that are robust, clinically grounded, and ready for real-world deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ClinConsensus：用于评估中文医疗大语言模型跨难度水平的共识基准
大语言模型（LLMs）正越来越多地应用于健康管理，在疾病预防、临床决策和长期照护等方面展现出潜力。然而，现有医疗基准仍主要静态且任务孤立，未能捕捉真实临床工作流的开放性、纵向结构及安全关键性复杂性。我们引入ClinConsensus，这是一个由临床专家策划、验证并质量控制的中文医疗基准。ClinConsensus包含2500个开放式案例，覆盖从预防与干预到长期随访的完整照护连续体，涵盖36个医学专科、12类常见临床任务类型，并逐步提升复杂度。为实现对复杂场景的可靠评估，我们采用基于评分量表的评分协议，并提出临床适用一致性得分（CACS@k）。我们进一步引入双评委评估框架，结合高能力LLM作为评委与通过监督微调训练的轻量化、本地可部署评委模型，实现与医师判断一致的可扩展且可重复评估。利用ClinConsensus，我们对多个领先LLM进行全面评估，发现其在任务主题、照护阶段和医学专科间存在显著异质性。尽管表现最佳的模型整体得分相近，但在推理能力、证据使用及纵向随访能力上差异显著，临床可操作的治疗规划仍为关键瓶颈。我们发布ClinConsensus作为可扩展基准，以支持开发稳健、临床导向且适用于真实部署的医疗LLM。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for realistic, clinically grounded benchmarks to evaluate Chinese medical LLMs, the authors introduce ClinConsensus—a 2500-case benchmark curated by clinicians covering 36 specialties and 12 task types across care stages with increasing complexity. They employ a rubric-based grading system and propose the Clinically Applicable Consistency Score (CACS@k) to measure model performance, supported by a dual-judge framework combining a high-capacity LLM judge and a distilled local model. Experimental results show that while top models achieve similar overall scores, they vary significantly in reasoning quality, evidence handling, and longitudinal care planning, with clinically actionable treatment planning remaining a persistent weakness.
为评估中文医疗大语言模型的临床实用性，作者构建了ClinConsensus基准，包含2500个由临床专家编纂的开放病例，覆盖36个专科、12类临床任务及递进式复杂度。采用基于评分量表的评估体系与临床适用一致性得分（CACS@k），并引入双判官框架（高能力LLM判官+本地部署的蒸馏模型）。实验表明，顶尖模型整体得分相近，但在推理质量、证据使用和长期随访能力上差异显著，临床可执行治疗规划仍是主要瓶颈。
FluxMem: Adaptive Hierarchical Memory for Streaming Video Understanding
Authors: Yiweng Xie, Bo He, Junke Wang, Xiangyu Zheng, Ziyi Ye, Zuxuan Wu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:16:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:16:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted at CVPR 2026. Project page: https://yiwengxie.com/FluxMem/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper presents FluxMem, a training-free framework for efficient streaming video understanding. FluxMem adaptively compresses redundant visual memory through a hierarchical, two-stage design: (1) a Temporal Adjacency Selection (TAS) module removes redundant visual tokens across adjacent frames, and (2) a Spatial Domain Consolidation (SDC) module further merges spatially repetitive regions within each frame into compact representations. To adapt effectively to dynamic scenes, we introduce a self-adaptive token compression mechanism in both TAS and SDC, which automatically determines the compression rate based on intrinsic scene statistics rather than manual tuning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that FluxMem achieves new state-of-the-art results on existing online video benchmarks, reaching 76.4 on StreamingBench and 67.2 on OVO-Bench under real-time settings, while reducing latency by 69.9% and peak GPU memory by 34.5% on OVO-Bench. Furthermore, it maintains strong offline performance, achieving 73.1 on MLVU while using 65% fewer visual tokens.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FluxMem：面向流式视频理解的自适应分层记忆
本文提出FluxMem，一种无需训练的高效流式视频理解框架。FluxMem通过分层两阶段设计自适应压缩冗余视觉记忆：(1) 时间邻接选择（TAS）模块移除相邻帧间的冗余视觉标记；(2) 空域域整合（SDC）模块进一步将每帧内空间重复区域合并为紧凑表示。为有效适应动态场景，我们在TAS和SDC中引入自适应标记压缩机制，依据场景内在统计自动确定压缩率，无需手动调参。大量实验表明，FluxMem在现有在线视频基准上取得新SOTA：实时设置下于StreamingBench达76.4、OVO-Bench达67.2，同时在OVO-Bench上降低延迟69.9%、峰值GPU内存34.5%。此外，其离线性能亦强劲，在MLVU上达73.1，且视觉标记使用量减少65%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient real-time video understanding without retraining, FluxMem introduces a training-free framework that adaptively compresses visual memory through a two-stage hierarchical design: Temporal Adjacency Selection removes redundant tokens across adjacent frames, while Spatial Domain Consolidation merges repetitive regions within frames into compact representations. Both stages employ self-adaptive compression mechanisms that adjust compression rates based on scene statistics, eliminating manual tuning. Experiments show FluxMem achieves state-of-the-art results on streaming benchmarks—76.4 on StreamingBench and 67.2 on OVO-Bench under real-time constraints—while cutting latency by 69.9% and peak GPU memory by 34.5% on OVO-Bench, and retains strong offline performance (73.1 on MLVU) using 65% fewer visual tokens.
为实现无需训练的高效实时视频理解，FluxMem提出一种自适应分层记忆压缩框架：首先通过时序邻近选择模块去除相邻帧间的冗余视觉token，再通过空间域整合模块将帧内重复区域合并为紧凑表示。两个模块均采用基于场景统计的自适应压缩机制，无需人工调参。实验表明，该框架在流媒体基准上达到最优性能——实时环境下StreamingBench为76.4、OVO-Bench为67.2，同时在OVO-Bench上降低延迟69.9%、峰值显存34.5%，且在离线任务MLVU上仍保持73.1的高分，仅用65%的视觉token。
UNCLE-Grasp: Uncertainty-Aware Grasping of Leaf-Occluded Strawberries
Authors: Malak Mansour, Ali Abouzeid, Zezhou Sun, Qinbo Sun, Dezhen Song, Abdalla Swikir
First: 2026-01-20T21:27:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:15:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robotic strawberry harvesting remains challenging under partial occlusion, where leaf interference introduces significant geometric uncertainty and renders grasp decisions based on a single deterministic shape estimate unreliable. From a single partial observation, multiple incompatible 3D shape completions may be plausible, such that grasps deemed feasible on one completion can fail on another. This paper presents an uncertainty-aware grasping pipeline for partially occluded strawberries that explicitly models geometric uncertainty arising from both occlusion and learned shape completion. The proposed approach employs point cloud completion with Monte Carlo dropout to sample multiple shape hypotheses, generates candidate grasps for each completion, and evaluates grasp feasibility using physically grounded force-closure metrics. Rather than selecting a grasp from a single shape estimate, feasibility is aggregated across completions and a conservative lower confidence bound (LCB) criterion is used to decide whether grasping a strawberry should be attempted or safely abstained. The method is evaluated in simulation and on a physical robot under increasing levels of synthetic and real leaf occlusion. Experimental results demonstrate that uncertainty-aware decision making enables reliable abstention from high-risk grasp attempts under severe occlusion while maintaining robust grasp execution when geometric confidence is sufficient, outperforming deterministic baselines in both simulated and physical robot experiments.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of reliably grasping partially occluded strawberries under leaf interference, this paper introduces UNCLE-Grasp, an uncertainty-aware grasping pipeline that models geometric uncertainty from occlusion and shape completion. It uses Monte Carlo dropout to sample multiple 3D shape hypotheses from partial point clouds, generates grasps for each, and evaluates feasibility using force-closure metrics. The system aggregates grasp confidence across all hypotheses and applies a conservative lower confidence bound to decide whether to attempt or abstain from grasping. Experiments in simulation and on a real robot show that this approach successfully avoids risky grasps under heavy occlusion while maintaining high success rates when geometry is confident, outperforming deterministic methods.
为了解决叶片遮挡下草莓采摘机器人因几何不确定性导致的抓取决策不可靠问题，本文提出一种不确定性感知的抓取方法。该方法利用蒙特卡洛dropout生成多个可能的3D形状假设，为每个假设生成抓取候选方案，并通过力闭合指标评估抓取可行性。抓取决策基于所有假设的可行性聚合，采用保守的置信下界准则，使机器人在高不确定性时安全放弃抓取，而在几何置信度足够时仍能稳定执行抓取。仿真与实物机器人实验表明，该方法在不同遮挡程度下均优于确定性基线方法，兼具可靠性与成功率。
On the Rate of Convergence of GD in Non-linear Neural Networks: An Adversarial Robustness Perspective
Authors: Guy Smorodinsky, Sveta Gimpleson, Itay Safran
First: 2026-03-02T17:13:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:13:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the convergence dynamics of Gradient Descent (GD) in a minimal binary classification setting, consisting of a two-neuron ReLU network and two training instances. We prove that even under these strong simplifying assumptions, while GD successfully converges to an optimal robustness margin, effectively maximizing the distance between the decision boundary and the training points, this convergence occurs at a prohibitively slow rate, scaling strictly as $Θ(1/\ln(t))$. To the best of our knowledge, this establishes the first explicit lower bound on the convergence rate of the robustness margin in a non-linear model. Through empirical simulations, we further demonstrate that this inherent failure mode is pervasive, exhibiting the exact same tight convergence rate across multiple natural network initializations. Our theoretical guarantees are derived via a rigorous analysis of the GD trajectories across the distinct activation patterns of the model. Specifically, we develop tight control over the system's dynamics to bound the trajectory of the decision boundary, overcoming the primary technical challenge introduced by the non-linear nature of the architecture.
