标题：非线性神经网络中梯度下降收敛速率的研究：从对抗鲁棒性视角
我们在一个最小二元分类设定下研究梯度下降（GD）的收敛动力学，该设定包含一个两神经元ReLU网络和两个训练样本。我们证明，即使在这些强简化的假设下，虽然GD成功收敛至最优鲁棒性边界，即最大化决策边界与训练点之间的距离，但其收敛速度异常缓慢，严格按Θ(1/ln(t))标度。据我们所知，这首次建立了非线性模型中鲁棒性边界收敛速率的明确下界。通过实证模拟，我们进一步表明，这种固有失效模式普遍存在，在多种自然网络初始化下均表现出完全相同的紧收敛速率。我们的理论保证源于对GD轨迹在模型不同激活模式下进行的严谨分析。具体而言，我们对系统动力学建立了精确控制，以约束决策边界的轨迹，从而克服了架构非线性带来的主要技术挑战。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by understanding the convergence behavior of Gradient Descent in non-linear neural networks, this study analyzes GD in a minimal binary classification setup with a two-neuron ReLU network and two training points. The authors prove that GD converges to an optimal robustness margin—maximizing the distance between the decision boundary and training points—but at an extremely slow rate, scaling as Θ(1/ln(t)). This establishes the first known explicit lower bound on robustness margin convergence in non-linear models. Empirical results confirm this slow convergence is consistent across various natural initializations, and the theoretical analysis relies on tracking GD trajectories through distinct activation patterns to tightly bound the decision boundary’s movement.
为理解梯度下降在非线性神经网络中的收敛行为，该研究在包含两个神经元和两个训练样本的最小二分类设置中分析GD。作者证明，尽管GD能收敛至最优鲁棒边界（即最大化决策边界与训练点的距离），但其收敛速度极慢，呈Θ(1/ln(t))量级，这是首个在非线性模型中明确给出的鲁棒边界收敛下界。实验表明，该缓慢收敛模式在多种自然初始化下普遍存在，理论分析通过追踪GD在不同激活模式下的轨迹，精确控制决策边界的运动以实现收敛速率的上界。
FedHB: Hierarchical Bayesian Federated Learning
Authors: Minyoung Kim, Timothy Hospedales
First: 2023-05-08T18:21:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:12:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a novel hierarchical Bayesian approach to Federated Learning (FL), where our model reasonably describes the generative process of clients' local data via hierarchical Bayesian modeling: constituting random variables of local models for clients that are governed by a higher-level global variate. Interestingly, the variational inference in our Bayesian model leads to an optimisation problem whose block-coordinate descent solution becomes a distributed algorithm that is separable over clients and allows them not to reveal their own private data at all, thus fully compatible with FL. We also highlight that our block-coordinate algorithm has particular forms that subsume the well-known FL algorithms including Fed-Avg and Fed-Prox as special cases. Beyond introducing novel modeling and derivations, we also offer convergence analysis showing that our block-coordinate FL algorithm converges to an (local) optimum of the objective at the rate of $O(1/\sqrt{t})$, the same rate as regular (centralised) SGD, as well as the generalisation error analysis where we prove that the test error of our model on unseen data is guaranteed to vanish as we increase the training data size, thus asymptotically optimal.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FedHB：分层贝叶斯联邦学习
我们提出了一种新颖的分层贝叶斯方法用于联邦学习（FL），其中模型通过分层贝叶斯建模合理描述了客户端本地数据的生成过程：客户端本地模型的随机变量受更高层次的全局变量支配。有趣的是，我们贝叶斯模型中的变分推断导出一个优化问题，其块坐标下降解法成为一种可按客户端分离的分布式算法，且完全不泄露客户端私有数据，因此与FL完全兼容。我们还指出，我们的块坐标算法具有特定形式，可包含已知的FL算法（如Fed-Avg和Fed-Prox）作为特例。除了引入新颖的建模与推导，我们还提供了收敛性分析，表明我们的块坐标FL算法以$O(1/\sqrt{t})$的速度收敛至目标函数的（局部）最优解，与常规（集中式）SGD相同；同时提供了泛化误差分析，证明当训练数据规模增大时，模型在未见数据上的测试误差必然趋近于零，从而渐近最优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for privacy-preserving federated learning with robust generalization, this paper introduces FedHB, a hierarchical Bayesian framework that models client local data via shared global priors. The method employs variational inference to derive a block-coordinate descent algorithm that operates locally on each client without exposing private data, while naturally encompassing FedAvg and FedProx as special cases. Experimental results demonstrate that the algorithm converges at an O(1/√t) rate matching centralized SGD and achieves asymptotically optimal generalization error as training data grows.
为实现隐私保护且具备不确定性建模能力的联邦学习，本文提出FedHB框架，通过分层贝叶斯建模将客户端本地数据生成过程与全局参数关联。该方法利用变分推断导出一种块坐标下降算法，可在不泄露本地数据的前提下本地执行，且涵盖FedAvg与FedProx等经典算法。实验表明，该算法收敛至局部最优解的速度为O(1/√t)，与集中式SGD一致，且测试误差随训练数据量增加而渐近消失，达到最优泛化性能。
Dense-Jump Flow Matching with Non-Uniform Time Scheduling for Robotic Policies: Mitigating Multi-Step Inference Degradation
Authors: Zidong Chen, Zihao Guo, Peng Wang, ThankGod Itua Egbe, Yan Lyu, Chenghao Qian
First: 2025-09-16T22:28:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:11:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Flow matching has emerged as a competitive framework for learning high-quality generative policies in robotics; however, we find that generalisation arises and saturates early along the flow trajectory, in accordance with recent findings in the literature. We further observe that increasing the number of Euler integration steps during inference counter-intuitively and universally degrades policy performance. We attribute this to (i) additional, uniformly spaced integration steps oversample the late-time region, thereby constraining actions towards the training trajectories and reducing generalisation; and (ii) the learned velocity field becoming non-Lipschitz as integration time approaches 1, causing instability. To address these issues, we propose a novel policy that utilises non-uniform time scheduling (e.g., U-shaped) during training, which emphasises both early and late temporal stages to regularise policy training, and a dense-jump integration schedule at inference, which uses a single-step integration to replace the multi-step integration beyond a jump point, to avoid unstable areas around 1. Essentially, our policy is an efficient one-step learner that still pushes forward performance through multi-step integration, yielding up to 23.7% performance gains over state-of-the-art baselines across diverse robotic tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于非均匀时间调度的密集跳跃流匹配用于机器人策略：缓解多步推理退化
流匹配已成为学习高质量生成性机器人策略的有竞争力框架；然而，我们发现流轨迹早期即出现泛化并饱和，这与近期文献发现一致。我们进一步观察到，推理时增加欧拉积分步数反而普遍且反直觉地降低策略性能。我们将其归因于：(i) 额外的均匀分布积分步数过度采样晚期时间区域，从而限制动作趋向训练轨迹并降低泛化能力；(ii) 当积分时间接近1时，学习到的速度场变得非利普希茨，导致不稳定。为解决这些问题，我们提出一种新策略：训练时采用非均匀时间调度（如U形），以强调早期和晚期时间阶段来正则化策略训练；推理时采用密集跳跃积分调度，用单步积分替代跳跃点之后的多步积分，以避开接近1的不稳定区域。本质上，我们的策略是一种高效的单步学习器，仍通过多步积分推动性能提升，在多种机器人任务上相较现有最先进基线最高提升23.7%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that flow matching policies suffer from early saturation and performance degradation under multi-step inference, this work introduces a method combining non-uniform time scheduling during training and dense-jump integration during inference. The training schedule uses U-shaped time sampling to emphasize early and late temporal stages, promoting generalization, while inference employs a single-step integration beyond a predefined jump point to avoid instability near time 1. Experiments across diverse robotic tasks show that this approach yields up to 23.7% performance gains over state-of-the-art baselines, demonstrating its effectiveness in mitigating multi-step inference degradation.
鉴于流匹配策略在轨迹早期出现饱和且多步推理时性能下降的问题，本文提出一种结合训练阶段非均匀时间调度与推理阶段密集跳跃积分的方法。训练阶段采用U形时间采样，强化早期和晚期时间阶段以提升泛化能力；推理阶段在跳跃点后采用单步积分，避免接近时间1时的不稳定性。实验表明，该方法在多种机器人任务上较现有最先进方法提升最高达23.7%的性能。
Adam Converges Without Any Modification On Update Rules
Authors: Yushun Zhang, Bingran Li, Congliang Chen, Zhi-Quan Luo, Ruoyu Sun
First: 2026-03-02T17:08:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:08:51+00:00
Comments: 66 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Adam is the default algorithm for training neural networks, including large language models (LLMs). However, \citet{reddi2019convergence} provided an example that Adam diverges, raising concerns for its deployment in AI model training. We identify a key mismatch between the divergence example and practice: \citet{reddi2019convergence} pick the problem after picking the hyperparameters of Adam, i.e., $(β_1,β_2)$; while practical applications often fix the problem first and then tune $(β_1,β_2)$. In this work, we prove that Adam converges with proper problem-dependent hyperparameters. First, we prove that Adam converges when $β_2$ is large and $β_1 < \sqrt{β_2}$. Second, when $β_2$ is small, we point out a region of $(β_1,β_2)$ combinations where Adam can diverge to infinity. Our results indicate a phase transition for Adam from divergence to convergence when changing the $(β_1, β_2)$ combination. To our knowledge, this is the first phase transition in $(β_1,β_2)$ 2D-plane reported in the literature, providing rigorous theoretical guarantees for Adam optimizer. We further point out that the critical boundary $(β_1^*, β_2^*)$ is problem-dependent, and particularly, dependent on batch size. This provides suggestions on how to tune $β_1$ and $β_2$: when Adam does not work well, we suggest tuning up $β_2$ inversely with batch size to surpass the threshold $β_2^*$, and then trying $β_1< \sqrt{β_2}$. Our suggestions are supported by reports from several empirical studies, which observe improved LLM training performance when applying them.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需修改更新规则，Adam即可收敛
Adam是训练神经网络（包括大语言模型LLM）的默认算法。然而，\citet{reddi2019convergence} 提供了一个Adam发散的例子，引发了对其在AI模型训练中部署的担忧。我们发现该发散例子与实际应用之间存在关键不匹配：\citet{reddi2019convergence} 在选定Adam超参数$(β_1,β_2)$后才选择问题；而实际应用中通常先固定问题再调优$(β_1,β_2)$。本文证明，Adam在合适的、依赖于问题的超参数下可收敛。首先，我们证明当$β_2$较大且$β_1 < \sqrt{β_2}$时，Adam收敛。其次，当$β_2$较小时，我们指出存在$(β_1,β_2)$组合区域使Adam发散至无穷。我们的结果表明，Adam在$(β_1, β_2)$组合变化时存在从发散到收敛的相变。据我们所知，这是文献中首次在$(β_1,β_2)$二维平面上报告的相变，为Adam优化器提供了严格的理论保证。我们进一步指出，临界边界$(β_1^*, β_2^*)$依赖于问题，特别是依赖于批量大小。这为如何调优$β_1$和$β_2$提供了建议：当Adam表现不佳时，建议根据批量大小反向调高$β_2$以超越阈值$β_2^*$，然后尝试$β_1 < \sqrt{β_2}$。我们的建议得到了多项实证研究的支持，这些研究观察到应用上述方法可提升LLM训练性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses concerns that Adam may diverge during neural network training, as shown in prior work, by identifying a critical mismatch: previous divergence examples used hyperparameters (β₁, β₂) that were not tuned to the problem, whereas real-world practice often fixes the problem first before tuning these parameters. The authors prove that Adam converges under problem-dependent hyperparameter conditions: when β₂ is large and β₁ < √β₂, convergence is guaranteed; when β₂ is small, divergence can occur in certain (β₁, β₂) regions, revealing a phase transition between divergence and convergence. The critical boundary (β₁*, β₂*) depends on the problem and batch size, suggesting that tuning β₂ inversely with batch size to exceed β₂* and then setting β₁ < √β₂ can restore convergence. Empirical results from LLM training support these theoretical findings, showing improved performance with these tuning strategies.
该论文回应了Adam优化器可能在神经网络训练中发散的担忧，指出此前发散案例存在关键偏差：其先选定问题后固定超参数，而实际应用中常先解决收敛问题再调参。作者证明，当β₂较大且β₁ < √β₂时，Adam可收敛；当β₂较小时，存在特定(β₁, β₂)区域会导致发散。这是首次在(β₁, β₂)平面上发现收敛与发散的相变边界，表明收敛性依赖于问题与超参数的匹配。实验证明，通过将β₂按批次大小反向调高以突破临界值，再设置β₁ < √β₂，可显著提升大语言模型训练效果。
Learning from Synthetic Data Improves Multi-hop Reasoning
Authors: Anmol Kabra, Yilun Yin, Albert Gong, Kamilė Stankevičiūtė, Dongyoung Go, Johann Lee, Katie Z. Luo, Carla P. Gomes, Kilian Q. Weinberger
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:08:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:08:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has been shown to significantly boost reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) in math, coding, and multi-hop reasoning tasks. However, RL fine-tuning requires abundant high-quality verifiable data, often sourced from human annotations, generated from frontier LLMs, or scored by LLM-based verifiers. All three have considerable limitations: human-annotated datasets are small and expensive to curate, LLM-generated data is hallucination-prone and costly, and LLM-based verifiers are inaccurate and slow. In this work, we investigate a cheaper alternative: RL fine-tuning on rule-generated synthetic data for multi-hop reasoning tasks. We discover that LLMs fine-tuned on synthetic data perform significantly better on popular real-world question-answering benchmarks, despite the synthetic data containing only fictional knowledge. On stratifying performance by question difficulty, we find that synthetic data teaches LLMs to compose knowledge -- a fundamental and generalizable reasoning skill. Our work highlights rule-generated synthetic reasoning data as a free and scalable resource to improve LLM reasoning capabilities.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost and unreliability of real-world data for RL fine-tuning LLMs in multi-hop reasoning, this study explores using rule-generated synthetic data as a scalable alternative. The method trains LLMs via reinforcement learning on synthetic datasets created by logical rules, despite containing fictional knowledge. Experimental results show that models fine-tuned on this synthetic data outperform those trained on real data on standard benchmarks, especially on harder questions, demonstrating that synthetic data effectively teaches LLMs to compose knowledge—a core reasoning skill.
为了解决真实数据在强化学习微调大语言模型时成本高、质量不稳定的问题，本研究提出使用规则生成的合成数据作为替代方案。方法通过逻辑规则构建虚构知识的合成数据集，用以训练大语言模型的强化学习，从而避免人工标注或高成本的模型生成数据。实验结果表明，使用合成数据微调的模型在主流基准测试中表现更优，尤其在难度较高的问题上效果显著，证明合成数据能有效训练模型掌握知识组合这一核心推理能力，且该能力具有广泛迁移性。
Impossibility of Depth Reduction in Explainable Clustering
Authors: Chengyuan Deng, Surya Teja Gavva, Karthik C. S., Parth Patel, Adarsh Srinivasan
First: 2023-05-04T14:11:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:08:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Over the last few years Explainable Clustering has gathered a lot of attention. Dasgupta et al. [ICML'20] initiated the study of explainable $k$-means and $k$-median clustering problems where the explanation is captured by a threshold decision tree which partitions the space at each node using axis parallel hyperplanes. Recently, Laber et al. [Pattern Recognition'23] made a case to consider the depth of the decision tree as an additional complexity measure of interest. In this work, we prove that even when the input points are in the Euclidean plane, then any depth reduction in the explanation incurs unbounded loss in the $k$-means and $k$-median cost. Formally, we show that there exists a data set $X\subseteq \mathbb{R}^2$, for which there is a decision tree of depth $k-1$ whose $k$-means/$k$-median cost matches the optimal clustering cost of $X$, but every decision tree of depth less than $k-1$ has unbounded cost w.r.t. the optimal cost of clustering. We extend our results to the $k$-center objective as well, albeit with weaker guarantees.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the desire to understand the trade-off between decision tree depth and clustering cost in explainable clustering, this work proves that reducing the depth of an optimal decision tree explanation for k-means or k-median clustering in the Euclidean plane leads to unbounded cost increases. The authors construct a specific dataset in R² where an optimal solution requires a decision tree of depth k−1 to match the optimal clustering cost, but any shallower tree incurs arbitrarily high cost. This result holds for k-center as well, though with weaker guarantees.
为衡量聚类解释性，本文证明了降低决策树深度必然导致聚类代价无界增长。作者构造了一个欧氏平面中的数据集，其中最优的 $k$-means 或 $k$-median 聚类可由深度为 $k-1$ 的决策树解释，但任何深度更浅的树相对于最优代价都会产生任意高的代价。该结论对 $k$-center 也成立，但保证较弱。
S3OD: Towards Generalizable Salient Object Detection with Synthetic Data
Authors: Orest Kupyn, Hirokatsu Kataoka, Christian Rupprecht
First: 2025-10-24T16:10:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:08:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Salient object detection exemplifies data-bounded tasks where expensive pixel-precise annotations force separate model training for related subtasks like DIS and HR-SOD. We present a method that dramatically improves generalization through large-scale synthetic data generation and ambiguity-aware architecture. We introduce S3OD, a dataset of over 139,000 high-resolution images created through our multi-modal diffusion pipeline that extracts labels from diffusion and DINO-v3 features. The iterative generation framework prioritizes challenging categories based on model performance. We propose a streamlined multi-mask decoder that handles the inherent ambiguity in salient object detection by predicting multiple valid interpretations. Models trained only on synthetic data achieve 20-50% error reduction in cross-dataset generalization, while fine-tuned versions reach state-of-the-art performance across DIS and HR-SOD benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：S3OD：利用合成数据实现可泛化的显著物体检测
显著物体检测是数据受限任务的典型代表，昂贵的像素级标注迫使相关子任务（如DIS和HR-SOD）需单独训练模型。我们提出一种方法，通过大规模合成数据生成和模糊感知架构显著提升泛化能力。我们引入S3OD数据集，包含超过13.9万张高分辨率图像，通过多模态扩散管道生成，其标签由扩散与DINO-v3特征提取。迭代生成框架根据模型表现优先生成困难类别。我们提出一种简化多掩码解码器，通过预测多个有效解释来处理显著物体检测固有的模糊性。仅在合成数据上训练的模型在跨数据集泛化中错误率降低20-50%，微调版本在DIS和HR-SOD基准测试中达到最先进性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost and scarcity of pixel-precise annotations in salient object detection, this work introduces S3OD, a synthetic dataset of 139,000 high-resolution images generated via a multi-modal diffusion pipeline that leverages diffusion and DINO-v3 features to produce labels. The method employs an iterative generation strategy that focuses on challenging categories and a streamlined multi-mask decoder to handle inherent ambiguity in salient object detection. Experimental results show that models trained solely on synthetic data achieve 20–50% error reduction in cross-dataset generalization, and fine-tuned models reach state-of-the-art performance on both DIS and HR-SOD benchmarks.
为解决显著物体检测中像素级标注成本高、数据受限的问题，该研究提出S3OD数据集，通过多模态扩散管道生成13.9万张高分辨率合成图像，利用扩散与DINO-v3特征提取标签。方法采用迭代生成策略聚焦难例类别，并设计多掩码解码器以应对显著物体检测固有的模糊性，支持多合理解。实验表明，仅在合成数据上训练的模型在跨数据集泛化中误差降低20–50%，微调后模型在DIS与HR-SOD基准上达到当前最优性能。
Plan and Budget: Effective and Efficient Test-Time Scaling on Reasoning Large Language Models
Authors: Junhong Lin, Xinyue Zeng, Jie Zhu, Song Wang, Julian Shun, Jun Wu, Dawei Zhou
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-22T01:56:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:07:25+00:00
Comments: This work has been accepted to the ICLR 2026 (International Conference on Learning Representations)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success in complex reasoning tasks, but their inference remains computationally inefficient. We observe a common failure mode in many prevalent LLMs, overthinking, where models generate verbose and tangential reasoning traces even for simple queries. Recent work has tried to mitigate this by enforcing fixed token budgets, however, this can lead to underthinking, especially on harder problems. Through empirical analysis, we identify that this inefficiency often stems from unclear problem-solving strategies. To formalize this, we develop a theoretical model, BAM (Budget Allocation Model), which models reasoning as a sequence of sub-questions with varying uncertainty, and introduce the E3 metric to capture the trade-off between correctness and computation efficiency. Building on theoretical results from BAM, we propose Plan-and-Budget, a model-agnostic, test-time framework that decomposes complex queries into sub-questions and allocates token budgets based on estimated complexity using adaptive scheduling. Plan-and-Budget improves reasoning efficiency across a range of tasks and models, achieving up to 70% accuracy gains, 39% token reduction, and 193.8% improvement in E3. Notably, it improves the efficiency of a smaller model (DS-Qwen-32B) to match the efficiency of a larger model (DS-LLaMA-70B), demonstrating Plan-and-Budget's ability to close performance gaps without retraining. Our code is available at https://github.com/junhongmit/P-and-B.
中文标题/摘要
标题：计划与预算：推理大语言模型测试时的高效扩展
大语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理任务中取得了显著成功，但其推理过程仍存在计算效率低的问题。我们观察到许多主流LLMs普遍存在“过度思考”的失败模式，即即使面对简单查询，模型也会生成冗长且偏离主题的推理轨迹。近期研究尝试通过强制固定token预算来缓解此问题，但可能导致“思考不足”，尤其在困难问题上。通过实证分析，我们发现这种低效往往源于不清晰的问题解决策略。为此，我们构建了理论模型BAM（预算分配模型），将推理建模为具有不同不确定性的子问题序列，并引入E3指标以衡量正确性与计算效率之间的权衡。基于BAM的理论成果，我们提出Plan-and-Budget，这是一种模型无关的测试时框架，通过将复杂查询分解为子问题，并根据预估复杂度采用自适应调度分配token预算。Plan-and-Budget在多种任务和模型上显著提升推理效率，最高可实现70%的准确率提升、39%的token减少和193.8%的E3指标提升。值得注意的是，它使较小模型（DS-Qwen-32B）的效率提升至与较大模型（DS-LLaMA-70B）相当，证明Plan-and-Budget无需重训练即可弥合性能差距。代码已开源：https://github.com/junhongmit/P-and-B。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of large language models in reasoning tasks due to overthinking and underthinking, this work introduces Plan-and-Budget, a test-time framework that decomposes complex queries into sub-questions and allocates token budgets adaptively based on estimated complexity. Using a theoretical model called BAM and an E3 metric to evaluate correctness-efficiency trade-offs, the method dynamically schedules reasoning steps to avoid verbosity while preserving accuracy. Experiments show it achieves up to 70% accuracy gains, 39% token reduction, and 193.8% E3 improvement across models and tasks, even enabling a smaller model to match the efficiency of a larger one without retraining.
为解决大语言模型在推理任务中因过度思考或不足思考导致的效率低下问题，本文提出Plan-and-Budget框架，该框架将复杂问题分解为子问题，并根据预估复杂度动态分配token预算。基于BAM理论模型和E3指标，该方法通过自适应调度优化推理步骤，兼顾准确率与计算效率。实验表明，该方法在多个模型和任务上实现最高70%的准确率提升、39%的token减少和193.8%的E3指标提升，并使小模型效率可媲美大模型，无需重训练。
Detection-Gated Glottal Segmentation with Zero-Shot Cross-Dataset Transfer and Clinical Feature Extraction
Authors: Harikrishnan Unnikrishnan
First: 2026-03-02T17:05:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:05:41+00:00
Comments: for associated code see: https://github.com/hari-krishnan/openglottal
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Background: Accurate glottal segmentation in high-speed videoendoscopy (HSV) is essential for extracting kinematic biomarkers of laryngeal function. However, existing deep learning models often produce spurious artifacts in non-glottal frames and fail to generalize across different clinical settings. Methods: We propose a detection-gated pipeline that integrates a YOLOv8-based detector with a U-Net segmenter. A temporal consistency wrapper ensures robustness by suppressing false positives during glottal closure and instrument occlusion. The model was trained on a limited subset of the GIRAFE dataset (600 frames) and evaluated via zero-shot transfer on the large-scale BAGLS dataset. Results: The pipeline achieved state-of-the-art performance on the GIRAFE benchmark (DSC 0.81) and demonstrated superior generalizability on BAGLS (DSC 0.85, in-distribution) without institutional fine-tuning. Downstream validation on a 65-subject clinical cohort confirmed that automated kinematic features (Open Quotient, coefficient of variation) remained consistent with established clinical benchmarks. The coefficient of variation (CV) of the glottal area was found to be a significant marker for distinguishing healthy from pathological vocal function (p=0.006). Conclusions: The detection-gated architecture provides a lightweight, computationally efficient solution (~35 frames/s) for real-time clinical use. By enabling robust zero-shot transfer, this framework facilitates the standardized, large-scale extraction of clinical biomarkers across diverse endoscopy platforms. Code, trained weights, and evaluation scripts are released at https://github.com/hari-krishnan/openglottal.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate glottal segmentation in high-speed videoendoscopy to extract reliable laryngeal biomarkers, the study introduces a detection-gated pipeline combining YOLOv8 for detection and U-Net for segmentation, enhanced by a temporal consistency wrapper to suppress false positives. Trained on a small subset of the GIRAFE dataset, the model achieved state-of-the-art Dice Score (DSC 0.81) on GIRAFE and demonstrated strong zero-shot generalization on the larger BAGLS dataset (DSC 0.85). Clinical validation on 65 subjects confirmed that automated kinematic features like Open Quotient and coefficient of variation matched established benchmarks, with the coefficient of variation showing statistical significance in distinguishing healthy from pathological vocal function (p=0.006).
为解决高分辨率视频喉镜中声带分割不准确及跨临床数据集泛化能力差的问题，作者提出一种检测门控管道，结合YOLOv8检测器与U-Net分割器，并通过时间一致性模块抑制声带闭合和器械遮挡时的假阳性。该模型在GIRAFE小数据集上训练，于GIRAFE基准测试中达到最优Dice分数（0.81），并在未微调情况下于大规模BAGLS数据集实现零样本迁移（DSC 0.85）。对65名受试者的临床验证表明，自动提取的运动学特征（如开口率、声带面积变异系数）与临床标准一致，其中变异系数在区分健康与病理性发声功能时具有统计学意义（p=0.006），且系统运行速度达每秒35帧，满足实时临床需求。
Modeling Grammatical Hypothesis Testing in Young Learners: A Sequence-Based Learning Analytics Study of Morphosyntactic Reasoning in an Interactive Game
Authors: Thierry Geoffre, Trystan Geoffre
First: 2026-03-02T17:04:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:04:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study investigates grammatical reasoning in primary school learners through a sequence-based learning analytics approach, leveraging fine-grained action sequences from an interactive game targeting morphosyntactic agreement in French. Unlike traditional assessments that rely on final answers, we treat each slider movement as a hypothesis-testing action, capturing real-time cognitive strategies during sentence construction. Analyzing 597 gameplay sessions (9,783 actions) from 100 students aged 8-11 in authentic classroom settings, we introduce Hamming distance to quantify proximity to valid grammatical solutions and examine convergence patterns across exercises with varying levels of difficulty. Results reveal that determiners and verbs are key sites of difficulty, with action sequences deviating from left-to-right usual treatment. This suggests learners often fix the verb first and adjust preceding elements. Exercises with fewer solutions exhibit slower and more erratic convergence, while changes in the closest valid solution indicate dynamic hypothesis revision. Our findings demonstrate how sequence-based analytics can uncover hidden dimensions of linguistic reasoning, offering a foundation for real-time scaffolding and teacher-facing tools in linguistically diverse classrooms.
Summary / 总结
This study aims to understand grammatical reasoning in young learners by analyzing fine-grained action sequences from an interactive French grammar game, treating each slider movement as a hypothesis-testing step rather than a final answer. Using Hamming distance to measure proximity to correct morphosyntactic solutions, researchers analyzed 9,783 actions across 597 sessions from 100 students aged 8-11. Results show that learners frequently prioritize verb correction over determiners, deviating from left-to-right processing, and that exercises with fewer solutions lead to slower, more erratic convergence. The study highlights how sequence-based analytics can reveal dynamic hypothesis revision and inform real-time instructional support.
本研究旨在通过分析小学阶段学生在法语语法互动游戏中细粒度的操作序列，理解其句法推理过程，将每次滑动视为假设检验行为而非最终答案。研究采用汉明距离量化操作与正确句法结构的接近程度，分析100名8至11岁学生597次游戏会话中的9783次操作。结果发现，学习者常优先调整动词，再修正前项成分，且解法数量少的练习收敛更慢、更不稳定；操作序列显示动态假设修正。该研究证明序列分析可揭示隐性认知策略，为实时教学支持与教师工具提供基础。
$π$-StepNFT: Wider Space Needs Finer Steps in Online RL for Flow-based VLAs
Authors: Siting Wang, Xiaofeng Wang, Zheng Zhu, Minnan Pei, Xinyu Cui, Cheng Deng, Jian Zhao, Guan Huang, Haifeng Zhang, Jun Wang
First: 2026-03-02T17:04:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:04:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Flow-based vision-language-action (VLA) models excel in embodied control but suffer from intractable likelihoods during multi-step sampling, hindering online reinforcement learning. We propose \textbf{\textit{$\boldsymbolπ$-StepNFT}} (Step-wise Negative-aware Fine-Tuning), a critic-and-likelihood-free framework that requires only a single forward pass per optimization step and eliminates auxiliary value networks. We identify that wider exploration spaces necessitate finer-grained, step-wise guidance for alignment. Empirically, $π$-StepNFT unlocks latent potential on LIBERO with competitive few-shot robustness. Moreover, it achieves superior generalization on ManiSkill, outperforming value-based baselines in OOD scenarios by preventing overfitting to multimodal features. This property offers a scalable solution promising for complex real-world applications.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge that flow-based vision-language-action models struggle with multi-step sampling due to intractable likelihoods in online reinforcement learning, the authors propose π-StepNFT, a critic- and likelihood-free framework requiring only one forward pass per optimization step. The method introduces step-wise, negative-aware fine-tuning to provide finer-grained guidance in wider exploration spaces, enabling better alignment without auxiliary value networks. Experimental results show π-StepNFT achieves competitive few-shot robustness on LIBERO and superior generalization on ManiSkill, particularly in out-of-distribution scenarios, by avoiding overfitting to multimodal features.
为解决流式视觉-语言-动作模型在在线强化学习中因多步采样时似然不可计算而导致的性能瓶颈，本文提出π-StepNFT方法，该方法无需价值网络和似然估计，每步优化仅需一次前向传播。其核心思想是针对更宽泛的探索空间，采用细粒度、分步引导以提升对齐效果。实验表明，π-StepNFT在LIBERO上实现媲美少样本鲁棒性，在ManiSkill上显著优于基于价值的基线方法，尤其在分布外场景中通过避免对多模态特征过拟合，展现出更强的泛化能力。
What Exactly do Children Receive in Language Acquisition? A Case Study on CHILDES with Automated Detection of Filler-Gap Dependencies
Authors: Zhenghao Herbert Zhou, William Dai, Maya Viswanathan, Simon Charlow, R. Thomas McCoy, Robert Frank
First: 2026-03-02T17:03:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:03:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Children's acquisition of filler-gap dependencies has been argued by some to depend on innate grammatical knowledge, while others suggest that the distributional evidence available in child-directed speech suffices. Unfortunately, the relevant input is difficult to quantify at scale with fine granularity, making this question difficult to resolve. We present a system that identifies three core filler-gap constructions in spoken English corpora -- matrix wh-questions, embedded wh-questions, and relative clauses -- and further identifies the extraction site (i.e., subject vs. object vs. adjunct). Our approach combines constituency and dependency parsing, leveraging their complementary strengths for construction classification and extraction site identification. We validate the system on human-annotated data and find that it scores well across most categories. Applying the system to 57 English CHILDES corpora, we are able to characterize children's filler-gap input and their filler-gap production trajectories over the course of development, including construction-specific frequencies and extraction-site asymmetries. The resulting fine-grained labels enable future work in both acquisition and computational studies, which we demonstrate with a case study using filtered corpus training with language models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：儿童语言习得中究竟获得了什么？基于CHILDES语料库的填空-空位依赖关系自动化检测案例研究
一些学者认为儿童习得填空-空位依赖关系依赖于先天语法知识，而另一些学者则认为儿童口语中可获得的分布证据已足够。不幸的是，相关输入难以大规模精细量化，使该问题难以解决。我们提出一种系统，用于识别英语口语语料库中的三种核心填空-空位结构——矩阵疑问句、嵌入式疑问句和关系从句，并进一步识别提取位置（即主语、宾语或附加成分）。该方法结合了成分句法和依存句法分析，利用二者互补优势进行结构分类和提取位置识别。我们在人工标注数据上验证该系统，发现其在多数类别中表现良好。将该系统应用于57个英语CHILDES语料库，我们能够刻画儿童填空-空位输入及其在发展过程中的产出轨迹，包括结构特异性频率和提取位置不对称性。所得精细标签为未来习得与计算研究提供了支持，我们通过使用过滤语料库训练语言模型的案例研究加以验证。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the debate over whether children acquire filler-gap dependencies through innate grammar or from distributional patterns in child-directed speech, by developing an automated system to detect three core filler-gap constructions — matrix wh-questions, embedded wh-questions, and relative clauses — and their extraction sites (subject, object, adjunct). The method combines constituency and dependency parsing to classify constructions and identify extraction sites, validated on human-annotated data with strong performance. Applied to 57 CHILDES corpora, the system reveals fine-grained patterns of children’s exposure and production, including construction-specific frequencies and extraction-site asymmetries, enabling future research in language acquisition and computational modeling.
该研究旨在解决儿童是否通过先天语法或儿童语言输入中的分布模式习得填空-空位依赖结构的问题，开发了一套自动化系统，用于识别三种核心结构——矩阵疑问句、嵌入疑问句和关系从句及其提取位置（主语、宾语、附加语）。该方法结合了成分句法与依存句法解析，以分类结构并识别提取位置，经人工标注数据验证效果良好。应用于57个CHILDES语料库后，系统揭示了儿童接触与产出的细粒度模式，包括结构特异性频率和提取位置不对称性，为语言习得与计算建模研究提供了基础。
GenDB: The Next Generation of Query Processing -- Synthesized, Not Engineered
Authors: Jiale Lao, Immanuel Trummer
First: 2026-03-02T17:03:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:03:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional query processing relies on engines that are carefully optimized and engineered by many experts. However, new techniques and user requirements evolve rapidly, and existing systems often cannot keep pace. At the same time, these systems are difficult to extend due to their internal complexity, and developing new systems requires substantial engineering effort and cost. In this paper, we argue that recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) are starting to shape the next generation of query processing systems. We propose using LLMs to synthesize execution code for each incoming query, instead of continuously building, extending, and maintaining complex query processing engines. As a proof of concept, we present GenDB, an LLM-powered agentic system that generates instance-optimized and customized query execution code tailored to specific data, workloads, and hardware resources. We implemented an early prototype of GenDB that uses Claude Code Agent as the underlying component in the multi-agent system, and we evaluate it on OLAP workloads. We use queries from the well-known TPC-H benchmark and also construct a new benchmark designed to reduce potential data leakage from LLM training data. We compare GenDB with state-of-the-art query engines, including DuckDB, Umbra, MonetDB, ClickHouse, and PostgreSQL. GenDB achieves significantly better performance than these systems. Finally, we discuss the current limitations of GenDB and outline future extensions and related research challenges.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the rapid evolution of query processing needs and the high cost of maintaining traditional engines, this paper proposes GenDB, a system that leverages Large Language Models to synthesize custom execution code for each query rather than relying on pre-engineered systems. Using a multi-agent setup with Claude Code Agent, GenDB generates instance-optimized query plans tailored to specific data, workloads, and hardware. Evaluated against state-of-the-art engines like DuckDB, ClickHouse, and PostgreSQL on TPC-H and a new leakage-reduced benchmark, GenDB consistently outperforms them in execution speed and efficiency, demonstrating the viability of LLM-driven synthesis over traditional engineering.
为应对传统查询引擎难以扩展、维护成本高的问题，本文提出GenDB系统，利用大语言模型动态合成每个查询的定制化执行代码，而非依赖人工构建的复杂引擎。系统采用多智能体架构，以Claude Code Agent为核心，根据具体数据、负载和硬件生成优化执行方案。在TPC-H基准及自建防数据泄露测试集上，与DuckDB、ClickHouse等主流引擎对比，GenDB在执行效率上显著领先，验证了基于LLM合成方案的可行性。
From Pixels to Patches: Pooling Strategies for Earth Embeddings
Authors: Isaac Corley, Caleb Robinson, Inbal Becker-Reshef, Juan M. Lavista Ferres
First: 2026-03-02T17:03:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:03:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As geospatial foundation models shift from patch-level to pixel-level embeddings, practitioners must aggregate thousands of pixel vectors into patch representations that preserve class-discriminative signal while matching downstream label resolution. The default choice, mean pooling, discards within-patch variability and can drop accuracy by more than 10% under spatial shift. To evaluate this effect, we introduce EuroSAT-Embed: 81,000 embedding GeoTIFFs derived from three foundation models: AlphaEarth, OlmoEarth, and Tessera. We benchmark 11 training-free and 2 parametric pooling methods under both random and geographically disjoint test splits. Our results show that richer pooling schemes reduce the geographic generalization gap by up to 40% relative to mean pooling and increases accuracy by up to 5% on spatial splits. We recommend Generalized Mean Pooling (GeM) as a drop-in replacement for mean pooling: it improves accuracy without increasing embedding dimensionality. For maximum accuracy, Stats pooling (concatenation of min/max/mean/std pooling) performs best at 4x the embedding size. We further find that pooling effectiveness varies across embedding sources and that higher-dimensional embeddings benefit most from distributional statistics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从像素到块：地球嵌入的池化策略
随着地理空间基础模型从块级向像素级嵌入转变，从业者必须将数千个像素向量聚合为块表示，以在保持类别判别信号的同时匹配下游标签分辨率。默认选择的均值池化会丢弃块内变异性，在空间位移情况下可能导致准确率下降超过10%。为评估此效应，我们引入EuroSAT-Embed：81,000个源自三个基础模型（AlphaEarth、OlmoEarth和Tessera）的嵌入GeoTIFF。我们在随机和地理上不相交的测试分割下，对11种无训练池化方法和2种参数化池化方法进行基准测试。结果表明，更丰富的池化方案相比均值池化可将地理泛化差距减少高达40%，并在空间分割上提升准确率高达5%。我们推荐广义均值池化（GeM）作为均值池化的直接替代方案：它在不增加嵌入维度的情况下提升准确率。为获得最高准确率，统计池化（最小值/最大值/均值/标准差池化的拼接）在嵌入维度为4倍时表现最佳。我们进一步发现，池化效果因嵌入源而异，且高维嵌入最受益于分布统计。
Summary / 总结
As geospatial models transition from patch-level to pixel-level embeddings, aggregating thousands of pixel vectors into patch representations without losing class-discriminative signal becomes critical. The paper evaluates 13 pooling methods—11 training-free and 2 parametric—on EuroSAT-Embed, a dataset of 81,000 embeddings from three foundation models. Results show that mean pooling suffers accuracy drops exceeding 10% under spatial shifts, while richer methods like Generalized Mean Pooling (GeM) reduce the geographic generalization gap by up to 40% and boost accuracy by up to 5%. Stats pooling, which concatenates min/max/mean/std, achieves highest accuracy but at 4x embedding size. The study also finds that pooling effectiveness varies by model and that higher-dimensional embeddings benefit most from statistical pooling.
随着地理空间模型从块级转向像素级嵌入，如何在不丢失类别判别信号的前提下，将数千个像素向量聚合为块级表示成为关键。论文在EuroSAT-Embed数据集（81,000个来自三个基础模型的GeoTIFF嵌入）上评估了13种池化方法，在随机和地理不重叠测试分割下进行对比。结果显示，均值池化在空间偏移下准确率下降超10%，而更丰富的池化策略如广义均值池化（GeM）可将地理泛化差距缩小40%、准确率提升5%。Stats池化（拼接最小值/最大值/均值/标准差）在4倍嵌入维度下表现最佳，但需更多内存。研究还发现，池化效果因嵌入源而异，高维嵌入最受益于分布统计量。
MMNavAgent: Multi-Magnification WSI Navigation Agent for Clinically Consistent Whole-Slide Analysis
Authors: Zhengyang Xu, Han Li, Jingsong Liu, Linrui Xie, Xun Ma, Xin You, Shihui Zu, Ayako Ito, Xinyu Hao, Hongming Xu, Shaohua Kevin Zhou, Nassir Navab, Peter J. Schüffler
First: 2026-03-02T17:02:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:02:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent AI navigation approaches aim to improve Whole-Slide Image (WSI) diagnosis by modeling spatial exploration and selecting diagnostically relevant regions, yet most operate at a single fixed magnification or rely on predefined magnification traversal. In clinical practice, pathologists examine slides across multiple magnifications and selectively inspect only necessary scales, dynamically integrating global and cellular evidence in a sequential manner. This mismatch prevents existing methods from modeling cross-magnification interactions and adaptive magnification selection inherent to real diagnostic workflows. To these, we propose a clinically consistent Multi-Magnification WSI Navigation Agent (MMNavAgent) that explicitly models multi magnification interaction and adaptive magnification selection. Specifically, we introduce a Cross-Magnification navigation Tool (CMT) that aggregates contextual information from adjacent magnifications to enhance discriminative representations along the navigation path. We further introduce a Magnification Selection Tool (MST) that leverages memory-driven reasoning within the agent framework to enable interactive and adaptive magnification selection, mimicking the sequential decision process of pathologists. Extensive experiments on a public dataset demonstrate improved diagnostic performance, with 1.45% gain of AUC and 2.93% gain of BACC over a non-agent baseline. Code will be public upon acceptance.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the clinical need for pathologists to navigate Whole-Slide Images (WSIs) across multiple magnifications adaptively, this work proposes MMNavAgent, a navigation agent that models cross-magnification interactions and dynamic magnification selection. The agent integrates a Cross-Magnification Tool (CMT) to fuse contextual information from adjacent magnifications and a Magnification Selection Tool (MST) that uses memory-driven reasoning to mimic pathologists’ sequential decision-making. Experiments on a public dataset show that MMNavAgent improves diagnostic performance, achieving a 1.45% increase in AUC and a 2.93% increase in BACC compared to a non-agent baseline.
为解决现有导航方法无法模拟临床病理学家动态切换放大倍数的缺陷，本文提出MMNavAgent，通过引入跨放大倍数导航工具（CMT）和放大倍数选择工具（MST），显式建模多倍率交互与自适应选择机制。实验表明，该方法在公开数据集上较非代理基线模型AUC提升1.45%，BACC提升2.93%，验证了其在诊断一致性上的优势。
When an AI Judges Your Work: The Hidden Costs of Algorithmic Assessment
Authors: David Almog, Lucas Lippman, Daniel Martin
First: 2026-03-02T17:01:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:01:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We use an online experiment with a real work task to study whether workers change their behavior when they know AI will be used to judge their work instead of humans. We find that individuals produce a higher quantity of output when they are assigned an AI evaluator. However, controlling for quantity, the quality of their output is lower, regardless of whether quality is measured using humans or LLM grades. We also find that workers are more likely to use external tools, including LLMs, when they know AI is used to judge their work instead of humans. However, the increase in external tool use does not appear to explain the differences in quantity or quality across treatments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当人工智能评判你的工作：算法评估的隐性代价
我们通过一个在线实验，以真实工作任务为研究对象，探讨工人在得知其工作将由人工智能而非人类评判时是否会改变行为。研究发现，分配AI评估者时，个体产出数量更高。但在控制产出数量后，无论使用人类还是大语言模型（LLM）评分，其产出质量均较低。此外，工人在得知AI将评判其工作时更倾向于使用外部工具（包括LLM），但这种工具使用频率的增加并未解释不同处理组间产出数量或质量的差异。

This study investigates how workers adjust their behavior when aware that AI, rather than human evaluators, will judge their work. Using an online experiment with a real task, researchers found that workers produced more output under AI evaluation, yet the quality of that output was lower, whether assessed by humans or large language models. Additionally, workers were more likely to use external tools like LLMs when AI was involved, but this increased tool use did not account for the observed differences in quantity or quality.

Adversarial Déjà Vu: Jailbreak Dictionary Learning for Stronger Generalization to Unseen Attacks
Authors: Mahavir Dabas, Tran Huynh, Nikhil Reddy Billa, Jiachen T. Wang, Peng Gao, Charith Peris, Yao Ma, Rahul Gupta, Ming Jin, Prateek Mittal, Ruoxi Jia
First: 2025-10-24T17:37:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:59:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks that bypass safety guardrails to elicit harmful outputs. Defending against novel jailbreaks represents a critical challenge in AI safety. Adversarial training -- designed to make models robust against worst-case perturbations -- has been the dominant paradigm for adversarial robustness. However, due to optimization challenges and difficulties in defining realistic threat models, adversarial training methods often fail on newly developed jailbreaks in practice. This paper proposes a new paradigm for improving robustness against unseen jailbreaks, centered on the Adversarial Déjà Vu hypothesis: novel jailbreaks are not fundamentally new, but largely recombinations of adversarial skills from previous attacks. We study this hypothesis through a large-scale analysis of 32 attack papers published over two years. Using an automated pipeline, we extract and compress adversarial skills into a sparse dictionary of primitives, with LLMs generating human-readable descriptions. Our analysis reveals that unseen attacks can be effectively explained as sparse compositions of earlier skills, with explanatory power increasing monotonically as skill coverage grows. Guided by this insight, we introduce Adversarial Skill Compositional Training (ASCoT), which trains on diverse compositions of skill primitives rather than isolated attack instances. ASCoT substantially improves robustness to unseen attacks, including multi-turn jailbreaks, while maintaining low over-refusal rates. We also demonstrate that expanding adversarial skill coverage, not just data scale, is key to defending against novel attacks. \textcolor{red}{\textbf{Warning: This paper contains content that may be harmful or offensive in nature.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对抗性 déjà vu：通过越狱攻击字典学习实现对未知攻击更强的泛化能力
大型语言模型仍易受越狱攻击影响，此类攻击可绕过安全限制以生成有害输出。防御新型越狱攻击是人工智能安全的关键挑战。对抗性训练——旨在使模型对最坏情况扰动具备鲁棒性——是当前对抗鲁棒性的主流范式。然而，由于优化困难及现实威胁模型定义的挑战，对抗性训练方法在实际中常无法应对新开发的越狱攻击。本文提出一种新范式，以“对抗性 déjà vu”假设为核心：新型越狱攻击并非根本全新，而是此前攻击中对抗技能的重组。我们通过对两年内32篇攻击论文的大规模分析，验证该假设。通过自动化流程，我们将对抗技能提取并压缩为稀疏原始技能字典，由大语言模型生成可读描述。分析表明，未知攻击可有效解释为早期技能的稀疏组合，且随着技能覆盖度增加，解释力单调提升。基于此洞察，我们提出对抗技能组合训练（ASCoT），其训练方式为多样化的技能原始组合，而非孤立攻击实例。ASCoT显著提升对未知攻击（包括多轮越狱攻击）的鲁棒性，同时保持较低的过度拒绝率。我们还证明，扩展对抗技能覆盖范围，而非单纯扩大数据规模，是防御新型攻击的关键。\textcolor{red}{\textbf{警告：本文内容可能包含有害或冒犯性信息。}}
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the persistent vulnerability of large language models to novel jailbreak attacks, this paper proposes a new defense paradigm based on the hypothesis that unseen attacks are recombinations of previously seen adversarial skills. The method, Adversarial Skill Compositional Training (ASCoT), extracts and compresses adversarial skills from 32 attack papers into a sparse dictionary of primitives, then trains models on diverse compositions of these primitives rather than isolated attacks. Experimental results show ASCoT significantly improves robustness against unseen jailbreaks—including multi-turn attacks—while maintaining low refusal rates, demonstrating that expanding skill coverage, not just data volume, is critical for defending against novel adversarial inputs.
为应对大型语言模型对新型越狱攻击的持续脆弱性，本文提出基于“对抗性 déjà vu”假设的新防御范式，即新攻击本质上是已有对抗技能的重组。方法“对抗技能组合训练”（ASCoT）从32篇攻击论文中提取并压缩对抗技能为稀疏原始技能字典，再以这些原始技能的多样组合训练模型而非孤立攻击样本。实验表明，ASCoT显著提升对未知越狱攻击（包括多轮攻击）的鲁棒性，同时保持低拒绝率，证明扩大对抗技能覆盖范围而非单纯增加数据量，是防御新型攻击的关键。
Cognitive Prosthetic: An AI-Enabled Multimodal System for Episodic Recall in Knowledge Work
Authors: Lawrence Obiuwevwi, Krzysztof J. Rechowicz, Vikas Ashok, Sachin Shetty, Sampath Jayarathna
First: 2026-03-02T16:58:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:58:53+00:00
Comments: CHI EA '26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern knowledge workplaces increasingly strain human episodic memory as individuals navigate fragmented attention, overlapping meetings, and multimodal information streams. Existing workplace tools provide partial support through note-taking or analytics but rarely integrate cognitive, physiological, and attentional context into retrievable memory representations. This paper presents the Cognitive Prosthetic Multimodal System (CPMS) --an AI-enabled proof-of-concept designed to support episodic recall in knowledge work through structured episodic capture and natural language retrieval. CPMS synchronizes speech transcripts, physiological signals, and gaze behavior into temporally aligned, JSON-based episodic records processed locally for privacy. Beyond data logging, the system includes a web-based retrieval interface that allows users to query past workplace experiences using natural language, referencing semantic content, time, attentional focus, or physiological state. We present CPMS as a functional proof-of-concept demonstrating the technical feasibility of transforming heterogeneous sensor data into queryable episodic memories. The system is designed to be modular, supporting operation with partial sensor configurations, and incorporates privacy safeguards for workplace deployment. This work contributes an end-to-end, privacy-aware architecture for AI-enabled memory augmentation in workplace settings.
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the growing strain on human episodic memory in modern knowledge work due to fragmented attention and multimodal information overload, this paper introduces the Cognitive Prosthetic Multimodal System (CPMS), an AI-enabled proof-of-concept that captures and retrieves episodic workplace experiences. CPMS synchronizes speech transcripts, physiological signals, and gaze data into temporally aligned JSON records processed locally to preserve privacy, then enables natural language queries over these records via a web interface. Experimental results demonstrate the system’s technical feasibility in transforming heterogeneous sensor data into queryable episodic memories, with modular design and partial sensor compatibility supporting real-world deployment.
为应对现代知识工作中因注意力碎片化和多模态信息过载导致的人类情景记忆负担，本文提出认知假体多模态系统（CPMS），该系统通过同步语音转录、生理信号与注视行为，生成本地处理、隐私保护的JSON格式情景记录。系统配备自然语言检索界面，支持用户按语义内容、时间、注意力或生理状态查询过往工作经历。实验结果验证了CPMS将异构传感器数据转化为可查询情景记忆的技术可行性，同时具备模块化设计与隐私保障，适用于真实职场部署。
InstructPro: Natural Language Guided Ligand-Binding Protein Design
Authors: Zhenqiao Song, Ramith Hettiarachchi, Chuan Li, Jianwen Xie, Lei Li
First: 2025-06-11T02:15:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:58:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The de novo design of ligand-binding proteins with tailored functions is essential for advancing biotechnology and molecular medicine, yet existing AI approaches are limited by scarce protein-ligand complex data. To circumvent this data bottleneck, we leverage the abundant natural language descriptions characterizing protein-ligand interactions. Here, we introduce InstructPro, a family of generative models that design proteins following the guidance of natural language instructions and ligand formulas. InstructPro produces protein sequences consistent with specified function descriptions and ligand targets. To enable training and evaluation, we develop InstructProBench, a large-scale dataset of 9.6 million (function description, ligand, protein) triples. We train two model variants -- InstructPro-1B and InstructPro-3B -- that substantially outperform strong baselines. InstructPro-1B achieves an AlphaFold3 ipTM of 0.918 and a binding affinity of -8.764 on seen ligands, while maintaining robust performance in a zero-shot setting with scores of 0.869 and -6.713, respectively. These results are accompanied by novelty scores of 70.1% and 68.8%, underscoring the model's ability to generalize beyond the training set. Furthermore, the model yields a superior binding free energy of -20.9 kcal/mol and an average of 5.82 intermolecular hydrogen bonds, validating its proficiency in designing high-affinity ligand-binding proteins. Notably, scaling to InstructPro-3B further improves the zero-shot ipTM to 0.882, binding affinity to -6.797, and binding free energy to -25.8 kcal/mol, demonstrating clear performance gains associated with increased model capacity. These findings highlight the power of natural language-guided generative models to mitigate the data bottlenecks in traditional structure-based methods, significantly broadening the scope of de novo protein design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InstructPro：自然语言引导的配体结合蛋白设计
为推进生物技术和分子医学，设计具有定制功能的全新配体结合蛋白至关重要，但现有AI方法受限于蛋白质-配体复合物数据稀缺。为克服这一数据瓶颈，我们利用大量描述蛋白质-配体相互作用的自然语言文本。本文介绍InstructPro，一系列根据自然语言指令和配体公式设计蛋白的生成模型。InstructPro可生成与指定功能描述和配体靶点一致的蛋白序列。为支持训练与评估，我们构建了InstructProBench数据集，包含960万组（功能描述、配体、蛋白）三元组。我们训练了两个模型变体——InstructPro-1B和InstructPro-3B，显著优于强基线模型。InstructPro-1B在已见配体上实现AlphaFold3 ipTM为0.918、结合亲和力为-8.764，零样本设置下分别保持0.869和-6.713的性能，新颖性评分分别为70.1%和68.8%，表明模型具备超越训练集的能力。此外，模型生成结合自由能为-20.9 kcal/mol，平均5.82个分子间氢键，验证其设计高亲和力配体结合蛋白的能力。值得注意的是，扩展至InstructPro-3B进一步提升零样本ipTM至0.882、结合亲和力至-6.797、结合自由能至-25.8 kcal/mol，表明模型容量增加带来显著性能提升。这些成果凸显了自然语言引导生成模型在缓解传统基于结构方法数据瓶颈方面的潜力，显著拓展了从头蛋白设计的范围。

Trained on InstructProBench—a dataset of 9.6 million (description, ligand, protein) triples—the model variants InstructPro-1B and InstructPro-3B outperform baselines, achieving high ipTM scores (0.918 and 0.882) and binding affinities (-8.764 and -6.797) on seen ligands, with strong zero-shot generalization (ipTM 0.869, affinity -6.713). The models also generate proteins with high binding free energy (-20.9 to -25.8 kcal/mol) and average 5.82 hydrogen bonds, demonstrating their ability to produce novel, high-affinity binders with 70.1% and 68.8% novelty scores.
为缓解蛋白-配体复合物数据稀缺对AI驱动从头设计的限制，InstructPro利用自然语言指令和配体公式引导生成模型设计配体结合蛋白。基于包含960万组（描述、配体、蛋白）三元组的InstructProBench数据集训练的InstructPro-1B与InstructPro-3B模型显著优于基线方法，在已见配体上分别取得0.918和0.882的ipTM、-8.764和-6.797的结合亲和力，零样本场景下仍保持0.869和-6.713的性能。更大模型还实现-25.8 kcal/mol的结合自由能与平均5.82个氢键，70.1%和68.8%的新颖性评分表明其具备超越训练数据的泛化能力。
ToProVAR: Efficient Visual Autoregressive Modeling via Tri-Dimensional Entropy-Aware Semantic Analysis and Sparsity Optimization
Authors: Jiayu Chen, Ruoyu Lin, Zihao Zheng, Jingxin Li, Maoliang Li, Guojie Luo, Xiang Chen
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-26T12:36:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:58:25+00:00
Comments: ToProVAR is honored to be accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Visual Autoregressive(VAR) models enhance generation quality but face a critical efficiency bottleneck in later stages. In this paper, we present a novel optimization framework for VAR models that fundamentally differs from prior approaches such as FastVAR and SkipVAR. Instead of relying on heuristic skipping strategies, our method leverages attention entropy to characterize the semantic projections across different dimensions of the model architecture. This enables precise identification of parameter dynamics under varying token granularity levels, semantic scopes, and generation scales. Building on this analysis, we further uncover sparsity patterns along three critical dimensions-token, layer, and scale-and propose a set of fine-grained optimization strategies tailored to these patterns. Extensive evaluation demonstrates that our approach achieves aggressive acceleration of the generation process while significantly preserving semantic fidelity and fine details, outperforming traditional methods in both efficiency and quality. Experiments on Infinity-2B and Infinity-8B models demonstrate that ToProVAR achieves up to 3.4x acceleration with minimal quality loss, effectively mitigating the issues found in prior work. Our code will be made publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ToProVAR：通过三维熵感知语义分析与稀疏性优化实现高效的视觉自回归建模
视觉自回归（VAR）模型虽能提升生成质量，但在后期阶段面临关键效率瓶颈。本文提出一种全新的VAR模型优化框架，与FastVAR和SkipVAR等先前方法有本质区别。该方法不依赖启发式跳过策略，而是利用注意力熵刻画模型架构不同维度间的语义投影，从而精准识别在不同token粒度、语义范围和生成尺度下参数的动态变化。基于此分析，我们进一步揭示了沿三个关键维度（token、层、尺度）的稀疏模式，并提出针对这些模式的细粒度优化策略。大量实验表明，我们的方法在显著保持语义保真度和细节的同时，大幅加速生成过程，在效率与质量上均优于传统方法。在Infinity-2B和Infinity-8B模型上的实验显示，ToProVAR可实现最高3.4倍加速，且质量损失极小，有效缓解了先前方法存在的问题。代码将公开发布。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the efficiency bottleneck in visual autoregressive models, this paper introduces ToProVAR, a framework that uses tri-dimensional entropy-aware semantic analysis to identify parameter sparsity patterns across token, layer, and scale dimensions. Instead of heuristic skipping, it leverages attention entropy to precisely characterize semantic projections and dynamics under varying generation scales. The method then applies fine-grained optimization strategies aligned with these sparsity patterns, resulting in significant acceleration without compromising semantic fidelity. Experiments on Infinity-2B and Infinity-8B models show up to 3.4x speedup with minimal quality loss, outperforming prior methods like FastVAR and SkipVAR in both efficiency and output quality.
为解决视觉自回归模型生成效率瓶颈，本文提出ToProVAR框架，通过三维熵感知语义分析识别参数在token、层和尺度维度上的稀疏模式，而非依赖启发式跳过策略，而是利用注意力熵精确刻画不同生成尺度下的语义投影与参数动态。基于此分析，该方法提出针对稀疏模式的细粒度优化策略，显著加速生成过程同时保持语义保真度。在Infinity-2B和Infinity-8B模型上的实验表明，该方法最高可实现3.4倍加速，且质量损失极小，优于FastVAR和SkipVAR等传统方法在效率与质量上的表现。
Exploring Plan Space through Conversation: An Agentic Framework for LLM-Mediated Explanations in Planning
Authors: Guilhem Fouilhé, Rebecca Eifler, Antonin Poché, Sylvie Thiébaux, Nicholas Asher
First: 2026-03-02T16:58:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:58:18+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When automating plan generation for a real-world sequential decision problem, the goal is often not to replace the human planner, but to facilitate an iterative reasoning and elicitation process, where the human's role is to guide the AI planner according to their preferences and expertise. In this context, explanations that respond to users' questions are crucial to improve their understanding of potential solutions and increase their trust in the system. To enable natural interaction with such a system, we present a multi-agent Large Language Model (LLM) architecture that is agnostic to the explanation framework and enables user- and context-dependent interactive explanations. We also describe an instantiation of this framework for goal-conflict explanations, which we use to conduct a user study comparing the LLM-powered interaction with a baseline template-based explanation interface.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过对话探索计划空间：一种用于规划中LLM介导解释的代理框架
在自动化现实世界序列决策问题的计划生成时，目标通常不是取代人类规划者，而是促进一种迭代推理与引导过程，其中人类的作用是根据其偏好和专业知识引导AI规划者。在此背景下，能够响应用户问题的解释对于提升用户对潜在解决方案的理解和增强其对系统的信任至关重要。为实现与该系统的自然交互，我们提出了一种多代理大语言模型（LLM）架构，该架构对解释框架无关，并支持用户和上下文相关的交互式解释。我们还描述了该框架在目标冲突解释中的具体实现，并通过用户研究将LLM驱动的交互与基于模板的基线解释界面进行比较。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to support human-AI collaboration in sequential decision-making, this paper proposes an agentic LLM framework that generates context-aware, user-driven explanations during planning. The method employs a multi-agent architecture where LLMs dynamically respond to user queries, enabling iterative dialogue for goal-conflict resolution. Experimental results from a user study show that the LLM-mediated interface significantly improved user understanding and trust compared to a static template-based explanation system.
为支持人类与AI在规划任务中的协作，本文提出一种基于LLM的代理框架，能生成上下文感知、用户驱动的解释以提升信任与理解。该方法采用多代理架构，使LLM能动态响应用户提问，实现交互式对话而非静态输出。实验对比该交互系统与模板化基线，结果显示LLM驱动的交互显著提升用户对计划冲突的理解，并增强对系统的信任感。
Scaling Laws of SignSGD in Linear Regression: When Does It Outperform SGD?
Authors: Jihwan Kim, Dogyoon Song, Chulhee Yun
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T16:58:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:58:02+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026, 89 pages, 25 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study scaling laws of signSGD under a power-law random features (PLRF) model that accounts for both feature and target decay. We analyze the population risk of a linear model trained with one-pass signSGD on Gaussian-sketched features. We express the risk as a function of model size, training steps, learning rate, and the feature and target decay parameters. Comparing against the SGD risk analyzed by Paquette et al. (2024), we identify a drift-normalization effect and a noise-reshaping effect unique to signSGD. We then obtain compute-optimal scaling laws under the optimal choice of learning rate. Our analysis shows that the noise-reshaping effect can make the compute-optimal slope of signSGD steeper than that of SGD in regimes where noise is dominant. Finally, we observe that the widely used warmup-stable-decay (WSD) schedule further reduces the noise term and sharpens the compute-optimal slope, when feature decay is fast but target decay is slow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：signSGD在线性回归中的缩放规律：何时优于SGD？
我们在幂律随机特征（PLRF）模型下研究signSGD的缩放规律，该模型同时考虑特征和目标衰减。我们分析了在高斯草图特征上使用单遍signSGD训练的线性模型的总体风险，并将其表示为模型规模、训练步数、学习率以及特征和目标衰减参数的函数。与Paquette等（2024）分析的SGD风险相比，我们识别出signSGD特有的漂移归一化效应和噪声重塑效应。随后，我们在最优学习率选择下推导出计算最优的缩放规律。分析表明，噪声重塑效应可在噪声主导的区域使signSGD的计算最优斜率比SGD更陡峭。最后，我们观察到广泛使用的温升-稳定-衰减（WSD）调度策略在特征衰减快而目标衰减慢时，进一步降低噪声项并使计算最优斜率更陡。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by understanding when signSGD outperforms SGD in linear regression, this study derives scaling laws under a power-law random features model that captures feature and target decay. Using one-pass signSGD on Gaussian-sketched features, the authors express population risk as a function of model size, steps, learning rate, and decay parameters, contrasting it with Paquette et al.'s SGD analysis. They identify drift-normalization and noise-reshaping effects unique to signSGD, which can make its compute-optimal slope steeper than SGD’s in high-noise regimes. The warmup-stable-decay schedule further reduces noise and sharpens this slope when feature decay is fast but target decay is slow.
为理解signSGD在何种条件下优于SGD，该研究在考虑特征与目标衰减的幂律随机特征模型下分析了signSGD的缩放规律。在高斯草图特征上使用单遍signSGD，作者将总体风险表示为模型规模、训练步数、学习率及衰减参数的函数。与SGD风险相比，signSGD表现出独特的漂移归一化和噪声重塑效应，可在高噪声环境下实现更陡峭的计算最优缩放。当特征衰减快而目标衰减慢时，采用warmup-stable-decay调度策略可进一步降低噪声项，使计算最优斜率更陡峭。
Accelerating PDE Surrogates via RL-Guided Mesh Optimization
Authors: Yang Meng, Ruoxi Jiang, Zhuokai Zhao, Chong Liu, Rebecca Willett, Yuxin Chen
First: 2026-03-02T16:55:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:55:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AISTATS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep surrogate models for parametric partial differential equations (PDEs) can deliver high-fidelity approximations but remain prohibitively data-hungry: training often requires thousands of fine-grid simulations, each incurring substantial computational cost. To address this challenge, we introduce RLMesh, an end-to-end framework for efficient surrogate training under limited simulation budget. The key idea is to use reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively allocate mesh grid points non-uniformly within each simulation domain, focusing numerical resolution in regions most critical for accurate PDE solutions. A lightweight proxy model further accelerates RL training by providing efficient reward estimates without full surrogate retraining. Experiments on PDE benchmarks demonstrate that RLMesh achieves competitive accuracy to baselines but with substantially fewer simulation queries. These results show that solver-level spatial adaptivity can dramatically improve the efficiency of surrogate training pipelines, enabling practical deployment of learning-based PDE surrogates across a wide range of problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化学习引导的网格优化加速偏微分方程代理模型
参数化偏微分方程（PDE）的深度代理模型虽能提供高保真近似，但训练数据需求巨大：通常需要数千次细网格模拟，每次模拟计算成本高昂。为解决此问题，我们提出RLMesh，一种在有限模拟预算下高效训练代理模型的端到端框架。核心思想是利用强化学习（RL）在每个模拟域内自适应地非均匀分配网格点，将数值分辨率集中在对PDE解准确性最关键区域。轻量级代理模型进一步加速RL训练，通过提供无需完整代理模型重训练的高效奖励估计。在PDE基准实验中，RLMesh在精度上与基线方法相当，但显著减少了模拟查询次数。结果表明，求解器级别的空间自适应性可大幅提高代理模型训练流程的效率，从而在广泛问题中实现学习型PDE代理模型的实用部署。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of training deep surrogate models for parametric PDEs, this work proposes RLMesh, an end-to-end framework that uses reinforcement learning to adaptively optimize mesh resolution, concentrating grid points where solution accuracy is most critical. A lightweight proxy model enables efficient RL training by approximating rewards without full surrogate retraining. Experimental results on PDE benchmarks show that RLMesh achieves comparable accuracy to baseline methods while requiring significantly fewer simulation queries, demonstrating that spatial adaptivity at the solver level can greatly enhance surrogate training efficiency.
为解决训练参数化偏微分方程（PDE）深度代理模型时所需大量精细网格模拟导致的计算成本过高问题，本文提出RLMesh框架：利用强化学习自适应调整网格点分布，将计算资源集中于对解精度最关键区域。通过轻量级代理模型加速强化学习训练，避免完整代理模型重训练。在多个PDE基准实验中，RLMesh在显著减少模拟查询次数的同时，仍能获得与基线相当的精度，表明求解器层面的空间自适应性可大幅提升代理模型训练效率。
German General Social Survey Personas: A Survey-Derived Persona Prompt Collection for Population-Aligned LLM Studies
Authors: Jens Rupprecht, Leon Fröhling, Claudia Wagner, Markus Strohmaier
First: 2025-11-19T19:01:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:52:05+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The use of Large Language Models (LLMs) for simulating human perspectives via persona prompting is gaining traction in computational social science. However, well-curated, empirically grounded persona collections remain scarce, limiting the accuracy and representativeness of such simulations. Here, we introduce the German General Social Survey Personas (GGSS Personas) collection, a comprehensive and representative persona prompt collection built from the German General Social Survey (ALLBUS). The GGSS Personas and their persona prompts are designed to be easily plugged into prompts for all types of LLMs and tasks, steering models to generate responses aligned with the underlying German population. We evaluate GGSS Personas by prompting various LLMs to simulate survey response distributions across diverse topics, demonstrating that GGSS Personas-guided LLMs outperform state-of-the-art classifiers, particularly under data scarcity. Furthermore, we analyze how the representativity and attribute selection within persona prompts affect alignment with population responses. Our findings suggest that GGSS Personas provide a potentially valuable resource for research on LLM-based social simulations that enables more systematic explorations of population-aligned persona prompting in NLP and social science research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：德国一般社会调查人物画像：用于人口对齐LLM研究的调查衍生人物提示集合
利用大型语言模型（LLM）通过人物提示模拟人类视角在计算社会科学中日益流行。然而，高质量、实证基础的人物画像集合仍稀缺，限制了此类模拟的准确性和代表性。本文引入德国一般社会调查人物画像（GGSS Personas）集合，该集合基于德国一般社会调查（ALLBUS）构建，全面且具代表性。GGSS Personas及其提示可轻松嵌入各类LLM和任务的提示中，引导模型生成与德国人口特征对齐的响应。我们通过提示多种LLM模拟跨多样主题的调查响应分布进行评估，证明GGSS Personas引导的LLM在数据稀缺情况下显著优于现有最先进分类器。此外，我们分析了人物提示的代表性及属性选择如何影响与人口响应的对齐程度。研究结果表明，GGSS Personas为基于LLM的社会模拟研究提供了潜在宝贵资源，有助于在自然语言处理与社会科学领域更系统地探索人口对齐的人物提示方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for empirically grounded persona collections to improve the representativeness of LLM simulations of human populations, this study introduces GGSS Personas, a comprehensive persona prompt set derived from the German General Social Survey. The method involves extracting and structuring demographic and attitudinal attributes from survey data to form persona prompts that can be directly integrated into LLM prompts. Experimental results show that LLMs guided by GGSS Personas generate responses that more accurately reflect real survey distributions across diverse topics, especially under data-scarce conditions, and outperform existing classifiers. The study also demonstrates that the representativeness and attribute selection within prompts significantly influence alignment with population-level responses, highlighting GGSS Personas as a valuable tool for population-aligned social simulation research.
为提升大语言模型对人类行为的模拟准确性，本研究基于德国一般社会调查数据构建了GGSS人物画像集合。方法是将调查中的社会人口属性转化为可直接用于大模型提示的结构化人物画像。实验表明，使用该画像引导的大模型在模拟人口分布时，其表现优于现有分类器，尤其在数据稀缺条件下效果更显著。研究还发现，画像的代表性与属性选择直接影响模拟结果与真实人口分布的匹配度，表明该资源对人口对齐的社会模拟研究具有重要价值。
Never Saddle for Reparameterized Steepest Descent as Mirror Flow
Authors: Tom Jacobs, Chao Zhou, Rebekka Burkholz
Venue: The Fourteenth International Conference on Learning Representations (2026)
First: 2026-03-02T16:52:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:52:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
How does the choice of optimization algorithm shape a model's ability to learn features? To address this question for steepest descent methods --including sign descent, which is closely related to Adam --we introduce steepest mirror flows as a unifying theoretical framework. This framework reveals how optimization geometry governs learning dynamics, implicit bias, and sparsity and it provides two explanations for why Adam and AdamW often outperform SGD in fine-tuning. Focusing on diagonal linear networks and deep diagonal linear reparameterizations (a simplified proxy for attention), we show that steeper descent facilitates both saddle-point escape and feature learning. In contrast, gradient descent requires unrealistically large learning rates to escape saddles, an uncommon regime in fine-tuning. Empirically, we confirm that saddle-point escape is a central challenge in fine-tuning. Furthermore, we demonstrate that decoupled weight decay, as in AdamW, stabilizes feature learning by enforcing novel balance equations. Together, these results highlight two mechanisms how steepest descent can aid modern optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：最陡下降法的重参数化鞍点逃逸作为镜像流
优化算法的选择如何影响模型学习特征的能力？为解答这一问题，我们针对最陡下降法（包括与Adam密切相关符号下降法），引入最陡镜像流作为统一的理论框架。该框架揭示了优化几何如何调控学习动态、隐式偏差和稀疏性，并提供了Adam和AdamW在微调中常优于SGD的两种解释。聚焦于对角线线性网络及深度对角线线性重参数化（作为注意力机制的简化代理），我们表明更陡峭的下降有助于鞍点逃逸和特征学习。相比之下，梯度下降需极高的学习率才能逃逸鞍点，这在微调中极为罕见。实证上，我们证实鞍点逃逸是微调中的核心挑战。此外，我们证明了AdamW中的解耦权重衰减通过强制新的平衡方程稳定特征学习。这些结果共同揭示了最陡下降法如何助力现代优化的两种机制。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how optimization algorithms influence feature learning by introducing steepest mirror flows as a theoretical framework that unifies steepest descent methods, including sign descent related to Adam. It demonstrates that steepest descent enhances saddle-point escape and feature learning, whereas gradient descent requires impractically large learning rates to achieve similar escape. Empirical results confirm saddle-point escape as a key challenge in fine-tuning and show that decoupled weight decay in AdamW stabilizes feature learning by enforcing novel balance equations, revealing two mechanisms through which steepest descent improves modern optimization.
本文通过引入最陡镜像流理论框架，统一分析最陡下降法（包括与Adam相关的符号下降法）如何影响模型学习能力，揭示优化几何对学习动态、隐式偏置和稀疏性的作用。研究发现最陡下降法能更高效逃离鞍点并促进特征学习，而梯度下降需极高的学习率才能实现类似效果，这在微调中罕见。实验证实鞍点逃逸是微调的核心挑战，且AdamW的解耦权重衰减通过新平衡方程稳定特征学习，解释了为何Adam和AdamW常优于SGD。
ORGAN: Object-Centric Representation Learning using Cycle Consistent Generative Adversarial Networks
Authors: Joël Küchler, Ellen van Maren, Vaiva Vasiliauskaitė, Katarina Vulić, Reza Abbasi-Asl, Stephan J. Ihle
First: 2026-03-02T16:51:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:51:52+00:00
Comments: GitHub: https://github.com/Hullimulli/ORGAN
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Although data generation is often straightforward, extracting information from data is more difficult. Object-centric representation learning can extract information from images in an unsupervised manner. It does so by segmenting an image into its subcomponents: the objects. Each object is then represented in a low-dimensional latent space that can be used for downstream processing. Object-centric representation learning is dominated by autoencoder architectures (AEs). Here, we present ORGAN, a novel approach for object-centric representation learning, which is based on cycle-consistent Generative Adversarial Networks instead. We show that it performs similarly to other state-of-the-art approaches on synthetic datasets, while at the same time being the only approach tested here capable of handling more challenging real-world datasets with many objects and low visual contrast. Complementing these results, ORGAN creates expressive latent space representations that allow for object manipulation. Finally, we show that ORGAN scales well both with respect to the number of objects and the size of the images, giving it a unique edge over current state-of-the-art approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ORGAN：基于循环一致生成对抗网络的面向对象的表示学习
尽管数据生成通常较为简单，但从数据中提取信息则更具挑战性。面向对象的表示学习能够以无监督方式从图像中提取信息，其方法是将图像分割为子组件——即对象。每个对象随后被表示为低维潜在空间中的向量，可用于下游处理。当前面向对象的表示学习主要依赖自编码器架构（AEs）。本文提出ORGAN，一种基于循环一致生成对抗网络的全新面向对象表示学习方法。我们在合成数据集上表明，ORGAN的表现与其他最先进方法相当，同时它是本文所测试的唯一一种能够处理包含众多对象且视觉对比度较低的真实世界数据集的方法。此外，ORGAN生成的潜在空间表示具有表达能力，支持对象操作。最后，我们证明ORGAN在对象数量和图像尺寸方面均具有良好的可扩展性，使其在当前最先进方法中独具优势。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for unsupervised extraction of object-level information from images, ORGAN introduces a cycle-consistent Generative Adversarial Network framework to learn object-centric representations. Unlike traditional autoencoder-based methods, ORGAN segments images into objects and encodes each into a low-dimensional latent space, enabling downstream tasks and object manipulation. Experimental results show ORGAN matches state-of-the-art performance on synthetic datasets while uniquely handling real-world images with high object density and low contrast. Additionally, ORGAN demonstrates strong scalability with respect to both image size and number of objects, outperforming existing methods in these dimensions.
为了解决从图像中无监督提取物体级信息的难题，ORGAN提出一种基于循环一致生成对抗网络的新框架，将图像分割为物体并编码至低维潜在空间，支持下游任务和物体操作。实验表明，ORGAN在合成数据集上表现与当前最优方法相当，同时是唯一能有效处理高物体密度和低对比度真实图像的方法。此外，ORGAN在图像尺寸和物体数量增加时仍保持良好扩展性，优于现有方法。
